### [1] [CanvasAgent: Enabling Complex Image Creation and Editing via Visual Tool Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05465)
*Hairui Zhu,Yiying Yang,Tengjin Weng,Ziyu Lu,Xiao Yao,Xiaoyang Ye,Lin Ma,Wenhao Jiang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出CanvasCraft数据集和CanvasAgent模型，旨在解决复杂图像创建与编辑中多工具协作的挑战。通过14万条标注的可执行轨迹和1万条强化学习任务规范，训练一个能动态协调异构视觉工具的多轮交互式代理。该方法结合监督微调（SFT）与混合奖励的GRPO优化，在生成过程中实时分析中间结果并调整策略，显著提升复杂图像创作任务中的图像质量与流程合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态工具使用代理主要针对感知、搜索或特定领域编辑任务，缺乏大规模监督用于可执行的图像创建轨迹，难以支持复杂的多工具协作视觉创作需求。

Method: 构建大规模多模态工具使用数据集CanvasCraft，包含14万条可执行轨迹与1万条强化学习任务；设计CanvasAgent，采用监督微调（SFT）预训练，并通过结合结果与过程信号的混合奖励进行GRPO优化，实现对视觉状态演化下的动态工具选择与决策。

Result: 实验表明，CanvasAgent在最终图像质量与生成轨迹行为上均表现优异，验证了其在复杂多工具图像创作工作流中的有效性，同时证明了CanvasCraft数据集对推动该领域发展的价值。

Conclusion: CanvasCraft数据集与CanvasAgent模型共同推动了从感知增强推理向以操作为中心的视觉创作范式的转变，为复杂图像生成与编辑提供了可扩展、可执行的智能解决方案。

Abstract: Complex image creation and editing often require more than a single generation or editing model. A user request may involve synthesizing images, localizing objects, segmenting regions, editing selected content, compositing intermediate assets, reading text, and enhancing the final result. Such tasks shift multimodal agents from perception-augmented reasoning to manipulation-centered visual creation, where tools must actively transform visual states rather than merely inspect them. However, existing multimodal tool-use agents are mostly optimized for perception, search, or domain-specific editing, and lack large-scale supervision for executable image-creation trajectories. In this paper, we introduce CanvasCraft, a large-scale multimodal tool-use dataset for complex image creation and editing, and \textbf{CanvasAgent}, a tool-augmented multimodal agent that learns to orchestrate heterogeneous visual tools through multi-turn interaction. CanvasCraft contains 140K fully annotated executable trajectories and 10K
  RL task specifications. CanvasAgent is first trained with SFT to learn executable reasoning-action trajectories, and is then optimized with GRPO using a hybrid reward that combines outcome- and process-level signals. During rollout, CanvasAgent inspects intermediate results, tracks visual assets, and adapts tool decisions to the evolving visual state. Experiments evaluate both final image quality and trajectory behavior, demonstrating the effectiveness of CanvasAgent and the proposed dataset for complex multi-tool image creation workflows.

</details>


### [2] [A Task-Driven Evaluation of UAV Detection and Tracking under Synthetic Fog](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05467)
*Amir Pouladi,Vesal Ahsani,Haijun Li,Homayoun Najjaran,Afzal Suleman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个任务驱动的评估框架，将深度感知的合成雾生成、图像恢复、目标检测与跟踪集成于统一流程中。针对真实雾天无人机影像采集困难的问题，利用单目深度估计和大气散射模型从清晰图像中合成雾天场景。对比了经典、CNN和Transformer-based等恢复方法，并将其集成到下游感知流程中。在清洁与含雾训练条件下评估检测性能，同时在清洁、含雾和恢复视频序列上评估基于检测的跟踪性能。结果表明，雾严重影响检测与跟踪，主要表现为漏检增多；含雾训练最能提升鲁棒性，而测试时恢复对仅在清洁数据上训练的检测器最有益。研究强调恢复质量并不直接转化为感知性能提升，需联合评估检测与跟踪表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实雾天无人机影像难以获取且标注困难，导致现有方法在雾天环境下检测与跟踪性能下降。为解决这一问题，需要一种能够系统评估图像恢复对下游感知任务影响的框架。

Method: 结合单目深度估计与大气散射模型生成合成雾；对比多种图像恢复方法（经典、CNN、Transformer）；将最优恢复模型集成至检测与跟踪流程；在清洁与含雾数据上训练检测器，评估其在不同条件下的表现；在清洁、含雾及恢复视频上进行跟踪评估。

Result: 雾显著降低检测与跟踪性能，主要因漏检增加；含雾训练提升检测鲁棒性效果最佳；测试时恢复对仅在清洁数据上训练的检测器帮助最大；恢复质量与下游感知性能之间无直接线性关系。

Conclusion: 图像恢复质量不能单独作为评价标准，必须与检测和跟踪性能联合评估；含雾训练和测试时恢复各有优势，应根据训练策略选择合适方案。

Abstract: Fog severely degrades the visibility of small unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) in skydominant, long-range imagery, reducing the reliability of downstream detection and tracking. This paper presents a task-driven evaluation framework that links depth-aware synthetic fog generation, image restoration, object detection, and tracking within a unified pipeline. Given the practical difficulty of collecting and annotating foggy UAV scenes, synthetic fog is generated from real clear-weather outdoor images containing UAV targets using monocular depth estimation and the atmospheric scattering model. Representative restoration methods from classical, convolutional neural network (CNN)-based, and transformer-based families are first compared, after which the selected restoration model is integrated into the downstream perception pipeline. Detection is evaluated under both clean-only and fog-inclusive training regimes using multiple detector variants, while tracking-by-detection is assessed on clean, foggy, and restored video sequences. Beyond image-level restoration metrics, the study evaluates how fog and restoration affect detection robustness and tracking performance. The results show that fog substantially degrades both detection and tracking, primarily through increased missed detections. Fog-inclusive training provides the most consistent improvement in robustness, whereas test-time restoration is most beneficial when the detector has been trained only on clean imagery. These findings show that restoration quality does not necessarily translate into proportional gains in downstream perception and therefore should be evaluated jointly with detection and tracking performance.

</details>


### [3] [Binocular Gaze Estimation with Single Camera and Single Light Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05473)
*Tongbing Huang,Yang Fu,Yunfei Wang,Zhaocan Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种仅使用一个相机和一个光源的注视估计方法，通过几何对称生成虚拟光源和虚拟角膜反射点，利用双瞳距与双反射点距离的关系估计虚拟角膜反射点，并采用多项式回归进行注视估计。验证了一种新的归一化因子，适用于单反射点系统，性能可接受但略低于双实际光源系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在移动设备等场景中，减少硬件组件（尤其是光源）数量更优，但传统注视追踪至少需要一个相机和两个光源以实现自由头部运动下的注视估计。因此，亟需一种简化硬件配置的注视估计方法。

Method: 引入几何对称于相机的虚拟光源，生成图像中的虚拟角膜反射点；通过分析两瞳孔与两反射点之间的距离关系，估计虚拟反射点位置；基于假设存在两个光源的多项式回归模型进行注视估计，并提出适用于单反射点系统的新型归一化因子。

Result: 所提方法在仅使用一个光源的情况下实现了可接受的注视估计性能，但相比双光源系统略有性能下降。

Conclusion: 该方法成功实现了仅用一个相机和一个光源的注视估计，具备实用潜力，尤其适用于资源受限的移动设备场景。

Abstract: According to commonly consented theories, the minimum hardware requirement for gaze tracker is one camera and two light sources to realize gaze estimation with free head movements. However, in some scenarios such as eye tracking on mobile devices, it is preferable to use less components, especially light sources. We propose a gaze estimation method with one camera and one light source. A "virtual light source" is introduced, which is geometrically placed symmetrically to the real light source with respect to the camera, and generates a "virtual glint" in the acquired image. We estimate the "virtual glint" by exploiting the relationship between the distance between two pupils and two glints in the captured image, and estimate the gaze with polynomial regression assuming two light sources are available. A new normalization factor for regression method is verified, which turns out to be practical for one-glint system. The performance is proved to be acceptable, while degradation is noticed compared to system with two actual light sources.

</details>


### [4] [Ground3D-LMM: Fine-Grained 3D Point Grounding and Spatial Reasoning with LMM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05493)
*Amol Harsh,Zongyan Han,Jean Lahoud,Ye Liu,Rao Muhammad Anwer,Hisham Cholakkal,Salman Khan,Fahad Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Ground3D-LMM，一种统一的3D大模型，支持基于点云和可选RGB图像的3D空间对话，具备点定位响应与物体及部件级别的度量输出能力。为评估该模型在3D定位与度量方面的表现，作者构建了一个大规模数据集（约250万问答对），涵盖8个任务，并引入3D有根测量任务。实验表明，Ground3D-LMM在多个数据集和任务上表现出色，成为3D有根、度量感知对话理解的强基线。相关数据集与模型已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D大模型在对话中缺乏显式3D定位，而3D定位模型又不支持交互式、度量感知的对话，因此亟需一个能同时实现精确3D定位与真实单位度量输出的统一模型。

Method: 提出Ground3D-LMM模型，结合点云与可选RGB图像输入，支持点接地的对话响应和物体/部件级别的度量数值输出；设计并构建了包含密集标注的3D Grounded Measurement数据集，用于评估模型性能。

Result: 在多数据集和任务上的实验表明，Ground3D-LMM在3D定位与度量任务上达到领先性能，验证了其作为基准的有效性。

Conclusion: Ground3D-LMM成功实现了3D空间对话中的显式定位与度量输出，为未来研究提供了强有力的基线，数据集与模型已开源，推动3D交互理解的发展。

Abstract: Natural-language queries about 3D environments become actionable when responses are verifiable and metric. Verifiability requires explicit grounding to the referred 3D region, while metric answers report physical measurements in real-world units (e.g., size, thickness, clearance, and distance). Existing 3D large multimodal models (LMMs) approaches remain limited: conversational systems typically respond without explicit 3D grounding, while 3D grounding models are not designed for interactive, metric-aware dialogue. In this paper, we present Ground3D-LMM, a unified model that takes a point cloud and an optional RGB image as input and supports 3D spatial conversation with (i) point-grounded responses and (ii) metric numeric outputs at both object and part granularity, including multi-object queries. To evaluate this intersection of grounding and measurement, we define the 3D Grounded Measurement task, which requires predicting the referred 3D region and the corresponding metric quantities in real-world units. We introduce a large-scale dataset built on ScanNet and ScanNet++ datasets with dense object and part annotations and roughly 2.5M question-answer pairs spanning eight tasks, along with a manually verified test set. Extensive experiments on multiple datasets and tasks show that our proposed Ground3D-LMM model provides a strong baseline for grounded, metric-aware 3D conversational understanding. Our dataset and model are publicly available.

</details>


### [5] [Light-Omni: Reflex over Reasoning in Agentic Video Understanding with Long-Term Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05511)
*Chang Nie,Jiaju Wei,Junlan Feng,Chaoyou Fu,Caifeng Shan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Light-Omni 是一种轻量级、反射式的多模态视频理解框架，通过双上下文状态设计，在单次前向传播中快速构建全局上下文和参数化潜在状态，实现语义对齐的检索与即时响应，避免了传统方法中耗时的迭代推理。该框架在多个视频基准上表现优异，相比 M3-Agent 提升 2.4% 准确率，速度提升 12.1 倍，GPU 内存效率提高 2.6 倍，并可增强现有多模态大模型的性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频智能体依赖高成本的迭代推理来弥补全局上下文缺失和语义错位问题，导致延迟高、资源消耗大。因此需要一种更高效、低延迟的机制来实现长时程视频理解。

Method: 提出 Light-Omni 框架，包含两个核心组件：1）全局状态（有限大小的多模态脚本，持续从情景记忆中融合，保留近期细节并总结历史事件）；2）基于全局状态生成的参数化潜在状态，直接驱动动作并生成检索嵌入，实现快速响应。二者协同工作，实现无迭代推理的轻量化处理。

Result: 在多个视频理解基准测试中，Light-Omni 显著优于 M3-Agent，平均准确率提升 2.4%，推理速度提升 12.1 倍，GPU 内存使用减少 2.6 倍。同时，其作为记忆系统能有效提升现有多模态大模型的性能与效率。

Conclusion: Light-Omni 通过双上下文状态设计，实现了高效、低延迟、语义对齐的视频理解，为构建轻量级视频智能体提供了新范式，具有良好的通用性和扩展性。

Abstract: Agentic video understanding equips models with long-term memory to autonomously process and respond to continuous, long-horizon multimodal streams. However, advanced video agents often rely on ``detective-style'' iterative reasoning for action control (e.g., $\mathtt{search}$) and evidence aggregation, incurring prohibitive costs and latency. We argue that such heavy reasoning primarily compensates for the lack of global context and semantic misalignment in retrieval. This paper introduces Light-Omni, a multimodal agent framework for reflexive and lightweight video understanding. It achieves this through dual contextual states that instantly build the required context in a single forward pass. First, we maintain a global state, a finite-sized multimodal script continuously consolidated from episodic memory, serving as the global context for Light-Omni. Through hierarchical merging, it preserves recent details while summarizing past events. Second, conditioned on this global context, we generate a parametric latent state that directly drives autonomous actions and produces retrieval embeddings, with minimal latency. Benefiting from this coupled design, Light-Omni achieves semantically aligned retrieval and reflexive responses while avoiding iterative reasoning. Extensive experiments validate the effectiveness of Light-Omni across multiple video benchmarks. Notably, it outperforms M3-Agent with an average 2.4% accuracy gain, a 12.1$\times$ speedup, and a 2.6$\times$ improvement in GPU memory efficiency. Furthermore, it serves as a memory system to enhance both the performance and efficiency of existing MLLMs. Project page: https://clare-nie.github.io/Light-Omni.

</details>


### [6] [Statistical Adversaries: Natural Backdoor-like Features in Vision Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05516)
*Paul K. Mandal,Pavan Reddy,Tristan Malatynski*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了视觉数据中自然存在的统计信号，这些信号虽非恶意插入，但表现得像后门触发器，被称为统计对抗性攻击。通过分析ImageNet，发现与特定标签强相关的模式，并利用统计控制消除随机相关性，证明这些信号能直接且可预测地改变模型预测。此类信号比通用噪声更具针对性，且在不同模型架构间具有迁移性，表明部分漏洞源于数据集结构而非单一模型特性。结论指出，普通数据集中可能存在可被利用的对抗性表面，即使没有数据中毒，因此建议对数据集进行审计时将虚假结构视为潜在攻击面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究视觉数据中非恶意但可能引发模型误判的自然统计信号，揭示数据集结构本身可能构成对抗性攻击面。

Method: 分析ImageNet数据集，识别与特定标签强相关的统计模式；使用统计控制方法去除随机相关性；验证这些信号对模型预测的影响。

Result: 发现的统计信号能直接、可预测地改变模型预测，具有针对性和跨模型迁移能力，表明数据集结构是潜在攻击面。

Conclusion: 普通数据集可能包含无需数据中毒即可被利用的对抗性表面，应将虚假结构视为模型安全审计中的潜在攻击面。

Abstract: Model-specific adversarial attacks have been extensively studied. We study a different failure mode: naturally occurring statistical signals in vision data that can behave like backdoor-like triggers without being maliciously inserted. We call these signals statistical adversaries. We analyse Imagenet to find patterns that are strongly linked to certain labels. We then use statistical controls to remove random correlations from our candidate signals. Finally, we demonstrate that these signals directly and predictably alter model predictions. These statistical adversaries are more targeted than generic corruptions and transfer across different model architectures. This suggests that some vulnerabilities are driven by dataset structure and distribution rather than a single model's idiosyncrasies. We conclude that ordinary datasets can contain exploitable adversarial surfaces even in the absence of poisoning, and suggest that dataset audits should treat spurious structure not only as a source of bias or interpretability failure, but also as a latent attack surface for vision models.

</details>


### [7] [Rendering-Aware Bayesian 3D Gaussian Splatting with Native Uncertainty and Adaptive Complexity Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05522)
*Gaoxiang Jia,Vikram Appia,Junzhou Huang,Xinlei Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种渲染感知的贝叶斯3D高斯溅射框架，通过使用正态-逆威沙特后验分布来追踪高斯几何的均值和协方差，利用渲染导出的代理摘要实现不确定性建模。引入可选的狄利克雷过程扩展以提供概率成分使用信号，并明确区分闭式与近似推断边界。通过重渲染后验几何样本，实现原生预测不确定性，支持区间校准和主动视图选择。在固定预算的16至32个视图任务中，该方法在PSNR上提升0.453 dB，LPIPS降低0.0146，优于标准集成基线、PPU风格及NIW代理方法；同时，其95%覆盖率误差降低约17倍，接近名义覆盖率，训练成本仅为深度集成的三分之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准3D高斯溅射训练依赖点估计和手工调参，缺乏原生不确定性与合理复杂度控制，在稀疏视图或固定采集预算下难以有效识别弱支持几何并选择信息丰富的视图。需要一种能提供不确定性量化与主动学习能力的更优表示方法。

Method: 采用正态-逆威沙特（NIW）后验分布对高斯几何的均值和协方差进行建模，基于渲染生成的代理总结信息进行推断；引入狄利克雷过程扩展以实现成分使用的概率信号；设计训练流程以明确闭式与近似推断之间的界限；通过重渲染后验样本获得预测不确定性，用于主动视图选择与校准。

Result: 在16–32视图的固定预算任务中，新方法在PSNR上比标准集成基线提升0.453 dB，LPIPS降低0.0146，胜出29/39场景种子对和10/13场景均值；优于PPU风格（+0.355 dB）和NIW代理（+0.401 dB）。NIW原生置信区间将95%覆盖率误差降低约17倍（0.046 vs. 0.796），比3成员深度集成更接近名义覆盖率（0.047 vs. 0.454），且训练成本仅为三分之一。与标准3DGS对比，性能微升0.030 dB，仅增加1.6%训练时间。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯3DGS为决策导向任务（如主动视图选择）提供了实用的概率场景表示，兼具不确定性量化、高效推理与可控复杂度，显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian splatting (3DGS) is a strong representation for real-time novel-view synthesis, but its standard training pipeline relies on point estimates and hand-tuned heuristics, providing no native uncertainty or principled complexity control. This is most limiting under sparse views or fixed acquisition budgets, where a model must identify weakly supported geometry and select informative views. We introduce a rendering-aware Bayesian 3DGS framework that tracks Gaussian geometry with a Normal-Inverse-Wishart posterior over means and covariances using renderer-derived surrogate summaries. An optional Dirichlet-process extension adds a probabilistic component-usage signal, and the training schedule makes the closed-form versus approximate inference boundary explicit. Re-rendering posterior geometry samples yields native predictive uncertainty for interval calibration and active view selection. In a fixed-budget 16-to-32 active-view task, native NIW acquisition improves PSNR by +0.453 dB and LPIPS by -0.0146 over a scoring-only 3-member standard-ensemble baseline, winning 29/39 scene-seed pairs and 10/13 scene means; it also improves over PPU-style (+0.355 dB) and NIW-proxy (+0.401 dB) acquisition. NIW native intervals reduce 95% coverage error by about 17x relative to a shared proxy (0.046 vs. 0.796) and are about 10x closer to nominal coverage than a 3-member deep ensemble (0.047 vs. 0.454) at roughly one-third the training cost. As a reconstruction compatibility check, paired NIW-vs-standard analysis over 39 scene-seed runs yields +0.030 dB PSNR with 1.6% additional training time. These results position Bayesian 3DGS as a practical probabilistic scene representation for decision-facing tasks such as active view selection.

</details>


### [8] [Multi-Teacher Contrastive Distillation for Edge-Efficient Pathology Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05533)
*Tim Lenz,Maurice Heide,Marco Gustav,Nic G. Reitsam,Jakob Nikolas Kather*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MuCoDi是一种用于病理学图像分析的预训练框架，通过对比蒸馏将多个大型基础模型（PFMs）的冻结特征压缩为轻量级边缘设备适配的编码器。该方法在仅11.8K张全切片图像上使用1430万张切片进行训练，使小型RepViT和MobileOne模型达到接近教师模型的性能，同时显著减小模型规模与计算开销。例如，MuCoEdge-R1.0仅需640万参数和1.12 GFLOPs，AUROC达70.9%，在Raspberry Pi 5上实现605倍加速，证明了高质量病理表示可高效部署于边缘设备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算病理学基础模型虽性能优异，但体积庞大、推理成本高，难以在临床病理部门本地部署。亟需一种能保留高性能的同时大幅降低模型复杂度与计算需求的方法，以支持边缘设备上的实用化应用。

Method: 提出MuCoDi框架，采用基于MoCo v3的对比蒸馏策略，利用Virchow2、UNI2和H-Optimus-1等教师模型的冻结切片嵌入作为缓存键，训练轻量级学生模型（MobileOne和RepViT），通过非回归式特征对齐实现高效知识迁移。

Result: RepViT-based MuCoEdge模型在23个临床任务中表现优异，其中MuCoEdge-R2.3和MuCoEdge-R1.5的外部AUROC分别达到71.0%（仅比最佳教师低0.8个百分点），且在F1和AUPRC上表现领先；MuCoEdge-R1.0仅6.4M参数、1.12 GFLOPs，AUROC达70.9%；在Raspberry Pi 5上，微型MobileOne模型实现高达605倍的单图推理速度提升，同时保持66.5%-66.9%的外部AUROC。

Conclusion: MuCoDi成功实现了从大型病理基础模型到紧凑、高效边缘编码器的高性能知识迁移，使得具备临床实用价值的病理图像分析系统可在资源受限的边缘设备上部署，推动计算病理技术向真实世界落地迈进。

Abstract: Computational pathology foundation models (PFMs) have advanced whole-slide image analysis. However, their size and inference cost hinder local deployment in pathology departments. We propose MuCoDi, a pretraining framework that distills frozen tile embeddings from multiple PFMs into compact edge-oriented encoders. Instead of regressing individual teacher features, MuCoDi trains lightweight MobileOne and RepViT students with a contrastive distillation objective adapted from MoCo v3, where cached Virchow2, UNI2, and H-Optimus-1 embeddings replace momentum-encoder keys. We pretrain students on 14.3M TCGA tiles from only 11.8K WSIs and evaluate frozen encoders on 23 clinically curated downstream classification tasks. RepViT-based MuCoEdge students retain near-teacher performance while reducing model size by orders of magnitude: MuCoEdge-R2.3 and MuCoEdge-R1.5 reach 71.0% external AUROC, within 0.8 percentage points of the best teacher (Virchow2, 71.8%), while MuCoEdge-R2.3 obtains the best external F1 and the second-best AUPRC (51.8% and 53.3%). MuCoEdge-R1.0 reaches 70.9% AUROC with only 6.4M parameters and 1.12 GFLOPs. On a Raspberry Pi 5, sub-million-parameter MobileOne students achieve up to 605-fold single-tile speedup over Virchow2 while retaining 66.5% to 66.9% external AUROC, demonstrating that PFM-quality pathology representations can be moved toward practical edge deployment. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/mucodi-6243.

</details>


### [9] [Harnessing Generative Image Models for Training-Free Primitive Shape Abstraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05568)
*Gregor Kobsik,Tim Elsner,Leif Kobbelt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需训练的3D形状表示方法，通过多视图渲染、视觉语言模型分析语义部分、生成图像模型绘制颜色编码的分割掩码，并将其重新投影到几何体上，最后用超椭球体拟合每个部分。整个流程无任何可学习参数，具备类别无关和方向不变性，且性能随生成模型提升而提高。在HumanPrim和Toys4K数据集上，平均每个物体使用5-9个基元，取得了最低的Chamfer距离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的方法在处理3D形状表示时面临类别依赖和方向敏感的问题，且通常需要微调。本文旨在探索是否可以不经过任何训练直接利用大规模预训练视觉模型的能力，实现通用、鲁棒的3D形状分解与表示。

Method: 首先对3D对象进行多视图渲染；然后使用视觉语言模型识别其语义部分；接着通过提示生成式图像模型生成颜色编码的分割掩码；将该掩码重投影至原始几何结构；最后对每个部分使用超椭球体进行参数优化拟合。整个过程无任何可学习参数。

Result: 在HumanPrim和Toys4K数据集上，该方法在所有对比方法中实现了最低的Chamfer距离，平均每个物体使用5-9个基元。实验表明当前精度瓶颈在于部分分割而非基元拟合，未来生成模型的改进将直接提升本方法的表现。

Conclusion: 本文提出的训练自由框架成功实现了无需训练的3D形状紧凑表示，具备类别无关与方向不变特性，且性能可随生成模型发展而持续提升，为通用3D理解提供了新思路。

Abstract: Representing 3D shapes as compact sets of geometric primitives is fundamental to robotics, simulation, and scene understanding. Generative image models trained at scale have recently emerged as generalist visual learners that can identify and segment object parts directly in the image domain, across arbitrary categories and without task-specific training. Adapting such models to downstream tasks typically requires fine-tuning; we ask whether their pretrained capability can instead be harnessed directly, without any training, and answer affirmatively with a training-free harness. Our pipeline renders multi-view images of a 3D object, uses a vision-language model to analyze its semantic parts, prompts a generative image model to paint a color-coded part segmentation mask, reprojects it onto the geometry, and fits a superquadric primitive to each part via parameter optimization. The approach contains no learned parameters: it is category-agnostic and orientation-invariant, properties that previous learning-based models struggled with. Its accuracy ceiling rises with future generative-model improvements, which we confirm with a ground-truth segmentation study showing that part segmentation, not primitive fitting, is the current accuracy bottleneck. On HumanPrim and Toys4K, our method achieves the lowest Chamfer distance among all evaluated methods, using 5--9 primitives per object on average.

</details>


### [10] [Hierarchical Classification via Cascading Feature Elimination: Application to Human Phenotype Ontology-Aligned Facial Phenotyping (FaceMesh2HPO)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05585)

TL;DR: FaceMesh2HPO 是一个基于3D面部网格和人类表型本体（HPO）的框架，用于分类面部表型描述符以支持临床诊断。该框架利用124名临床医生对10种疾病（107个HPO术语）及非综合征对照的数据，从2D图像生成包含478个关键点的3D面部网格，并采用分层PointNet架构进行级联分类与特征剔除。最佳模型结合3D网格、面部轮廓和人口统计学信息，在父节点上表现优于叶节点，AUROC在~0.55至~0.89之间。外部验证显示不同疾病间泛化能力不一。研究证明了基于3D面部几何的层次建模可实现可解释且与本体关联的表型分类，但对罕见叶节点的性能仍有限。未来需提升数据多样性和特征选择策略以增强鲁棒性与临床实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建基于3D面部网格（478个关键点）的分层PointNet模型，融合2D图像生成的3D结构、面部轮廓和人口统计学特征；采用级联分类与特征消除策略，实现从父节点到叶节点的层次化表型预测。

Result: 模型在不同疾病中取得约0.55至0.89的AUROC，父节点分类性能显著高于叶节点；外部验证显示模型在不同疾病间泛化能力差异较大，尤其在罕见表型上表现不足。

Conclusion: 基于3D面部几何的层次建模可实现与HPO对齐的可解释表型分类，具备临床应用潜力，但受限于数据多样性与特征选择策略，对稀有表型的识别仍需改进。建议通过扩充数据集与优化特征工程提升模型鲁棒性与实用性。

Abstract: FaceMesh2HPO is a framework for classifying facial phenotypic descriptors aligned with the Human Phenotype Ontology (HPO) to support clinical diagnosis. Using annotations from 124 clinicians across 10 disorders (107 HPO terms) combined with non-syndromic controls, we generated 3D facial meshes (478 landmarks) from 2D images and trained a hierarchical PointNet-based pipeline with cascading classification and feature elimination. The best models, incorporating 3D meshes, facial outline, and demographic metadata, achieved AUROCs between ~0.55 and ~0.89, with higher performance at parent nodes than leaf terms. External validation showed variable generalizability across disorders. Results demonstrate that hierarchical modeling of 3D facial geometry enables interpretable, ontology-linked phenotype classification, though performance on rare leaf terms remains limited. Improved data diversity and feature selection strategies are needed to enhance robustness and clinical utility.

### [11] [Patch Knowledge Transfer for Efficient AI-Generated Image Quality Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05605)
*Jiquan Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于知识蒸馏的优化框架Patch Knowledge Transfer (PKT)，旨在解决AI生成图像感知质量评估中效率与准确率难以兼顾的问题。通过设计一个教师-学生双模型架构，利用多层级知识迁移机制，使学生模型在仅依赖全局处理的情况下，高效继承教师模型的表征能力，实现性能与计算成本的协同优化。实验表明，该方法在4个AIGIQA数据集上将计算成本降低67.7%，同时保持与教师模型相当的评估性能，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI生成图像质量评估面临两大挑战：复杂特征提取方法虽提升性能但计算开销大，难以实时推理；而简单的图像缩放方法虽高效但准确性差。因此亟需一种既能保证高精度又能实现高效推理的新方法。

Method: 提出Patch Knowledge Transfer (PKT)框架，采用双模型架构：教师模型结合局部与全局处理以提供高质量监督信号，学生模型仅使用全局处理，并通过多层级知识迁移机制从教师模型中学习表征能力，从而实现高效且精准的质量评估。

Result: 在4个AIGIQA数据集上的实验显示，学生模型性能接近教师模型，同时计算成本降低67.7%；相比现有方法，在模型效率与评估准确率之间取得了更优平衡。

Conclusion: PKT框架通过创新的多层级知识迁移机制，成功实现了视觉表征能力与推理效率的协同优化，为大规模AI生成图像的质量评估提供了高效、准确的解决方案。

Abstract: With the rapid advancement of image generation technologies, perceptual quality assessment of AI-generated images has emerged as a crucial research direction in computer vision. The core challenge of this task lies in achieving efficient quality assessment for massive generated images. Current mainstream approaches exhibit two key limitations: 1) Methods employing complex feature extraction strategies, while improving performance, incur prohibitive computational costs that hinder real-time inference; 2) Simple image scaling-based solutions, despite their computational efficiency, demonstrate significantly inferior assessment accuracy. To address this critical issue, we propose Patch Knowledge Transfer (PKT), a knowledge distillation-based optimization framework that achieves synergistic optimization of visual representation capability and inference efficiency through an innovative multi-level knowledge transfer mechanism. Specifically, we design a dual-model architecture: a teacher model with local-global hybrid processing provides high-quality supervision signals, while a student model relying solely on global processing efficiently inherits the teacher's representation capacity through multi-level supervision. Extensive experiments conducted on 4 AIGIQA databases demonstrate that the PKT framework enables the student model to maintain performance comparable to the teacher while reducing computational costs by 67.7\%. Furthermore, compared to existing methods, our approach achieves a superior balance between model efficiency and assessment accuracy.

### [12] [Cross-Contextual Vision-Language Adaptation with LoRA for Personalized Severe Adverse Event Detection in Clinical Wound Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05625)
*Aditi Naiknaware,Jian Sun,Aminreza Khandan,Shengyang Huang,Sean Dow,Bijan Najafi,Salimeh Sekeh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多模态框架，用于自动化伤口监测与严重不良事件（SAE）检测。该方法结合临床笔记与伤口描述，利用基于冻结的BiomedCLIP骨干网络的双流低秩适配（LoRA）框架，通过跨上下文LoRA融合机制实现临床语义与视觉特征的信息交互，生成上下文感知的多模态表示。为识别个性化SAE，设计了一种针对伤口的分布外（OOD）检测框架，综合语义匹配、视觉典型性、图文对齐等指标计算统一的SAE得分。同时引入协变量一致性和时间漂移惩罚以捕捉愈合动态。在纵向伤口数据集上的实验表明，该系统在伤口愈合评估和SAE检测方面表现优异，展示了语义丰富且时序敏感的视觉-语言系统在临床伤口监测中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前伤口监测面临及时识别感染、组织恶化和愈合延迟等严重不良事件的挑战，而现有视觉-语言模型缺乏领域特定的语义接地能力，难以整合图像与异构临床信息，且对训练分布外的情况检测能力有限。因此亟需一种能融合多源信息、具备个性化风险预警能力的智能监测系统。

Method: 采用双流低秩适配（LoRA）框架，基于冻结的BiomedCLIP模型编码临床文本与伤口视觉描述；引入跨上下文LoRA融合机制促进语义与视觉信息交互；构建联合评分机制进行分布外（OOD）检测，结合语义匹配、视觉典型性、图文一致性；引入时间一致性与漂移惩罚以建模愈合过程动态变化。

Result: 在真实临床纵向伤口数据集上，所提方法在伤口愈合评估和严重不良事件（SAE）检测任务中均表现出色，显著优于基线模型，验证了其在早期风险识别与个性化监测方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了语义丰富、时序感知的多模态视觉-语言系统在临床伤口监测中的巨大潜力，尤其适用于复杂、动态变化的医疗场景，为未来智能辅助诊断系统的发展提供了新思路。

Abstract: Wound monitoring is a critical yet underserved clinical challenge, where timely identification of severe adverse events (SAEs) such as infection, tissue deterioration, and delayed healing can significantly impact patient outcomes. While vision-language models (VLMs) show strong multimodal reasoning, they often lack domain-specific grounding to integrate wound imagery with heterogeneous clinical information, and provide limited mechanisms for detecting cases that diverge from the training distribution. We present a multimodal framework for automated wound monitoring and SAE detection. Our approach leverages paired clinical notes and wound descriptions capturing visual characteristics such as appearance, surrounding skin condition, color changes, and signs of inflammation or healing progression, encoded through a dual-stream Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) framework built on a frozen BiomedCLIP backbone. We introduce a cross-contextual LoRA fusion mechanism enabling information exchange between clinical semantics and visual wound descriptors, producing context-aware multimodal representations without full model fine-tuning. To identify personalized SAEs, we propose a wound-specific out-of-distribution (OOD) detection framework combining semantic matching, visual typicality, caption-text alignment, and caption-visual alignment into a unified SAE (OOD) score. To capture healing dynamics, we incorporate covariate consistency and temporal drift penalties that leverage changes in wound characteristics across visits. Experiments on a longitudinal wound dataset collected through clinical visits show promising performance on both wound healing assessment and SAE detection, highlighting the potential of semantically enriched, temporally aware vision-language systems for clinical wound monitoring and early risk identification.

### [13] [Taxlifier: Leveraging Disease Taxonomy for Enhanced Multi-Label Classification in Chest Radiography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05628)

Method: 提出两种层次化多标签分类技术：损失基方法将层次信息直接融入优化过程；logit基方法根据疾病分类体系中的父类调整各分类的预测概率。

Result: 在三个大规模数据集上，两种方法均显著优于基线，准确率提升11%-12%，AUC提升10%-13%，F1分数提升12%-24%。统计分析证实其鲁棒性和可靠性。

Abstract: Accurate and efficient classification of thoracic diseases in chest X-ray (CXR) images is crucial for timely diagnosis and treatment. However, the presence of multiple pathologies with overlapping visual characteristics poses significant challenges for automated classification systems. In this study, we propose two novel hierarchical multi-label classification techniques, namely the loss-based and logit-based methods, to address these challenges by leveraging the hierarchical relationships among different thoracic pathologies. The loss-based technique integrates hierarchical information directly into the optimization process, while the logit-based method adjusts the predicted probabilities of each class based on its parent class in the disease taxonomy. We evaluate the performance of both techniques using three large-scale CXR datasets: CheXpert (224,316 CXRs), PADCHEST (160,000 CXRs), and NIH (112,120 CXRs). The experimental results demonstrate significant improvements in accuracy, AUC, and F1 scores compared to the baseline method across various pathologies. The logit-based and loss-based methods improve accuracy by 12\% and 11\%, AUC by 13\% and 10\%, and F1 scores by 24\% and 12\%, respectively compared to the baseline. These results represent a substantial improvement over the baseline method. Furthermore, we conduct a comprehensive statistical analysis to validate the robustness and reliability of the proposed techniques. The integration of domain-specific hierarchical knowledge not only enhances the classification performance but also provides a more interpretable output for clinical decision support. Our findings highlight the potential of hierarchical multi-label classification in advancing computer-aided diagnosis systems for chest radiography.

### [14] [Recovering Cloud Microstructures with Cascaded Diffusion Inversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05637)
*Hanan Gani,Guy Pulik,Daniel Rosenfeld,Duncan Watson-Parris,Salman Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于扩散的两阶段超分辨率框架，用于提升多光谱云微结构图像的分辨率（4倍），在重建精度和视觉质量上优于现有Transformer和扩散模型基线。该方法能更好捕捉对云播种决策至关重要的细小云特征（如对流塔和云隙）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前地球静止和极轨卫星的空间分辨率不足以捕捉小尺度云特征，而现有超分辨率方法难以泛化到卫星捕获的云覆盖光谱图像。因此需要一种专门针对云微结构的高分辨率增强方法。

Method: 采用两阶段扩散超分辨率框架：第一阶段利用真实世界配对数据学习退化处理与跨传感器对齐；第二阶段通过自监督内部降级高分辨率数据来优化结构学习与纹理合成。

Result: 所提方法在重建准确性和视觉质量方面均优于现有最先进的模型，尤其在捕捉细小云微结构（如对流塔、云隙）方面表现更优。消融实验表明，第一阶段擅长粗略结构保真度，第二阶段增强细节和真实感。

Conclusion: 该方法为改进云微物理分析提供了实用路径，并推动了人工智能在气候与可持续性领域的应用。代码和模型已公开。

Abstract: High-resolution satellite imagery is critical for observing fine-scale cloud structures that inform weather modification strategies like cloud seeding for rain-enhancement. However, the spatial resolution of current geostationary and polar-orbiting satellites is often insufficient for capturing small cloud features. Current super-resolution methodologies are suited for natural images and, therefore, struggle to generalize to satellite-captured spectral images of cloud cover. To address this, we propose a two-stage diffusion-based super-resolution framework to enhance the resolution of multi-spectral cloud microstructures by a factor of $4\times$. Specifically, we use inverse diffusion to recover the high resolution properties from low resolution. Stage 1 utilizes real-world paired data to learn robust degradation handling and inter-sensor alignment, while Stage 2 employs a self-supervised internal downgrading of high resolution data to refine structural learning and texture synthesis. Our approach outperforms the state-of-the-art transformer and diffusion-based baselines in both reconstruction accuracy and visual quality. We demonstrate that the two-stage method better captures fine cloud microstructures (e.g. convective turrets and cloud gaps) that are crucial for effective cloud seeding decisions. Ablation studies confirm the complementary benefits of the two stages: Stage 1 excels in coarse structural fidelity, while Stage 2 contributes enhanced detail and realism. These results highlight a practical path toward improving cloud microphysics analysis and as a step towards utilizing AI for climate and sustainability. Our code and models are publicly available at: https://github.com/hananshafi/superresolution-cloud-microphysics.

### [15] [VEIL: How Visual Encoding Hijacking Induces Bias In Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05641)
*Suranjana Sooraj,Xuyang Chen,Madhumitha Venkatesan,Dongyu Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VEIL 系统性研究了图表编码对时序数据分类中模型学习表示的影响，发现可视化设计显著影响模型对时间模式的捕捉能力，强调图表设计应被视为表示与测量问题而非单纯建模选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前时序数据通过图表图像输入CNN进行分类已普遍，但尚不清楚模型是学习真实时间模式还是依赖图表设计带来的视觉线索，亟需系统评估图表编码对模型学习的影响。

Method: 采用相似性分析、可迁移性分析和注意力归因分析等多维度方法，考察不同图表编码下模型表示的学习情况，并结合注意力引导训练验证其有效性。

Result: 注意力引导训练在编码敏感性一致时能缓解视觉线索依赖，但在缺乏此类信号时效果有限甚至产生负面影响；研究表明可视化设计深刻影响模型表示，应将图表基时序分类视为表示与测量问题。

Conclusion: 图表设计选择显著塑造模型所学表示，建议在图表基时序分类中重视可视化设计作为核心要素，而非仅关注模型架构。

Abstract: Rendering time series as chart images for CNN-based classification has become increasingly common in time-series classification (TSC). However, it remains unclear whether models learn underlying temporal patterns or rely on encoding-specific visual cues introduced by chart design. We present VEIL: a systematic study examining how chart encodings influence learned representations through complementary analyses of similarity, transferability, and attribution. Attention-guided training appears to mitigate this effect when encoding sensitivity is consistently identified across diagnostics, but provides limited or negative benefit when such signals are absent. These findings position VEIL within the broader question of how machines perceive visualizations -- extending graphical perception from human readers to vision models -- and show that visualization design choices shape learned representations in ways that warrant treating chart-based TSC as a representation and measurement problem rather than a simple modeling decision.

</details>


### [16] [REVIVE: A Multi-Modal Framework for Vandalism Detection and Recovery in Autonomous Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05649)
*Abdullah Tariq Choudhry,Tapadhir Das*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出REVIVE框架，用于恢复自动驾驶车辆中因恶意遮挡（VOA）导致的图像损坏。该框架整合了四步流程：二值化VOA检测、多类遮挡模式识别、基于EfficientNet的U-Net分割，以及基于BLIP引导的Stable Diffusion、直接像素替换或自适应中值滤波的类型感知恢复。实验表明，直接像素替换在对齐参考条件下可实现接近完美的重建效果（召回率从0.588提升至0.967），而Stable Diffusion表现不一但可作为异步恢复分支。引入参考可用性质量门控机制后，平均召回率回升至0.608，确保输出流始终不低于原始未修复帧的表现，显著提升了感知系统的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动驾驶系统面临恶意遮挡攻击（VOA）威胁，现有方法仅能检测被篡改图像，缺乏对物理遮挡后图像恢复的有效手段，导致下游感知任务性能下降。因此亟需一种高效、可靠的图像恢复框架以保障摄像头感知的连续性和准确性。

Method: REVIVE框架包含四个核心模块：(1) 二值化检测判断是否存在遮挡；(2) 多分类识别具体遮挡模式；(3) 使用EfficientNet-U-Net进行精细遮挡区域分割；(4) 根据遮挡类型选择不同恢复策略——包括BLIP引导的Stable Diffusion生成式修复、直接像素替换或自适应中值滤波。此外，设计了一个参考可用性质量门控机制，仅允许高质量修复结果进入下游处理链路。

Result: 在500组真实追踪图像对上评估，未经恢复的VOA使YOLOv8l检测召回率降至0.588；采用直接像素替换后，召回率恢复至0.967，F1-score达0.970。其他基线方法如LaMa、Telea和Navier-Stokes虽改善图像相似性，但对检测性能提升有限。引入质量门控后，即使在非理想条件下，平均召回率仍保持在0.608，优于无门控时的0.304，且不会劣化于原始未修复帧。

Conclusion: REVIVE提供了一套结构化、可扩展的恶意遮挡恢复框架，有效应对自动驾驶场景下的视觉感知退化问题。通过智能路由与质量控制机制，确保恢复输出始终具备可用性，显著增强系统鲁棒性与实用性。

Abstract: Autonomous vehicles (AVs) face increasing threats from vandalism-induced occlusion attacks (VOAs) that compromise camera-based perception. While detection frameworks can identify vandalized images, restoring camera-stream utility after physical occlusion remains underexplored. This paper presents present the Recovery and Enhancement of Vandalized Images for Vision Excellence (REVIVE) framework, a vandalism recovery pipeline integrating: (1) binary VOA detection, (2) multi-class VOA pattern identification, (3) EfficientNet-based U-Net segmentation, and (4) type-aware recovery using Bootstrapping Language-Image Pre-training (BLIP)-guided Stable Diffusion inpainting, direct pixel replacement, or adaptive median filtering. Stable Diffusion shows variable reconstruction performance (per-pattern SSIM 0.667-0.867, PSNR 15.4-26.7dB) across VOA patterns, while aligned direct pixel replacement achieves near-identical reconstruction under the aligned-reference condition. On 500 tracked clean/vandalized image pairs, unrecovered VOAs reduce YOLOv8l object-detection recall to 0.588, while direct pixel replacement restores recall to 0.967 and F1-score to 0.970 under that aligned-reference condition. LaMa, Telea, and Navier-Stokes baselines improve image similarity but provide more limited downstream detection recovery, and Stable Diffusion is treated as an asynchronous recovery branch subject to a quality gate rather than a blocking real-time perception step. We evaluate a reference-available quality gate that filters recovered candidates before downstream use: without it, type-aware routing degrades per-image recall to 0.304, whereas with it, recall returns to 0.608, at or above the unrecovered baseline, ensuring the forwarded stream is never worse than the unrecovered frame. REVIVE therefore, provides a structured recovery framework from VOAs in AVs.

</details>


### [17] [Clustered Codebook Quantization for 2D Gaussian-based Image Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05667)
*Runze Cheng,Yicheng Zhan,Josef Spjut,Kaan Akşit*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Cluster-Guided Vector Quantization (CGVQ)方法，通过将高斯参数分组量化以提升压缩效率，在保持视觉质量的同时将比特率降低20%。

Method: 将高斯参数预先划分为同质组进行量化，从而提高压缩效率并实现更精确的参数重建。

Result: 实验表明，与基线相比，CGVQ在保持相近视觉质量的前提下，将比特率降低了20%。

Conclusion: CGVQ通过分组量化优化了高斯基图像表示的率失真性能，显著提升了压缩效率。

Abstract: Gaussian-based image representations effectively model image content using compact parametric primitives while preserving high visual fidelity, yet storing a large number of floating-point parameters per primitive degrades rate-distortion efficiency at higher fidelity targets. To improve the rate-distortion performance in Gaussian representation, we present our Cluster-Guided Vector Quantization (CGVQ), a Gaussian primitive based image compression method. Our key idea is to partition Gaussian parameters further into homogeneous groups prior to quantization, enabling higher compression efficiency and accurate parameter reconstruction. In practice, our extensive experiments show that CGVQ decreases the bpp by 20% with respect to our baseline, while maintaining on-par visual quality

### [18] [Robust Face Super-Resolution and Recognition Through Multi-Feature Aggregation in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05702)
*Marcelo dos Santos,Rayson Laroca,João Carlos Raposo Neves,David Menotti*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FASR++ 是一种基于扩散模型的超分辨率算法，利用参考低分辨率图像和多个辅助低质量图像的特征，生成高质量的超分辨率图像，有效减少身份失真，提升人脸识别性能。该方法无需显式提供软属性或计算梯度，可在多个标准数据集上实现最先进的验证、人脸识别和图像质量指标（如PSNR、SSIM、LPIPS）表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 监控环境中获取的图像常因分辨率低、姿态变化、光照不均和遮挡等问题导致人脸识别困难。现有超分辨率方法易引入图像失真和身份偏差，需结合额外信息以增强识别鲁棒性。

Method: FASR++ 基于扩散模型，融合参考低分辨率图像与多幅辅助低质量图像的特征，通过隐式建模生成高保真超分辨率图像，避免显式属性引导或梯度计算。

Conclusion: FASR++ 通过利用多帧辅助信息与扩散模型，实现了高质量且身份忠实的超分辨率重建，为低质量监控图像的人脸识别提供了高效预处理方案。

Abstract: Images acquired in surveillance environments often suffer from conditions such as low resolution, variations in pose, irregular illumination, and occlusions. Due to the low quality of these images, face recognition algorithms often struggle. This major limitation can be addressed by employing super-resolution techniques that enhance the details of the image. However, due to the high degree of difficulty of the problem, most super-resolution algorithms tend to cause distortions in the image and in the individual's identity. Thus, additional information must be incorporated into the processing to improve recognition robustness. In this regard, surveillance cameras can capture multiple images, even at low quality, and the data extracted from these images, such as consecutive video frames, can significantly enhance both super-resolution and facial recognition. In this work, we introduce FASR++, a diffusion-model-based super-resolution algorithm. It leverages a reference low-resolution image and features extracted from multiple auxiliary low-quality images to generate a super-resolved output, minimizing distortions in the individual's identity. Our approach recovers facial features without explicitly providing soft attributes or computing a function gradient to guide the reconstruction process. FASR++ generates high-quality images that can considerably improve performance in face recognition tasks when used as a pre-processing step. We validate our approach on two standard face recognition datasets and attain state-of-the-art results for verification, face recognition, and image quality metrics such as PSNR, SSIM, and LPIPS.

### [19] [Scene Graph Thinking: Reinforcing Structured Visual Reasoning for Multimodal Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05716)
*Zhiwei Yang,Yuanchen Wu,Nan Zhang,Yucong Meng,Ke Yan,Shouhong Ding*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Scene Graph Thinking (SaGe)新范式，通过显式的场景图表示实现细粒度、结构化的视觉推理。利用自动化数据引擎将图像-文本语料转化为结构化场景图，并构建120K高质量训练数据。采用两阶段图对齐后训练策略：监督微调使多模态大模型内化结构化推理能力，强化学习微调则引入以节点为代理的图奖励机制，促进高效图探索。在八个多模态基准测试中表现显著提升，尤其在细粒度感知与推理任务上效果突出。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型主要关注孤立物体，忽视结构化关系，限制了其在视觉密集型任务中的表现。为提升模型对复杂视觉场景的理解与导航能力，亟需引入更精细的结构化推理机制。

Method: 设计自动化数据引擎将图像-文本数据转换为结构化场景图（实体为节点，视觉关系为边）；构建120K高质量训练数据，基于场景图采样推理轨迹；采用两阶段图对齐后训练：监督微调用于内化结构化推理，强化学习微调引入节点作为代理的图奖励以优化探索效率。

Result: 在八个多模态基准测试中均取得显著性能提升，特别是在细粒度感知与推理任务中表现出色，验证了该方法的有效性与通用性。

Conclusion: Scene Graph Thinking (SaGe) 通过结构化场景图与图对齐训练策略，有效提升了多模态大模型在复杂视觉任务中的感知与推理能力，为未来多模态智能系统提供了新的发展方向。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated strong perception and reasoning capabilities. However, most existing models focus on isolated objects and neglect structured relationships for efficient target navigation, limiting their performance on visually intensive tasks. To address this challenge, we introduce Scene Graph Thinking (SaGe), a novel paradigm that enables fine-grained and structured visual reasoning through explicit scene-graph representations. Specifically, we first introduce an automated data engine that converts flat image-text corpora into structured scene graphs, where hierarchical entities constitute the nodes and diverse visual relations define the edges. Building upon this, we construct 120K high-quality training data by sampling reasoning traces from scene graphs. Then, two-stage graph-aligned post-training paradigms are introduced, where supervised fine-tuning internalizes MLLMs with structured reasoning, and subsequent reinforcement fine-tuning proposes node-as-proxy graph rewards to consolidate efficient graph exploration. With curated data and graph-aligned training, our approach achieves significant improvements across eight multimodal benchmarks, demonstrating strong effectiveness on fine-grained perception and reasoning tasks. Code is available at https://github.com/zwyang6/SaGe.

### [20] [Association Restoration Test: Revealing Restorable Shortcuts after Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05726)
*Amy Lu,Changxiu Ji*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Association Restoration Test (ART)以评估模型在去关联后是否仍能功能性地恢复学习到的标签-属性捷径。通过估计条件关联方向、放大残差成分并用原始分类头评估修改后的特征，ART揭示了现有评价指标（如输出鲁棒性、表示探测）无法捕捉的功能性恢复能力。实验表明，不同指标反映不同维度的捷径缓解效果，强调应采用面向恢复的评估方法来改进去关联与捷径缓解技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法无法判断去关联后保留的关联是否仍可被原始分类器功能使用，导致对去关联效果的评估不充分。

Method: 提出Association Restoration Test (ART)，包括估计类条件关联方向、放大残差组件，并使用原始分类头评估修改后的特征，以检测功能性的捷径恢复可能性。

Result: 在Waterbirds、CelebA、SpuCoDogs及ISIC时间戳伪影扩展数据集上，输出指标、表示探测和ART分别刻画了捷径缓解的不同方面；证明了功能恢复能力是独立且重要的评估维度。

Conclusion: 应发展面向恢复的评估范式，以更准确衡量针对学习到的关联而非单一类别或概念的去关联与捷径缓解方法的有效性。

Abstract: Association unlearning aims to disable learned label-attribute shortcuts while preserving task performance. Existing evaluations mainly measure output-level robustness or probe whether shortcut attributes remain readable in frozen features, but neither test determines whether a retained association remains functionally usable by the original classifier. We propose the Association Restoration Test (ART), a post-hoc diagnostic for functional shortcut restorability. ART estimates class-conditional association directions, amplifies residual components, and evaluates the modified features with the original classifier head. Across Waterbirds, CelebA, SpuCoDogs, and an ISIC timestamp-artifact extension, we show that output metrics, representation probes, and ART characterize distinct aspects of shortcut mitigation. These findings motivate restoration-aware evaluation for unlearning and shortcut-mitigation methods that target learned associations rather than individual classes or concepts.

### [21] [SAMPLe: SAM-based Optimizer for Prompt Learning in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05727)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提示学习方法在提升特定任务性能时往往牺牲了对未见数据的泛化能力，主要由于可学习提示集有限，导致过拟合训练分布。

Method: 提出 SAMPLe（Sharpness-Aware Minimization Prompt Learning），一种基于损失曲面尖锐度感知的优化策略，动态调整优化过程以适应局部曲率和梯度特性，从而在探索与利用之间取得平衡。

Result: SAMPLe 在多种提示学习框架（如 CoOp、CoCoOp、MaPLe、TCP、Co-Prompt）中均显著提升模型性能，增强对未见数据的适应能力，且表现优于现有优化器，具有良好的通用性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SAMPLe 为提示学习提供了一种无需修改模型结构的通用解决方案，有效缓解了性能-泛化之间的权衡，保留了预训练 VLM 的强大泛化潜力。

Abstract: Pre-trained Vision-Language Models (VLMs) like CLIP have proven highly effective as foundation models for various downstream applications. However, prompt learning in VLMs encounters a performance-generalization dilemma: while prompts can be tuned to achieve high accuracy on seen distributions, this tuning process often undermines their generalizability to unseen data. The limited set of learnable prompts, which contextualize and condition the input to steer it toward the task within the pretrained VLM, tends to overfit the training data, leading to a trade-off between task-specific performance and preserving generalization. To address this dilemma, we introduce SAMPLe (Sharpness-Aware Minimization Prompt Learning), a plug-in sharpness-aware optimizer that enhances prompt generalizability by accounting for loss landscape sharpness. Unlike conventional methods, SAMPLe balances exploration and exploitation by satisfying objective function constraints at each step, dynamically adapting to the current optimization state based on the local curvature and gradient properties. This approach reduces overfitting on seen distributions and improves adaptability to unseen data, preserving the generalization potential of pre-trained VLM models. We integrate SAMPLe into multiple prompt learning frameworks, including CoOp, CoCoOp, MaPLe, TCP, and Co-Prompt, demonstrating its effectiveness across diverse methods. Experiments show that SAMPLe elevates prompt learning frameworks and consistently outperforms existing optimizers across diverse settings, establishing itself as a robust, model-agnostic solution for prompt learning.

### [22] [ARMS: Anchor-Relational Motion Streaming for Seamless Solo-Social Motion Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05733)
*Huakun Liu,Qing Yu,Kent Fujiwara,Hideaki Uchiyama,Kiyoshi Kiyokawa*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ARMS提出了一种统一的因果生成过程，通过动态不对称表示解耦个体时间演化与人之间对齐，实现独处与交互状态的无缝切换，支持长时序、增量式动作生成，并在过渡平滑性和社交一致性上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多生成固定长度的动作片段，难以处理独处与互动之间的动态转换，且不适用于长时间增量生成，因此需要一种能够统一处理独处与交互、支持连续生成的新框架。

Method: ARMS采用因果潜在空间和因果关系扩散模型，引入伙伴参考的相对位移项来解耦个体时间演化与人际对齐，通过模式感知的关系门控机制控制跨主体连接，实现同一模型下独处与交互的灵活生成。

Result: 实验表明，ARMS在动作过渡平滑性与社交一致性方面显著优于以交互为中心的基线方法，同时在人类交互基准测试中也达到竞争性表现。

Abstract: Generating temporally continuous and socially coherent human motion from text remains a fundamental challenge, particularly in realistic streams where people act alone, enter interactions, and later disengage. Most existing methods generate fixed-length motion clips under static agent configurations, which makes them brittle to solo-social transitions and unsuitable for incremental generation over long horizons. We propose ARMS, an Anchor-Relational Motion Streaming framework that unifies solo motion and human-human interaction within a single causal generative process. ARMS introduces a dynamics-asymmetric representation that decouples per-person temporal evolution from inter-person alignment via a partner-referenced relative-translation term, enabling seamless switching of social coupling without sacrificing long-horizon stability or spatial consistency between agents. On top of a causal latent space, a causal relational diffusion model progressively refines motion segment by segment using only past context, capturing both intra-person temporal dependencies and inter-person relations. Mode-aware relational gating activates or masks cross-agent connections, allowing the same model to support both solo and interaction generation. Experiments show that ARMS improves transition smoothness and social coherence compared to interaction-centric baselines, while also achieving competitive results on human-human interaction benchmarks.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出并行化GALF与CCALF的设计，采用自适应参数决策机制优化GALF，设计基于失真估计的单次遍历CCALF方案，避免实际滤波操作以减少计算开销。

Result: 与VTM-8.0相比，图像缓冲区访问从152次降至1次，ALF模块运行时间节省约25%，编码性能变化可忽略不计，部分技术已集成至VVC参考软件。

Conclusion: 所提优化框架显著降低了ALF模块的内存访问和计算开销，提升了编码效率，具备良好的工程应用价值，已在实际标准实现中得到采纳。

Abstract: In the Versatile Video Coding~(VVC) standard, adaptive loop filter~(ALF), including Geometry transformation-based Adaptive Loop Filter~(GALF) and Cross Component Adaptive Loop Filter~(CCALF), plays an essential role in reducing compression artifacts. However, it also has high coding complexity and requires many picture buffer accesses in the encoder that will increase external memory access and is unfriendly to the software and hardware design. Therefore, we propose an optimized ALF framework, including the parallel design of GALF and CCALF, the adaptive parameter decision of GALF, and one-pass CCALF scheme by effectively estimating the CCALF filtering distortion without conducting filter operation. Compared to VTM-8.0, the proposed method can reduce the picture buffer access from 152 to 1 and achieve roughly 25\% time-savings of the ALF module with negligible coding performance change under RA configuration. Some of the proposed methods have been adopted in the VVC reference software.

</details>


### [24] [Image2Sim: Scaling Embodied Navigation via Generative Neural Simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05765)
*Zihan Wang,Seungjun Lee,Yinghao Xu,Gim Hee Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Image2Sim是一个实时神经仿真框架，通过从带姿态的RGB-D图像序列构建高质量交互环境，实现3D空间锚定与照片级观察合成的解耦。该方法使用前馈特征高斯模型将带姿态的RGB-D观测提升为3D特征高斯表示，并采用几何感知的一步像素流渲染模型生成高质量全景RGB-D观测。Image2Sim可自动创建大量交互场景和导航训练样本，支持在模拟环境中训练导航模型，并在真实世界零样本设置下实现良好迁移，表明可扩展的神经仿真可作为大规模具身导航训练的有效基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Image2Sim框架，通过解耦3D空间锚定与视觉合成，利用前馈特征高斯模型将带姿态的RGB-D输入快速转换为3D特征高斯表示；并设计几何感知的一步像素流模型，将稀疏噪声的高斯投影转化为高质量全景观测。同时作为自动化数据引擎，生成大量高保真观测、可执行动作和多样化导航指令。

Result: 成功将大量视频和图像转换为近20,000个交互场景，生成超过1000万条导航训练样本；基于这些模拟环境训练的导航模型在主流基准上表现优异，并能有效零样本迁移到真实世界。

Conclusion: 可扩展的神经仿真能够作为大规模具身导航训练的实用基底，显著推动该领域的发展。

Abstract: Embodied navigation aims to build agents that interpret multimodal goals, reason in 3D space, and reach target destinations reliably in the real world. However, progress remains constrained by the lack of scalable, high-fidelity, and physically grounded interactive environments. Although real-world scanned datasets offer visual realism, they are limited by scale. In contrast, synthetic simulators scale more easily but often exhibit large sim-to-real gaps. We introduce Image2Sim, a real-time neural simulation framework that constructs high-quality interactive environments from posed RGB-D image sequences. The central idea is to decouple 3D spatial anchoring from photorealistic observation synthesis. For scene construction, Image2Sim uses a feed-forward feature Gaussian model that lifts posed RGB-D observations into a 3D feature-Gaussian representation in a single pass. For rendering, we propose a Geometry-Aware One-Step Pixel Flow model that transforms sparse and noisy Gaussian projections into high-quality panoramic RGB-D observations. Image2Sim also serves as a fully automated embodied data engine that generates high-fidelity observations, executable actions, and diverse navigation instructions at scale. It converts large collections of videos and images into nearly 20K interactive scenes and synthesizes more than 10 million navigation training samples. Navigation models trained entirely in these neural environments achieve strong improvements on major benchmarks and transfer effectively to real-world zero-shot settings. These results suggest that scalable neural simulation can serve as a practical training substrate for embodied navigation at scale.

### [25] [LEGATO 2: Toward Multimodal Sheet Music Recognition and Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05769)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Legato 2 采用系统级分割与自回归视觉-语言模型相结合的架构，沿乐谱的水平行顺序处理，逐步提取符号记号与语义信息，支持生成包含文本内容的符号转录。

Conclusion: Legato 2 是首个实现系统级顺序处理、支持文本嵌入的端到端大模型，在光学乐谱识别与下游音乐理解任务中均达到新高度，为音乐信息处理提供了可扩展、高精度的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose a novel pipeline, Legato 2, for extracting symbolic notation and semantic knowledge from images of sheet music. Legato 2 features the first large-scale neural model for optical music recognition (OMR) to operate sequentially on a system-by-system basis, following the horizontal lines of notation as they are read on the page, rather than treating the page as an undifferentiated image, enabling better scaling to arbitrarily long inputs. ### [26] [Benchmarking the Robustness of Autonomous Driving to Environmental Illusions: A Lane Perception Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05783)
*Tianyuan Zhang,Xianglong Liu,Aishan Liu,Lu Wang,Yitong Zhang,Peng Yue,Mingchuan Zhang,Siyuan Liang,Dacheng Tao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究针对自动驾驶中被忽视的环境幻觉（如阴影、反射、轮胎痕迹）对车道感知的干扰问题，提出首个基准数据集LanEvil++，涵盖14类幻觉，基于CARLA生成94个高保真3D场景，包含90,292张标注图像、1,596段视频和41,855个视觉问答对。实验表明，环境幻觉显著降低现有车道检测（LD）与视觉-语言模型（ADVLMs）性能，平均导致LD准确率下降5.27%、F1分数下降10.49%，ADVLMs的GPT分数下降2.03%、语言分数下降0.75%。其中阴影影响最严重，最高使准确率下降7.20%。闭环仿真与真实案例均显示幻觉可引发错误驾驶决策。为此提出多模态幻觉防御方法MIDA，显著提升鲁棒性，使LD模型和ADVLMs分别提升4.23%和3.82%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究普遍忽视真实驾驶环境中自然存在的环境幻觉（如阴影、反射、轮胎痕迹），这些现象会干扰视觉感知，导致场景误判，威胁自动驾驶系统安全，亟需系统评估与应对。

Method: 构建首个面向车道感知的环境幻觉评估基准LanEvil++，利用CARLA模拟器生成94个可控高保真3D场景，采集90,292张图像、1,596段视频及41,855个视觉问答对；通过对比分析主流车道检测模型与视觉-语言模型在幻觉下的表现，识别关键脆弱因素，并提出多模态幻觉防御方法MIDA以增强鲁棒性。

Result: 环境幻觉显著降低主流车道感知模型性能：LD模型平均准确率下降5.27%、F1下降10.49%；ADVLMs的GPT分数下降2.03%、语言分数下降0.75%；阴影为最严重干扰因素，最大造成7.20%准确率损失；闭环仿真与真实场景验证均揭示其引发安全风险；所提MIDA方法有效提升鲁棒性，分别实现4.23%和3.82%的性能增益。

Conclusion: 环境幻觉是自动驾驶系统中不可忽视的安全隐患，尤其严重影响车道感知任务。本研究通过建立LanEvil++基准并提出MIDA方法，首次系统揭示了幻觉对感知模型的影响机制，并提供了有效的防御策略，为提升自动驾驶系统的环境鲁棒性提供了重要支撑。

Abstract: Environmental illusions (eg., shadows, reflections, and tire marks) are naturally existing yet overlooked phenomena in real-world driving environments. They can disturb visual perception, leading to misinterpretation of the scene and posing serious safety risks to autonomous driving (AD) systems. However, existing researches largely overlook these phenomena, leaving a critical gap. To address this issue, we study AD robustness through the lane perception perspective, a fundamental task supporting core functions like cruise control and lane centering. We focus on two representative models: conventional lane detection (LD) and vision-language model-based systems (ADVLMs). In this work, we introduce the first benchmark, LanEvil++, for evaluating the robustness of lane perception under environmental illusions. LanEvil++ encompasses 14 types of illusions and leverages the CARLA simulator to generate 94 high-fidelity, fully controllable 3D scenes, yielding a dataset of 90,292 annotated images, 1,596 video clips, and 41,855 visual question answering pairs. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that environmental illusions substantially degrade the performance of state-of-the-art LD methods. On average, LD models experience a 5.27% drop in Accuracy and a 10.49% decline in F1-score, while ADVLMs show a 2.03% reduction in GPT-score and a 0.75% drop in Language-score. Among all illusions, shadows emerge as the most disruptive factor, reducing accuracy by up to 7.20%. Furthermore, closed-loop simulations reveal that these illusions can lead to incorrect driving decisions. Complementary real-world case studies highlight safety-critical failures in actual traffic scenes. To enhance robustness, we propose the Multimodal Illusion Defense Approach (MIDA). MIDA achieves substantial gains under challenging conditions, boosting robustness by 4.23% on LD models and 3.82% on ADVLMs.

### [27] [DeSeG: Decoupling Semantic Intent and Geometric Constraints for Physically Plausible Human-Scene Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05787)
*Jiakun Li,Zhe Li,Wenqiang Wu,Zheng Chang,Mingqi Gao,Jinyu Yang,Feng Zheng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成模型存在语义-几何纠缠的归纳偏置，导致在严格几何约束下忽略语义意图，引发身体与场景穿透等物理幻觉。需要解耦语义与几何，以实现更真实的交互生成。

Method: 提出层次化框架DeSeG：1）残差语义规划器，将文本指令与规范化目标体素编码至紧凑隐空间，实现独立于空间轨迹的细粒度语义控制；2）物理正则化扩散执行器，将可微排斥势场嵌入扩散目标，强制生成过程考虑碰撞规避。

Result: 在Lingo数据集上，DeSeG显著优于现有基线：平均场景穿透减少47%，语义对齐提升29%，达到当前最佳性能。

Conclusion: DeSeG通过显式解耦语义意图与几何约束，有效缓解了语义-几何纠缠问题，显著提升了人类-场景交互生成的物理真实性与语义一致性，为高保真虚拟人交互建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: Synthesizing physically plausible human-scene interactions (HSI) remains a critical challenge in computer vision and the development of human avatars. Although recent generative models enable diverse motion synthesis, they suffer from an inductive bias referred to as semantic-geometric entanglement. Because spatial constraints often strongly correlate with specific actions in training data, monolithic models will learn the shortcut bias, aggressively overriding the semantic intent when faced with strict geometric cues. Furthermore, this entanglement exacerbates physical hallucinations, such as body-scene penetrations. To address these limitations, we propose DeSeG, a hierarchical framework that explicitly decouples semantic intent from geometric constraints. First, we introduce a Residual Semantic Planner that encodes textual instructions and canonicalized goal voxels into a compact latent space, enabling fine-grained semantic control independent of spatial trajectories. Second, we propose a physics regularized diffusion executor that incorporates differentiable repulsive potential fields directly into the diffusion objective, enforcing collision-aware motion generation. Extensive experiments on the Lingo dataset demonstrate that DeSeG achieves state-of-the-art performance, reducing mean scene penetration by 47% and improving semantic alignment by 29% over the SOTA baselines.

### [28] [Segmentation before Answering: Pixel Grounding for MLLM Visual Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05798)

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SegAnswer方法，将多模态大模型的视觉推理单位从传统的边界框（bounding box）升级为像素级分割掩码（segmentation mask），以实现更精细的视觉区域聚焦。该方法通过消除背景干扰和冗余物体，提升视觉输入的精确性，并更好地匹配模型对视觉标记的位置嵌入结构。实验表明，该方法在高分辨率感知、通用感知及幻觉抑制等多个基准上均取得一致改进，同时在分割任务中表现优异，验证了其可靠的像素级定位能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出SegAnswer框架，先进行像素级图像分割生成掩码，再将分割后的区域作为视觉输入送入多模态大模型，实现以分割掩码为单位的视觉-语言推理。该方法利用细粒度掩码隔离目标，增强视觉输入的准确性，并与模型的位置嵌入机制更好对齐。

Result: 在多个主流基准测试中，包括高分辨率感知、通用感知和抗幻觉能力评估，SegAnswer均表现出显著优于传统边界框方法的性能；同时在图像分割任务上也展现出良好的泛化能力，证明其具备可靠的像素级定位能力。

Conclusion: SegAnswer通过引入像素级分割掩码作为视觉推理的基本单元，有效提升了多模态大模型在复杂视觉场景下的推理精度与鲁棒性，为未来‘思考图像’的精细化推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Recent advancements in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have evolved from static perception to interleaved visual-language reasoning, often referred to as ``thinking with images''. A basic operation in this reasoning process is to zoom in on regions of interest (often represented with bounding boxes) to acquire finer visual details. In this paper, we propose \textbf{Seg}mentation before \textbf{Answer}ing (SegAnswer), which shifts the unit of zoom-in from the popular bounding box to pixel-level segmentation mask. By employing fine-grained masks to isolate the target area from cluttered environments, segmented visual input yields a more precise region of interest, effectively filtering out redundant background and interfering objects. Furthermore, the discrete patches of segmented visual input align more seamlessly with how MLLMs structure visual tokens via positional embeddings. In experiments, we evaluate SegAnswer across diverse benchmarks, including high-resolution perception, general perception, and hallucination. It achieves consistent improvements and also exhibits considerable performance on segmentation tasks, validating its capability for reliable pixel grounding.

### [29] [TRIG: Trajectory-Rig Decoupled Metric Geometry Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05801)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出TRIG框架，通过解耦相机位姿为自车轨迹与相机刚性结构成分，采用解耦编码与监督策略分别约束轨迹演化与刚性几何；引入稀疏时空注意力，分离跨相机交互与时间聚合过程，降低全局注意力计算成本。

Abstract: Vision-centric autonomous driving requires accurate metric geometry and ego-motion estimation from synchronized multi-camera observations. Recent visual geometry models show strong performance in pose estimation, depth prediction, and 3D reconstruction, but are not tailored to rigid multi-camera driving systems. They often encode camera poses as entangled representations, in which time-varying ego-motion and static camera-rig geometry are jointly modeled, limiting the utilization of vehicle-side geometric priors. We propose Trajectory-Rig Decoupled Metric Geometry Learning (TRIG), a geometry perception framework for autonomous driving. TRIG factorizes camera poses into ego-trajectory and camera-rig components, enabling separate modeling of ego-motion and static multi-camera topology. We introduce decoupled pose encoding and supervision, which separately constrain trajectory evolution and rig geometry for metric-consistent learning. Moreover, sparse Temporal--Spatial attention separates cross-camera interaction from temporal aggregation, reducing global attention cost while preserving geometric reasoning. Experiments on five autonomous driving benchmarks show that TRIG achieves state-of-the-art performance in pose estimation, metric depth prediction, and 3D reconstruction.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ROP是可预防的儿童失明原因，尤其在低收入和中等收入国家，缺乏训练有素的眼科医生；Plus病作为治疗指征，其判断主观且变异大，亟需自动化筛查工具以扩大专科服务覆盖范围，但目前非洲地区的相关研究证据仍有限。

Method: 基于121名肯尼亚早产儿的数据，涵盖237只眼和1635张眼底图像，由两名分级员标注血管用于分割训练。采用患者分组嵌套交叉验证，评估了包括图像分类器、多实例学习、多任务分割-分类以及分步分类在内的11种模型配置，比较其在眼级Plus检测中的性能。

Result: 血管分割在测试集上取得平均Dice系数0.533、IoU 0.368、敏感性0.623和特异性0.979。仅使用RGB图像的分类器虽敏感性高但易过度转诊，而结合分割的模型更具特异性。通过组合策略——以OR方式提高敏感性，以AND方式提升特异性，或采用概率集成方法，达到最佳综合性能：敏感性0.692，特异性0.914，平衡准确率0.803，优于单一视觉分类器。

Conclusion: 在肯尼亚数据中，分类与血管分割在ROP Plus检测中具有互补作用：分类器有助于敏感发现病例，分割则提升特异性并减少过度转诊。未来非洲地区的ROP人工智能系统应采用融合工作流程，并开展多中心前瞻性验证。

Abstract: Background. Retinopathy of prematurity (ROP) is a preventable cause of childhood blindness, with rising burden in low- and middle-income countries where ROP-trained ophthalmologists are scarce. Plus disease, marked by retinal vessel dilation and tortuosity, triggers treatment but is subjective and variable. Automated screening could extend specialist reach, but African evidence remains limited.
  Methods. We analysed 121 Kenyan preterm infants, covering 237 eyes and 1,635 fundus images graded as No Plus, Pre-Plus or Plus. Vessel annotations from two graders supported segmentation training. Eleven configurations were evaluated for eye-level Plus detection using patient-grouped nested cross-validation, including image classifiers, multiple-instance learning, multi-task segmentation-classification, and segment-then-classify pipelines.
  Results. Vessel segmentation was feasible, achieving pooled Dice 0.533, IoU 0.368, sensitivity 0.623 and specificity 0.979 on held-out images. RGB classifiers were highly sensitive but over-referred, while segmentation-coupled models were more specific. Combining approaches improved performance: an OR-based screen achieved the highest sensitivity, an AND-based confirmation achieved the highest specificity, and a probability ensemble gave the best balanced performance, with sensitivity 0.692, specificity 0.914 and balanced accuracy 0.803, outperforming the vision classifier alone.
  Conclusions. Classification and vessel segmentation are complementary for ROP Plus detection in Kenyan data. Classifiers support sensitive case-finding, while segmentation improves specificity and reduces over-referral. African ROP AI systems should use combined workflows and undergo prospective multi-site validation.

</details>


### [31] [Realistic Compound-Lens Defocus Blur Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05837)
*Yunkyu Lee,Woohyeok Kim,Sunghyun Cho*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于合成多样化复合镜头真实感散焦模糊图像数据集的流水线，结合了高效的波光学点扩散函数（PSF）计算、深度感知的散焦渲染及相机图像信号处理（ISP）模拟，生成大规模、高保真的合成数据集CLDefocus。实验表明，基于该数据集训练的模型在跨设备泛化能力上优于现有真实和合成数据集训练的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习去模糊方法依赖于训练数据，且在不同相机和镜头间性能下降，主要由于现有数据集在光学多样性和真实性方面存在局限。为解决这一问题，需要一种能够生成多样化、真实感强的散焦模糊数据集的方法。

Method: 提出了一种集成波光学点扩散函数计算（通过Debye CZT传播）、深度感知散焦渲染（包含遮挡处理）以及在辐射线性空间中进行模糊合成并模拟相机ISP的统一流水线，以实现大规模、真实感强的散焦图像对生成。

Result: 成功构建了名为CLDefocus的大规模合成数据集，涵盖多种镜头特性；分析表明真实采集数据集存在缺陷，可能影响全参考评估的公平性；基于CLDefocus训练的模型在跨设备场景下表现出更强的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的合成流水线可有效生成多样化、真实感强的散焦模糊数据集，显著提升去模糊模型的跨设备泛化性能，为后续视觉任务提供了高质量训练资源。

Abstract: Defocus blur degrades fine image structures and limits visual perception, which can adversely affect downstream vision tasks. Although recent deep learning deblurring methods have achieved strong performance, their effectiveness depends on training data and often degrades across cameras and lenses due to limited optical diversity and realism in existing datasets. In this paper, we propose a pipeline for synthesizing realistic defocus deblurring datasets for diverse compound lenses. It integrates efficient wave-optics PSF computation via Debye CZT propagation, depth-aware defocus rendering with occlusion handling, and blur synthesis in the radiometrically linear space with camera ISP simulation. This unified pipeline enables the scalable generation of photorealistic defocus datasets with diverse lens characteristics. Using our pipeline, we generate CLDefocus, a large-scale synthetic dataset containing lens-diverse defocus image pairs. We further analyze the limitations of real-captured defocus datasets and show that such imperfections can bias full-reference evaluation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that models trained on CLDefocus achieve improved cross-device generalization compared to models trained on existing real and synthetic datasets.

### [32] [Breaking Spurious Correlations via Generative Randomization and Cross-Variant Self-Supervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05850)
*Suraj Yadav,Anjaneya Sharma,Siddharth Yadav*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种两阶段框架，通过生成干预来学习背景无关的视觉表征。首先利用零样本分割分离前景对象，并通过结构保持的扩散模型生成上下文变化的图像变体；其次引入跨变体自监督学习，使同一对象在不同背景下的变体形成对比学习中的正样本对，从而促使编码器关注对象本身而非背景。最后通过分层学习率的GroupDRO微调策略进一步提升鲁棒性。在多个分布偏移基准测试中表现优异，尤其在Waterbirds、MetaShift和NICO++上分别达到92.5%、81.7%和87.4%的最佳最差组性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络在经验风险最小化训练下容易因依赖物体标签与背景之间的虚假相关性，在分布偏移场景中表现不佳。现有生成方法虽能生成反事实图像，但通常仅作为数据增强，未能强制模型摆脱对背景的依赖。因此需要一种机制来显式地学习与背景无关的表示。

Method: 提出两阶段框架：第一阶段使用零样本分割提取前景，并通过结构保持的扩散模型生成背景变换的图像变体；第二阶段采用跨变体自监督学习，以不同背景下的同一对象变体为正样本对进行对比学习，迫使编码器聚焦于对象本质特征。随后采用带分层学习率的ERM热启动与GroupDRO微调策略优化模型鲁棒性。

Result: 在Waterbirds、MetaShift和NICO++等多个分布偏移基准上均取得领先性能，其中最差组准确率分别达到92.5%、81.7%和87.4%，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架有效引导模型学习背景不变的视觉表征，显著提升了在分布偏移场景下的泛化能力，为解决模型对虚假相关性的依赖提供了新思路。

Abstract: Deep neural networks trained with Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM) often fail under distribution shifts because they exploit spurious correlations between object labels and background context. Recent generative approaches address this issue by creating counterfactual images with altered contexts, but typically use these samples as standard data augmentation, leaving the model free to retain background-sensitive representations. We propose a two-stage framework that uses generative intervention to explicitly learn background-invariant visual representations. First, we isolate the foreground object using zero-shot segmentation and generate context-shifted variants with a structure-preserving diffusion model, preserving object identity while varying the surrounding environment. We then introduce Cross-Variant Self-Supervised Learning, where variants of the same object under different backgrounds form positive pairs in a contrastive objective. This encourages the encoder to align object-centric representations while suppressing background-specific cues. Then, we fine-tune the pretrained encoder using an ERM warm-up followed by GroupDRO with layer-wise learning rates. Experiments on distribution-shift benchmarks demonstrate best worst-group performance, achieving 92.5% on Waterbirds, 81.7% on MetaShift, and 87.4% on NICO++. Code: https://github.com/surajyadav-research/GRSSL

</details>

Method: 提出 AVA-VLM 模型，采用人类式的粗到细推理策略：先在低分辨率全局图像上进行初步判断，仅当必要时才请求高分辨率局部区域进行详细分析；同时构建区域感知的 Chain-of-Thought 数据集，训练模型决策机制。

Conclusion: AVA-VLM 通过模仿人类观察行为，实现高效且可靠的视觉理解，适用于复杂多变的真实施工场景监控任务。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are promising for construction-site monitoring, and recent construction-tailored VLMs have primarily adapted pretrained VLMs through direct QA-style fine-tuning from a single global image. We argue that this direct paradigm remains limited for in-the-wild deployment in terms of operational range, reliability under reduced-resolution inputs, and inference efficiency. To address these challenges, we propose AVA-VLM, an Adaptive Visual Attention-Vision Language Model that follows a human-inspired coarse-to-fine reasoning strategy. AVA-VLM first reasons over a low-resolution global image and selectively requests a high-resolution local crop only when detailed inspection is needed, similar to how a human inspector zooms in on hard-to-see yet important areas. We further introduce a region-aware Chain-of-Thought dataset that teaches the model when to inspect, where to crop, and how to use local evidence. Experiments show that AVA-VLM improves reliability under long-distance and reduced-resolution conditions while substantially reducing visual-token usage.

### [35] [Few-Medoids: An Embarrassingly Simple Coreset Selection Method for Few-Shot Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05891)
*Cemil-Andrei Dilmac,Florinel-Alin Croitoru,Radu Tudor Ionescu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种简单有效的少样本知识蒸馏中数据集核心子集选择方法few-medoids，该方法通过选取每类样本中距离类别中心（平均图像）最近的样本构建核心子集。在四个数据集和三种教师-学生模型组合上的大量实验表明，few-medoids consistently优于随机选择和其他现有核心子集选择方法，可作为未来研究中的即插即用基线。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在少样本知识蒸馏场景下，传统的核心子集选择策略往往难以超越随机选择基准，因此需要一种简单但高效的替代方案来提升模型训练效率与性能。

Method: few-medoids 方法通过计算每个类别的平均图像（中心点），并选择距离该中心最近的样本构成核心子集，实现快速且具有代表性的数据选择。

Result: 在多个图像分类任务和模型配置上，few-medoids 均显著优于随机选择及其他主流核心子集选择方法，表现出稳定且一致的优越性。

Abstract: Coreset selection aims to identify a small and highly representative subset of a massive dataset for efficient model training. The problem remains challenging even in the few-shot knowledge distillation (KD) setup, where a full-scale pre-trained teacher informs the student network. Typical sample selection strategies often struggle to surpass the random selection baseline. In this paper, we showcase few-medoids, an embarrassingly simple coreset selection strategy that chooses the samples closest to the centroid (average image) of each class. We present extensive KD experiments on four datasets, covering a wide range of image classification problems, and three teacher-student model pairs, comprising both convolutional and transformer networks. Although the proposed method is embarrassingly simple, our empirical results indicate that few-medoids is able to consistently surpass the random selection baseline, as well as the other coreset selection strategies. We therefore consider that few-medoids can be used as a drop-in replacement for commonly-used baselines (e.g. herding or k-center Greedy), in future research on coreset selection. To reproduce the reported results, we publicly release our code at https://github.com/CemilAndreiDilmac/Few-Shot-KD-Coreset.

### [36] [GaussFusion: Towards Multimodal 3D Gaussian Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05906)

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting provides an explicit representation that jointly models geometry and appearance, serving as a scalable foundation for 3D representation learning. Existing pre-training methods for Gaussian representations, such as masked Gaussian reconstruction, primarily capture local structures but offer limited semantic supervision. In this paper, we propose GaussFusion, a multimodal pre-training framework for 3D Gaussian representations. GaussFusion integrates image and text supervision into masked Gaussian modeling through cross-modal semantic alignment, enabling the Gaussian encoder to learn both visual and language-level semantic information during pre-training. To better adapt masked modeling to the non-uniform distribution of Gaussian primitives, we further propose Gaussian Salience-guided Multi-scale Hole Masking (GSHM). GSHM constructs spatially continuous masked regions based on Gaussian salience. By applying hole masks at multiple scales, GSHM encourages the encoder to capture both fine-grained local patterns and broader structural dependencies. Extensive experiments on downstream tasks demonstrate that GaussFusion improves the transferability of Gaussian representations. ### [37] [PolicyShiftGuard: Benchmarking and Improving Policy-Adaptive Image Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05910)
*Mingyang Song,Luxin Xu,Haoyu Sun,Minzhou Pan,Yu Cheng,Bo Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究政策自适应图像防护，提出PolicyShiftBench基准和PolicyShiftGuard模型，通过两阶段训练实现对不同安全政策的灵活响应，显著提升模型在政策变化下的鲁棒性与泛化能力。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实场景中同一图像在不同产品或政策下可能被允许或禁止，现有图像防护模型依赖图像固有安全性，无法适应动态政策变化，亟需具备政策自适应能力的防护机制。

Method: 提出PolicyShiftGuard模型，采用两阶段训练：先使用随机策略监督微调（RP-SFT）增强多策略理解，再通过边界对比较损失（BP-Adapt）学习相同图像在通过/阻止政策间的区分能力。

Conclusion: 政策自适应图像防护是实际部署中的关键挑战，PolicyShiftGuard通过精心设计的训练策略实现了对新政策的有效泛化，为构建可动态调整的安全防护系统提供了有效解决方案。

Real deployments are different: the same image may be allowed in one product, restricted in another, and newly disallowed when a policy boundary changes. We study policy-adaptive image guardrailing, where a model must decide whether an image violates the currently supplied policy and generalize to held-out policy definitions. We introduce PolicyShiftBench, a comprehensive benchmark with 2,000 policy-discriminative instances over 265 images, where each image is paired with 7.55 policy-conditioned prompts on average to test whether models adapt to the active policy rather than relying on image-level safety priors. We then propose PolicyShiftGuard, a compact policy-conditioned guardrail trained with a two-stage training recipe that combines Randomized Policy SFT (RP-SFT) with Boundary-Pair Policy Adaptation (BP-Adapt). BP-Adapt trains matched prompts for the same image and risk category using standard label supervision and a pairwise comparison loss that separates blocking policies from passing policies. Experiments show that existing VLMs and specialized guardrails remain brittle under policy shifts, while PolicyShiftGuard substantially improves policy-sensitive performance. The 7B model achieves SOTA performance of 76.9 Avg. F1 and 72.1 Avg. PSS on PolicyShiftBench, transfers well to UnSafeBench and SafeEditBench, and improves the latency-performance trade-off with a concise output format. Ablations confirm that matched pass/block boundary pairs are essential for stable policy adaptation.

</details>


### [38] [Progressive Reasoning with Primitive Correction for Compositional Zero-Shot Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05911)
*Ziyi Chen,Haoyan Shi,Sunhan Xu,Congyan Lang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PRPC提出一种渐进式推理框架，通过双向依赖建模和原型修正机制，显式捕捉属性与对象间的上下文关系，解决传统方法中独立预测或单向条件建模导致的误差传播问题。该框架将CZSL建模为结构化的问答式思维链过程，并引入基于GRPO的强化学习后训练，提升中间推理步骤的可靠性与逻辑一致性。在三个基准数据集上实验表明，PRPC达到当前最优性能，验证了渐进推理与双向修正的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在组合零样本学习（CZSL）中要么独立预测属性和对象，忽略了它们之间的强上下文依赖；要么采用单向条件建模（如以对象引导属性预测），易受误差传播影响。因此，亟需一种能够同时建模双向依赖并抑制早期错误的方法。

Method: PRPC将CZSL建模为结构化的Q&A式思维链推理过程，通过逐步推理实现属性与对象的相互校正。利用预定义的语义步骤约束多模态大模型生成中间决策，并引入基于GRPO的强化学习后训练，给予每一步推理阶段奖励，以增强推理过程的可靠性和逻辑一致性。

Result: 在三个主流CZSL基准数据集上的大量实验表明，PRPC显著优于现有方法，实现了当前最优性能，证明了渐进推理与双向修正机制对提升组合泛化能力的有效性。

Conclusion: PRPC通过显式建模属性与对象间的双向依赖关系，结合渐进式推理与中间步骤的相互校正，有效缓解了误差传播问题，显著提升了组合零样本学习的鲁棒性与泛化能力，是当前最先进方法。

Abstract: Compositional Zero-Shot Learning (CZSL) aims to combine known attributes and objects as primitives for recognizing previously unseen attribute-object pairs. Prior works either predict attributes and objects independently, missing their strong contextual dependency, or use unidirectional conditional modeling (e.g., object-guided attribute prediction), which is prone to error propagation. We propose PRPC, a Progressive Reasoning framework with Primitive Correction, which explicitly models the bidirectional dependency between attributes and objects via step-wise inference. PRPC performs mutual correction of primitives to suppress prediction errors in earlier steps. Specifically, we formulate CZSL as structured, Q&A-style Chain-of-Thought reasoning process and constrain the MLLM to follow predefined semantic steps to generate intermediate decisions. To further enhance the reliability and logical consistency of intermediate reasoning, we introduce reinforcement learning post-training with a GRPO-based objective, providing step-level rewards aligned with the progressive inference procedure. Extensive experiments on three CZSL benchmarks demonstrate that PRPC achieves state-of-the-art performance, validating the effectiveness of progressive reasoning and bidirectional correction for robust compositional generalization.
