Result: LLaVA和Qwen在各项指标上表现出色，双向余弦相似度达0.67–0.76；在462个实际验证的交通标志中，有68个被识别为因逆反射性能不足需立即更换，验证了框架的有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的综合评估框架实现了日间与夜间性能的系统化融合，具备高精度、低成本、可扩展的优势，可作为传统人工检测的高效替代方案，适用于各类交通管理部门进行交通标志的智能化维护管理。

Abstract: Traffic signs are crucial components of road safety, serving as visual tools under all lighting conditions. The Manual on Uniform Traffic Control Devices (MUTCD) specifies daytime visual factors such as legibility and color contrast, and nighttime retroreflectivity requirements. Traditional assessment methods rely on manual inspections, which the Federal Highway Administration (FHWA) notes are subjective, labor-intensive and pose safety concerns, while retroreflectometers are expensive and unaffordable for smaller agencies. Most existing studies focus on either daytime factors or nighttime retroreflectivity but rarely integrate both aspects comprehensively. This study develops a novel framework that systematically evaluates traffic signs through integrated daytime-nighttime assessment. The methodology employs three fine-tuned Vision Language Models (VLMs) for daytime visual performance assessment across four key factors: legibility, color, surface and shape integrity, and surrounding environment conditions. VLM predictions are converted to numerical scores through sentiment analysis and Contrastive Language-Image Pre-Training (CLIP) scoring, while nighttime performance is assessed using LiDAR-derived retroreflectivity following established calibration procedures. The framework integrates these components into a comprehensive Sign Condition Index (SCI) for maintenance guidance. Evaluation results demonstrated that LLaVA and Qwen outperformed InternVL, achieving bidirectional cosine similarity scores of 0.67-0.76 across all factors. Among 462 validated traffic signs, 68 were flagged by the proposed framework as requiring immediate replacement due to inadequate retroreflectivity performance. This research provides a cost-effective alternative to traditional manual inspections for comprehensive traffic sign condition assessment.

### [88] [Prompt-Adapter Context Routing for Parameter-Efficient Multi-Shot Long Video Extrapolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06481)
*Anna Córdoba,Adam Puente Tercero,Nerea Angulo Hijo,Mar Linares Tercero,Julia Barrientos,Ainhoa Miranda,Jesús Olivera*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成方法在长视频外推中面临实体一致性差、场景结构混乱、视觉风格不统一及因果进展断裂等问题，尤其在无需全模型微调的前提下实现高质量长视频生成仍具挑战。因此需要一种轻量级、可扩展且能保持长期一致性的方法。

Method: PACR-Video 冻结文本到视频扩散变换器，引入低秩时序适配器，由学习的镜头角色提示标记驱动；构建递归提示银行存储前序镜头中的实体、位置、动作和风格提示，并通过适配器门控机制根据叙事依赖动态路由；采用 Shot-Local/Story-Global 目标函数，融合下一镜头重建、跨镜头身份对比与提示稀疏正则化；设计适配器组合调度策略平衡早期视觉一致性与后期事件推进及视角变化。

Result: 在六个多镜头与长视频基准上，PACR-Video 在分布质量、语义对齐、身份一致性、时间平滑性、运动稳定性、过渡连贯性和人类偏好等方面均超越文本到视频、基于微调、记忆增强、流式处理及递归上下文等基线方法，证明了紧凑提示路由与轻量时序适配足以支持稳定长视频外推。

Conclusion: PACR-Video 证明了仅通过少量可学习参数（如提示标记与适配器）即可实现高质量、长期一致的视频生成，为高效、可控的长视频外推提供了新范式。

Abstract: We present PACR-Video, a parameter-efficient framework for multi-shot long video extrapolation that preserves recurring entities, scene structure, visual style, and causal progression without full generator fine-tuning. PACR-Video keeps a text-to-video diffusion transformer frozen and augments it with low-rank temporal adapters conditioned by learned shot-role prompt tokens. To maintain long-horizon coherence, it builds a recursive prompt bank that stores compact entity, location, action, and style prompts from previous shots, then routes them through adapter gates according to predicted narrative dependencies. A Shot-Local/Story-Global tuning objective combines next-shot reconstruction, cross-shot identity contrast, and prompt sparsity regularization, while an adapter composition schedule balances early-shot visual consistency with later-shot event progression and viewpoint change. Across six multi-shot and long-video benchmarks, PACR-Video outperforms text-to-video, tuning-based, memory-augmented, streaming, and recursive-context baselines on distributional quality, semantic alignment, identity consistency, temporal smoothness, motion stability, transition coherence, and human preference. These results show that compact prompt routing and lightweight temporal adaptation provide sufficient controllable capacity for stable long video extrapolation.

### [89] [Mitigating Domain Shift in Conditioned Floor Plan Generation: Synthetic Pre-training for Data-Efficient Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06483)
*Matthieu Ospici,Arnaud Gueze,Luc Bourrat,Adrien Bernhardt*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有条件化平面图生成模型在跨域应用中表现不佳，因不同地区建筑风格、空间限制和建造习惯差异大，而获取新标注数据成本高。当前缺乏对这类模型鲁棒性的系统研究，亟需有效方法以减少对目标域标注数据的依赖。

Method: 提出一种程序化合成数据生成方法，通过强制施加非重叠房间、合法门位置、图一致性等物理约束，同时引入高度不规则的空间布局与剧烈几何扰动来牺牲建筑真实性，从而构建大规模合成训练数据集，并用于模型预训练及微调初始化。

Conclusion: 通过引入具有严格物理约束但弱化建筑真实性的合成数据进行预训练，可有效提升条件化平面图生成模型的跨域鲁棒性，大幅降低对目标域标注数据的需求，为实际部署提供高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Robustness to domain shift is a key requirement for floor plan generative models to be applicable beyond the single dataset they were trained on, as floor plans vary widely across regions due to distinct architectural cultures, spatial constraints, and construction practices, while acquiring new annotated datasets remains costly and domain-specific. Yet, no prior work has studied this robustness in the context of conditioned floor plan generation. In this paper, we evaluate state-of-the-art models from two fundamentally different generative paradigms across three public datasets (RPLAN, MagicPlan and Swiss Dwellings) and show that they are highly sensitive to domain shift, with up to an order of magnitude performance degradation when transferred across domains. We show that pre-training on this synthetic data considerably improves zero-shot cross-domain performance, outperforming in-domain training on MagicPlan. Furthermore, it provides a highly effective initialization for fine-tuning, accelerating target domain adaptation and outperforming real-world initialization baselines by up to 40% in a low-data regime.

### [90] [AirflowAttack: Thermal-Airflow Adversarial Perturbations against Infrared Remote-Sensing Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06485)
*Cong Su,Jiaju Han,Xuemeng Sun,Chengyin Hu,Qike Zhang,Jiujiang Guo,Yiwei Wei,Jiahuan Long*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AirflowAttack is the first adversarial attack targeting infrared remote-sensing vision-language models (VLMs), leveraging thermal-airflow turbulence as a physical perturbation prior. It uses a lightweight, input-agnostic generator to create realistic perturbations that achieve a 48.5% mean zero-shot attack success rate across five CLIP backbones—surpassing existing IR-specific baselines. The attack reduces scene-classification accuracy by up to 38.2% in six state-of-the-art VLMs and induces overconfidence in misclassification, with models falsely interpreting perturbations as real thermal features. Ablation studies confirm the airflow prior enhances physical plausibility without sacrificing attack effectiveness. The work introduces a benchmark across 11 models and 4 tasks, revealing significant vulnerabilities in IR VLMs.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Vision-language models are increasingly used in security-critical infrared remote sensing, but their vulnerability to adversarial attacks remains unexplored. This work aims to identify and exploit such vulnerabilities, particularly through physically plausible perturbations derived from real-world thermal-airflow dynamics.

Method: AirflowAttack employs a lightweight generator that synthesizes input-agnostic perturbations guided by physically plausible airflow patterns. The generator is optimized on a surrogate CLIP model and then transferred to multiple target VLMs. The method leverages thermal-airflow turbulence as a natural perturbation prior to ensure realism.

Result: The attack achieves a 48.5% mean zero-shot scene-classification attack success rate across five CLIP backbones, outperforming four IR-specific baselines (27.7–37.0%). It reduces accuracy by up to 38.2% in six state-of-the-art VLMs and causes models to become more confident in incorrect predictions, mistaking perturbations for genuine thermal evidence like temperature gradients and convection. Ablations confirm that the airflow prior improves physical plausibility without reducing attack efficacy.

Conclusion: This work reveals critical adversarial vulnerabilities in infrared remote-sensing VLMs. By using thermally grounded perturbations, AirflowAttack demonstrates that current models can be misled into false confidence, highlighting the urgent need for robustness evaluation and defense mechanisms in this emerging domain.

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly deployed on infrared (IR) remote sensing imagery in security-critical settings, yet their adversarial robustness remains unexamined. We present AirflowAttack, to our knowledge the first adversarial attack for IR remote-sensing VLMs and the first to weaponize thermal-airflow turbulence as the perturbation prior. A lightweight generator synthesizes a single input-agnostic perturbation regularized toward physically plausible airflow patterns. Optimized on one surrogate CLIP model, it attains a mean zero-shot scene-classification attack success rate (ASR, the fraction of samples whose top-1 class changes) of 48.5% across five diverse CLIP backbones, far exceeding four IR-specific physical baselines (27.7--37.0%). Applied to six state-of-the-art VLMs, it cuts scene-classification accuracy by up to 38.2% relative, yet paradoxically makes some models more confident in their IR analysis, confabulating the perturbation as genuine thermal evidence such as temperature gradients and convection. Ablations show the airflow prior raises physical plausibility at no measurable cost to attack success. Together with a benchmark spanning eleven models and four tasks, these findings expose critical vulnerabilities in the rapidly expanding IR VLM ecosystem.

To stabilize error accumulation during step-wise autoregressive rollout, we introduce point-cloud skeletons that decouple foreground and background assets and project them into camera-view painted-point and template-depth conditions, providing appearance and geometric cues. ### [95] [From RGB Generation to Dense Field Readout: Pixel-Space Dense Prediction with Text-to-Image Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06553)
*Zanyi Wang,Xin Lin,Haodong Li,Dengyang Jiang,Yijiang Li,Pengtao Xie*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出ReChannel，一种基于预训练DiT的轻量级密集预测框架，通过将任务原生输出（如深度、法向量、透明度等）映射到图像平面上的固定像素块，避免了传统方法中对RGB生成接口的依赖。仅使用约33K参数的共享线性头实现高效推理，在多个基准测试上达到新SOTA，尤其在无裁剪图抠图、KITTI深度估计和指代分割任务中表现优异，并比现有方法更快更准确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将密集预测任务转化为目标生成，依赖于RGB合成的输出接口，但密集预测实际需要的是与输入图像平面一致的任务原生输出，而非新渲染的图像内容。因此，需要一种更直接、更高效的接口来利用生成模型中的丰富先验知识。

Method: 提出ReChannel：保留VAE编码器以处理输入分布，移除目标侧解码器；冻结DiT主干并引入任务专用LoRA适配器；通过一个共享的局部线性头将每个令牌映射到其对应大小为p×p×K_t的像素空间块，不引入额外的空间混合。

Result: 在六个密集预测任务和十余个基准上验证，显著提升无裁剪图抠图、KITTI深度估计和指代分割性能，达到新SOTA；在40亿参数设置下，精度更高且速度提升2.48倍，优于基于编辑+潜空间解码的方法。

Conclusion: 生成式预训练可有效服务于密集感知任务，无需继承其复杂的生成输出接口。ReChannel通过极简结构实现了高效、高精度的密集预测，证明了任务原生输出与图像平面对齐的重要性。

Abstract: Large-scale text-to-image models are attractive backbones for dense prediction because RGB generation pretraining learns rich semantic, structural, and geometric priors. Existing generative and editing approaches reuse these priors by casting dense prediction as target generation: annotations such as depth, normals, alpha mattes, masks, and heatmaps are encoded into an RGB-trained VAE latent space and decoded back as image-like targets. We argue this inherits more of the generative output interface than dense prediction requires: unlike RGB synthesis, dense prediction asks for pixel-correct, task-native fields on the same image plane, not new RGB content to be rendered. Our key observation is that a pretrained DiT already organizes RGB inputs through a patch-to-token-to-patch lattice on the image plane, so each token indexes a fixed output patch whose channels can carry task-native quantities instead of RGB appearance. We instantiate this as ReChannel: we keep the VAE encoder for the DiT's input distribution but drop the target-side decoder, adapt the frozen DiT with task LoRA, and map each token to its p x p x K_t pixel-space patch through a shared token-local linear head--about 33K parameters, no spatial mixing. Using FLUX-Klein, we evaluate on six dense prediction tasks and over a dozen benchmarks. This minimal interface sets new state-of-the-art on trimap-free matting, KITTI depth, and referring segmentation, and stays competitive on normals, saliency, and pose. In a matched 4B setting it is more accurate and 2.48x faster than an edit-plus-latent-decode counterpart--dense perception can benefit from generative pretraining without inheriting its output interface.

</details>


### [96] [ProxyPose: 6-DoF Pose Tracking via Video-to-Video Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06555)
*Ruihang Zhang,Felix Taubner,Pooja Ravi,Kiriakos N. Kutulakos,David B. Lindell*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ProxyPose提出了一种新的6-DoF姿态跟踪方法，将问题重新表述为视频到视频的翻译任务。仅需输入视频和第一帧中的一个标记像素，通过微调的视频扩散模型生成一个代理视频，该视频展示了一个彩色多面体在与目标表面区域相同的刚性运动下进行运动。由于代理视频的几何和外观是已知的，其6-DoF轨迹可通过现成的姿态估计求解器恢复。该方法利用大规模视频预训练吸收了处理纹理缺失、透明、反射或变形表面等挑战性情况的能力，且无需依赖3D模型、深度图、物体掩码等额外输入，实现了当前最佳的跟踪精度。此外，该方法还扩展至人脸跟踪、相机姿态估计及复杂真实场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理无纹理、透明、反射或可变形表面时表现不佳，且通常需要额外输入如3D模型、深度图或物体掩码。因此，迫切需要一种不依赖这些额外信息、能有效应对复杂材质和形变的通用6-DoF姿态跟踪方法。

Method: 将6-DoF姿态跟踪转化为视频到视频的翻译任务。使用微调的视频扩散模型，根据输入视频和一个标记像素生成一个代理视频，该视频包含一个具有已知几何和外观的彩色多面体，其运动与目标区域一致。然后利用标准姿态估计方法从代理视频中恢复6-DoF轨迹。

Result: ProxyPose在无需额外输入的情况下实现了当前最先进的6-DoF姿态跟踪精度，并在合成数据上微调后即可有效工作。同时，其能力成功扩展至人脸跟踪、相机姿态估计以及复杂的野外场景，显著超越了现有方法的适用范围。

Conclusion: ProxyPose通过将姿态跟踪问题转化为视频翻译，充分利用了视频预训练模型的强大表征能力，实现了对各种挑战性表面的高精度、通用性强的6-DoF姿态跟踪，且在不依赖额外先验信息的前提下达到了前所未有的性能。

Abstract: Tracking the six-degree-of-freedom (6-DoF) pose of objects and surfaces from monocular video is a long-standing problem in computer vision. To tackle this problem, existing methods require inputs beyond the video itself-such as 3D models, depth maps, object masks, or task-specific learned features-and they struggle with textureless, transparent, reflective, or deformable surfaces. Here, we introduce ProxyPose, which recasts 6-DoF pose tracking as video-to-video translation. Given only a video and a single marked pixel in the first frame, a fine-tuned video diffusion model translates the input into a proxy video-a synthetic video depicting a colored polyhedron undergoing the same local rigid-body motion as the surface region at the marked pixel. Because the proxy's geometry and appearance are known by construction, recovering its full 6-DoF trajectory reduces to classical pose estimation with off-the-shelf solvers. This formulation leverages large-scale video pre-training to absorb the hardest aspects of pose tracking-handling challenging materials, occlusions, and deformations-into the translation step, while operating at the pixel level with no assumptions about object identity, boundaries, or global rigidity. ProxyPose achieves state-of-the-art 6-DoF pose tracking accuracy without the additional inputs required by competing methods and after fine-tuning the video model only on synthetic data. We further demonstrate that ProxyPose extends to face tracking, camera pose estimation, and challenging in-the-wild scenes that are beyond the reach of existing approaches. Project page: https://ruihangzhang97.github.io/proxypose/.

</details>


### [97] [Vision as Unified Multimodal Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06560)
*Xiaoyang Han,Jianhua Li,Kewang Deng,Zukai Chen,Xuanke Shi,Sihan Wang,Boxuan Li,Linyan Wang,Siyi Xie,Xin You,Jinsheng Quan,Zhongang Cai,Haiwen Diao,Ziwei Liu,Lei Yang,Dahua Lin,Quan Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究将计算机视觉任务统一为多模态生成问题，通过自然语言指令和可选的视觉提示，使一个统一的多模态模型能够处理检测、OCR、分割、深度估计等多种视觉任务，输出文本、图像或混合形式的结果。通过构建大规模的视觉指令-响应语料库（SenseNova-Vision Corpus），在预训练模型基础上进行微调，无需任务特定结构即可实现广泛的任务覆盖，并在多个基准上达到与专用模型相当甚至更优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算机视觉系统通常针对特定任务设计，架构复杂且难以扩展。本文旨在通过统一的多模态生成框架，实现跨任务的通用性与可扩展性，降低模型设计复杂度，推动视觉能力融入通用基础模型。

Method: 将各类视觉任务转化为自然语言指令与对应输出（文本/图像/混合）的生成任务；构建包含多种目标类型的指令-响应数据集（SenseNova-Vision Corpus）；基于预训练的统一多模态模型，使用该语料库进行微调，并辅以其他多模态数据保持能力。

Result: 单一模型成功覆盖检测、OCR、关键点估计、分割、深度估计、表面法向预测、点图、相机位姿估计等任务，在结构化视觉理解、密集几何预测、分割和多视角几何任务中表现媲美甚至超越专门优化的系统。

Conclusion: 统一的多模态生成范式为整合多样化计算机视觉能力提供了一条可扩展路径，有助于将视觉理解能力高效集成到通用基础模型中，具有重要的应用前景。模型与数据集已公开。

Abstract: We formulate computer vision as unified multimodal generation, where heterogeneous visual tasks are expressed in the native text and image generation spaces of a unified multimodal model, without task-specific architectures. Under this formulation, SenseNova-Vision uses natural-language instructions and optional visual prompts to specify tasks, target regions or views, and decoding conventions, and generates responses as text for symbolic outputs, images for dense spatial predictions, or mixed text-and-image outputs for compositional tasks. To support large-scale training, we convert diverse computer vision annotations into instruction-response examples compatible with these generation spaces, resulting in the SenseNova-Vision Corpus, a computer-vision instruction-response corpus spanning text, image, and mixed targets. Starting from an off-the-shelf pretrained unified multimodal model, SenseNova-Vision is trained primarily on this corpus, with auxiliary multimodal data used as a capability-preserving mixture, and requires no task-specific prediction heads or architectural modifications. The resulting model covers a broad range of vision tasks, including detection, OCR, keypoint estimation, segmentation, depth estimation, surface normal prediction, point maps, and camera pose estimation, while supporting language-defined variants that combine category, color, region, and other visual cues. Experiments show that a single unified model can match leading task-specialized systems across structured visual understanding, dense geometric prediction, segmentation, and multi-view visual geometry. These results suggest unified multimodal generation as a scalable route for integrating computer vision capabilities into general-purpose foundation models. The model and corpus are publicly available.

</details>

### [98] [How Personas Can Influence Agents to Play Split or Steal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05398)
*Carlos Leon,Alexandre Rodrigues,Pedro Gamito,Thomas D. Parsons*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了角色设定（persona）提示在迭代分裂或窃取游戏中的影响，发现角色设定显著影响大语言模型代理在社会困境中的策略行为。在160次每轮15回合的实验中，约74%的回合为双方合作（Split），背叛（Steal）仅占不足11%。不同模型表现各异：phi4和Ministral 3:3b始终表现出高度合作性，而Gemma系列模型则策略更不稳定。基于五大性格特质分析，亲社会与原则型角色最稳定合作，分析型角色更倾向背叛。话题分析显示，友谊相关对话多伴随合作决策，金钱与复仇话题则多见于背叛行为；情感标签以中性或积极为主，解释力有限。研究为未来结合虚拟现实的人类-虚拟人类互动实验提供了基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究角色设定提示在社会困境情境中对大语言模型代理战略行为的影响，尤其是其在重复信任博弈中的有效性与一致性。

Method: 在迭代分裂或窃取游戏中，使用四个开源大模型（Ministral 3:3b, phi4:14b, Gemma3:12b, Gemma4:e4b）在两种温度设置（0.3 和 0.7）及零温度下的确定性决策条件下，与由GPT-4.1 mini控制的虚拟人类（VH）进行交互。共进行160次实验，每次15轮，使用欧洲葡萄牙语。通过行为频率、人格特质映射、话题分析与情感分析评估角色设定与模型差异的影响。

Result: 多数回合（约74%）为双方合作，背叛率低于11%。phi4与Ministral 3:3b在不同温度下均保持高合作性，Gemma系列模型策略波动较大。亲社会与原则型角色最稳定合作，分析型角色更倾向于背叛。友谊相关话题与合作行为相关，金钱与复仇话题则与背叛行为相关。情感分析显示情绪以中性或积极为主，但对行为解释力有限。

Conclusion: 角色设定提示能有效引导大语言模型在重复信任博弈中的合作行为，但其效果受模型本身特性影响显著。不同模型对同一角色设定反应不一，需谨慎选择模型与角色组合。研究结果为未来虚拟现实环境中人机互动实验提供了可靠的行为基准。

Abstract: Personas are often employed to guide large language model agents, yet their effectiveness in shaping strategic behavior in social dilemma settings remains uncertain. To address this, we examined the impact of persona prompts in an iterated Split or Steal game where persona-driven agents interacted with a Virtual Human (VH) controlled by a fixed prompt. Agents were instantiated from four open models (Ministral 3:3b, phi4:14b, Gemma3:12b, and Gemma4:e4b) at two temperature settings (0.3 and 0.7) and deterministic decision with zero temperature, while the VH was powered by GPT 4.1 mini. Across 160 sessions of 15 rounds each conducted in European Portuguese, mutual Split outcomes dominated (roughly 74 percent of rounds), with exploitation occurring in fewer than 11 percent of rounds. Model choice significantly influenced behavior: phi4 and Ministral 3:3b remained consistently cooperative across temperatures, whereas Gemma3:12b and Gemma4:e4b exhibited more varied strategies and outcomes. Analyses based on Big Five personality traits indicated that Prosocial and Principled personas were most consistently cooperative, while Analytical personas were more likely to exploit the VH. Topic analysis revealed that friendship-related dialogue aligns with Split decisions, whereas money and vengeance-related content is more prevalent in Steal outcomes; sentiment labels were predominantly neutral or happy and provided limited additional explanatory value. These findings characterize the interaction between persona prompts and model differences in repeated trust games and serve as a baseline for planned virtual reality studies involving human participants interacting with an embodied VH.

</details>


### [99] [Benchmarking KV-Cache Optimizations across Task Quality and System Performance for Long-Context Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05399)
*Nikita Agrawal,Ruben Mayer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个面向工作负载的基准测试，评估多种KV-cache优化技术（如KIVI、TurboQuant、SnapKV、CaM）在不同模型和任务下的表现，涵盖长文本问答、单文档问答、少样本学习和摘要等场景。结果表明压缩比不能单独作为性能预测指标，KIVI4在质量稳定性上表现最佳，SnapKV在长上下文吞吐量上最强，CaM在特定问答任务中提升显著但对工作负载敏感。研究强调应根据具体应用场景选择合适的压缩机制，而非采用统一方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV-cache压缩技术缺乏统一的比较基准，因评估环境（模型、任务、预算、服务栈）各异，难以客观衡量其实际效果。为解决此问题，需建立一个标准化的评估框架，以指导长期上下文推理系统的部署决策。

Method: 构建基于LongBench风格的多任务基准测试，涵盖多文档问答、单文档问答、少样本学习与摘要任务；使用Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct和Mistral-7B-Instruct-v0.3模型，在不同上下文长度区间内评估多种压缩方法（量化、剪枝、合并），并测量任务质量、平均输出吞吐率、首次生成时间及实际压缩比。

Result: 压缩比并非端到端性能的可靠指标；KIVI4在跨模型任务中表现出最稳定的输出质量；SnapKV在长上下文场景下实现最高吞吐量；CaM在部分问答任务中带来显著收益，但其性能受工作负载影响大，压缩比与质量波动明显。

Conclusion: 应根据具体应用场景选择适合的KV-cache优化机制，避免‘一刀切’的压缩策略。该研究为长上下文服务系统提供了可操作的部署建议。

Abstract: Large language model serving is increasingly limited by KV-cache growth under long-context workloads, yet existing KV-cache compression techniques are difficult to compare because they were evaluated on different models, tasks, budgets, and serving stacks. This paper presents a workload-aware benchmark of representative KV-cache optimization mechanisms spanning quantization, pruning, and merging, including KIVI, TurboQuant, SnapKV, and CaM, evaluated on LongBench-style multi-document QA, single-document QA, few-shot learning, and summarization workloads using Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct and Mistral-7B-Instruct-v0.3. The benchmark measures task quality, mean output throughput, mean time-to-first-token, and realized compression ratio across context-length buckets. The results show that the compression ratio alone is a poor predictor of end-to-end performance. KIVI4 provides the most stable quality across models, SnapKV delivers the strongest long-context throughput, and CaM yields large gains on selected QA workloads but exhibits substantial workload sensitivity in both quality and realized compression ratio. These findings motivate workload-aware selection of KV-cache mechanisms rather than one-size-fits-all compression and provide deployment guidance for long-context serving systems.

</details>


### [100] [Text Distance from Nested and Hierarchical Repetitions: A Compression-Based Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05416)
*Xiaojun Hu,Jing Wang,Jingwen Zhang,Fengyao Zhai,Xiao Xie,Hao Liao,Zengru Di,Yu Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出基于算法信息论（AIT）的Ladderpath方法，用于提取语言序列中嵌套和层次化的重复子结构，通过三种距离度量（归一化压缩距离NCD及两种直接来自Ladderpath表示的距离）实现强且一致的文本分类性能，尤其在分布外（OOD）和少样本场景下优于gzip-NCD和BERT。结果表明Ladderpath捕捉的结构化表示能保留序列内在特性，提供轻量、可解释、无需训练的文本建模替代方案，凸显了基于AIT的方法在结构化与领域无关序列理解中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本建模方法在分布外和低资源场景下表现不佳，且常依赖大量训练数据或缺乏可解释性。本文旨在探索一种不依赖训练、基于算法信息论的结构化序列分析方法，以实现更通用、可解释且高效的文本理解。

Method: 提出Ladderpath方法，利用算法信息论思想，从语言序列中提取嵌套和层次化的重复子结构；基于该表示构建三种距离度量：归一化压缩距离（NCD）以及两种源自Ladderpath的新型距离；结合k近邻分类器进行文本分类。

Result: 所提方法在多种任务（包括分布内、分布外、少样本）中表现优异，显著优于gzip-based NCD和BERT模型，尤其在分布外和低资源设置下优势明显。结构化表示具有良好的泛化能力与可解释性，且无需训练。

Conclusion: Ladderpath方法成功将算法信息论应用于序列分析，其生成的结构化表示能够有效捕捉序列的本质特征，为无监督、轻量级、可解释的文本建模提供了新范式，展示了基于AIT方法在通用序列理解中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: We present a new method for structural sequence analysis grounded in Algorithmic Information Theory (AIT). At its core is the Ladderpath approach, which extracts nested and hierarchical relationships among repeated substructures in linguistic sequences -- an instantiation of AIT's principle of describing data through minimal generative programs. These structures are then used to define three distance measures: a normalized compression distance (NCD), and two alternative distances derived directly from the Ladderpath representation. Integrated with a $k$-nearest neighbor classifier, these distances achieve strong and consistent performance across in-distribution, out-of-distribution (OOD), and few-shot text classification tasks. In particular, all three methods outperform both gzip-based NCD and BERT under OOD and low-resource settings. These results demonstrate that the structured representations captured by Ladderpath preserve intrinsic properties of sequences and provide a lightweight, interpretable, and training-free alternative for text modeling. This work highlights the potential of AIT-based approaches for structural and domain-agnostic sequence understanding.

</details>


### [101] [Most LLM Conformity Needs No Speaker: Measuring the Speaker-Free Floor in Peer-Pressure Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05545)
*Yibo Hu,Jiaming Qu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大语言模型在回答问题时看似服从群体意见的现象，实际上很大程度上源于重复错误答案本身的影响，而非真正来自其他说话者的社会影响。通过引入‘无来源’条件（即移除说话者信息但保留错误答案），发现即使没有说话者，仍有66.5%的正确答案被错误修改，远高于仅重新提问时的10.3%。这一现象在不同模型和数据集上普遍存在，且在答案改写或隐藏选项的情况下依然存在。研究强调，现有基准测试因未分离“说话者”与“重复答案”两个变量，导致误判社会影响程度。因此，应先测量去除说话者后仍存在的修正基线，再评估源属性带来的额外影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型的‘从众’行为研究依赖于包含说话者和重复错误答案的混合提示，但无法区分是社会影响还是重复内容本身导致答案变化。这种混淆可能使研究误判模型的真实从众机制。因此需要明确区分这两种因素，以更准确地评估模型的社会认知特性。

Method: 设计并实施‘无来源’条件实验：在保持错误答案重复的前提下，移除说话者身份信息，对比模型在有无说话者情况下的回答变化。使用六种开源大语言模型，在七个问答与推理数据集上进行测试，并考察答案改写、选项隐藏等变体情形。同时引入不同来源框架（如专家小组、最小人称标签）以分析其调节作用。

Result: 在无来源条件下，66.5%的原本正确的答案被错误修改，显著高于单纯重问时的10.3%。该效应在不同模型、数据集及开放回答设置下均成立。即使答案被改写或选项隐藏，该现象依然存在。专家小组框架会进一步提升错误修正率，而简单的人称标签则无明显效果。模型一旦翻转，通常表现出高度自信的错误答案，且简单的校准无法恢复原始正确答案。

Conclusion: 大语言模型中的多数所谓‘从众’行为并非由社会影响驱动，而是由重复错误答案本身引起的认知偏差。因此，评估模型的社会影响必须先扣除‘无来源’条件下的基线误差，否则将高估社会影响的作用。未来基准测试应优先测量去除说话者后的残留效应，以获得更真实、可比的评估结果。

Abstract: LLM conformity is often used to describe cases where a model changes a correct answer toward a peer or group response. We show that most of this apparent conformity survives even after the peer is removed. The reason is a confound: standard conformity prompts mix two cues at once, the presence of a speaker and the repeated wrong answer itself. Existing benchmarks vary these cues together, so they cannot tell how much of the revision actually depends on the speaker. We introduce a no-source condition: the same asserted answer with the explicit speaker removed. Across six open-weight LLMs and seven QA and reasoning datasets, this condition alone causes harmful revision in $66.5\%$ of initially correct cases, compared with $10.3\%$ under a plain re-ask. The effect also remains when the repeated answer is paraphrased and when answer options are hidden in an open-ended setting. Source framing mainly modulates this floor: expert-panel framing raises it, while minimal person labels do not reliably raise it. When models flip, they are usually confidently wrong, and simple recalibration does not recover the original answer. Source attribution still matters, but it should be measured as an increment above this speaker-free floor. The methodological lesson is that conformity benchmarks should first measure what remains after the speaker is removed; without this step, benchmarks may mistake repeated text for social influence.

</details>


### [102] [The yes-no bias of large language models reflects answer order and wording, not shifts in moral judgment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05552)
*Haonan Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过交叉对称化实验设计，分离语言模型在道德困境判断中由格式引发的非逻辑偏差。发现前沿大模型（如Claude）存在显著的“顺序偏见”和“词汇偏向”，尤其“no”词的出现导致更强的否定倾向，但这种偏差可通过替换关键词消除，表明模型并非真正排斥，而是受表面文本影响。小模型则表现出特定于自身的偏差模式。研究提出一个最小模型 $P = \sigma((\theta\pm m)/s)$ 来量化框架敏感性 $m$ 与道德决断力 $s$，并证明其与采样温度无关。结论强调：评估模型价值观必须跨框架提问，而非单一问法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明，大语言模型在道德判断中会因问题表述的微小变化而改变答案，尤其在二元选择题中出现‘是/否’偏差，这在人类中并不明显。然而，传统单次提问无法区分这种偏差是由逻辑、词汇还是呈现顺序引起的，因此亟需一种能分离这些因素的心理测量方法。

Method: 引入交叉对称化心理测量工具：将所有逻辑上等价的问题形式以平衡方式成对反转（如正反向表述），构建语料库；通过评分系统获取模型在不同形式下的连续评价，从而恢复内在道德尺度；再通过更换关键词为任意标签来解耦词汇与答案的关系，识别出顺序、词汇、语义等独立影响因素。

Result: 前沿模型（如Claude）的道德立场 $\theta$ 几乎不受格式影响（跨形式不一致性仅0.12-0.21），但其二元输出附带显著人工效应：顺序偏见（最后打印选项更易被选）和词汇偏见（'no'更常被选）。此现象在Claude中尤为严重（-0.32至-0.86），而GPT-5.5和Gemini几乎无影响，且随推理延长减弱。当关键词被替换后，原始回答偏差消失，说明模型不排斥‘否’本身，而是受文字表面影响。

Conclusion: 要准确衡量模型的价值观，必须通过跨框架提问，避免单一格式带来的认知污染。模型的‘拒绝倾向’实为表层文本驱动的人工产物，而非深层信念。研究提供了一套通用工具，可用于任何道德困境集和二元问答场景。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly issue judgments read as binary verdicts, and a growing literature reports such judgments shifting under logically irrelevant changes of wording - among them an amplified yes-no bias on moral dilemmas, absent in humans. A single framing cannot say what such a shift is: in a yes/no question the word "no" is at once logical verdict, lexical token, and last-printed option. We introduce a psychometric battery that separates these: crossed symmetrization - every logically irrelevant factor flipped in balanced pairs - across a corpus of question forms. A graded rating across logically equivalent forms recovers a coherent internal moral scale: frontier models' stance $θ$ is nearly format-invariant (cross-form incoherence 0.12-0.21 on a $\pm 1$ axis); small open-weight models fail in model-specific ways. Forcing the verdict through yes/no overlays a decomposable artifact: an order bias toward the last-printed option - opposite to classic human primacy - plus a lexical pull toward the word "no"; the artifact is substantial only in the Claude models (story-averaged -0.32 to -0.86), $\approx 0$ for GPT-5.5 and Gemini, and shrinks under extended reasoning. The word and the verdict share one token; swapping the words for arbitrary labels separates them, and the verdict-attached logical bias proves $\approx 0$ for every frontier model, while model-specific label and order attachments remain: the models are not drawn toward rejecting - the pull follows the printed surface, not the verdict it carries. A minimal model, $P = σ((θ\pm m)/s)$, summarizes any such artifact by a framing susceptibility m and a moral decisiveness s, measurably distinct from sampling temperature. The battery applies unchanged to any dilemma set and binary format: measuring what a model values requires crossing the frames of the question, not asking once.

</details>


### [103] [Prompt Robustness Is Task-Dependent: Comparing Objective and Belief-Style Questions in LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05554)
*Sadia Kamal,Arefa Patwary,Anthony Marchiafava,Atriya Sen,Sagnik Ray Choudhury*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型在客观问题与主观问题上的提示鲁棒性差异，发现模型对提示变化的响应受问题类型、提示修改方式和模型本身的影响，表明将模型回答视为其价值观或信念的证据存在脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对大语言模型的评估常将提示后的回答视为模型价值或信念的体现，但这一假设在涉及政治立场、社会态度等主观问题时尤为脆弱，因此需要考察不同问题类型下提示的鲁棒性差异。

Method: 通过在四个指令微调模型家族上测试三个客观数据集（MMLU、ARC、CulturalBench）和三个主观数据集（Political Compass Test、ValueBench、World Values Survey），对每个问题/陈述应用多种提示修改（如措辞、框架、格式变化），并使用二项广义估计方程分析答案一致性。

Result: 结果显示模型、数据集、提示类别及其交互作用均具有显著影响，且数据集类型与提示类别的交互效应较大，说明提示鲁棒性依赖于问题类型、提示变化方式及具体模型。

Conclusion: 提示鲁棒性并非普遍一致，其表现因问题类型、提示修改方式和模型而异，因此不应简单将模型回答视为其内在价值观或信念的可靠指标。

Abstract: Survey-style evaluations of large language models often treat a prompted response as a measure of a model's values or beliefs. This assumption is particularly fragile when responses are read as evidence of political values, social attitudes, or beliefs. We ask whether prompt robustness differs between objective questions with fixed answers and subjective questions that ask for opinions or values. We evaluate four instruction-tuned model families on three objective datasets (MMLU, ARC, and CulturalBench) and three subjective datasets (Political Compass Test, ValueBench, and World Values Survey). For each question/statement, we apply multiple types of prompt changes, such as variations in wording, framing, and format, and measure whether the model gives the same answer across variants. Using a binomial generalized estimating equation, we find significant effects of model, dataset, prompt category, and their interactions. The dataset type effect is also significant, and the interaction between dataset type and prompt category is large. These results show that prompt robustness depends on the question type, the prompt change, and the model.

### [104] [ResonatorLM: Causal Resonant Field Mixing for Efficient Long-Context Language Modelin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05583)
*Archie Chaudhury*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ResonatorLM introduces a physics-inspired alternative to self-attention in transformers, using damped resonators to model long sequences more efficiently. It achieves significant speedups in training, prefill, and decode phases, with improved accuracy on long-context tasks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformers and traditional models like RNNs and CNNs struggle with efficiency when handling long contexts, prompting the need for a new mechanism that maintains performance while improving scalability.

Method: ResonatorLM replaces self-attention dot products with causal functions based on damped resonators, treating token sequences as a one-dimensional latent field. It is implemented within a standard network architecture and evaluated on long-context modeling tasks.

Result: In a 6M parameter setting, ResonatorLM shows increasing training and prefill speedups with sequence length, achieves 6.47x faster decode speed than optimized transformers at 32K tokens, and improves accuracy to 61.31% on WikiText (vs. 55.32% for standard transformers).

Conclusion: ResonatorLM offers a promising alternative to attention mechanisms, enabling efficient and accurate long-context modeling through physics-based computation, with substantial performance gains in speed and accuracy.

Abstract: Contemporary language models are dominated by the transformer architecture, which leverages self-attention mechanisms to enable more efficient, parallelized training across a wide set of documents and corpora. This has allowed transformers to effectively model data across a wide range of modalities and contexts. However, transformers, along with their conventional counterparts such as recurrent neural networks (RNNs) and convolutional neural networks (CNNs), often struggle to maintain efficiency when processing long contexts. We introduce ResonatorLM, a new mechanism that replaces attention with a physics-derived alternative. ResonatorLM treats token sequences as a single, driven one-dimensional latent field and replaces attention dot products with causal functions of damped resonators. We implement ResonatorLM on a traditional network architecture and test it on standard long-context modeling tasks. We find that in a small, 6M matched setting, training and prefill speedups increase with sequence length, decode speed reaches 6.47x compared to that of a standard, optimized transformer at 32K tokens, and accuracy reaches 61.31 percent (compared to 55.32 percent) on WikiText.

### [105] [Revisiting the Relation Between Language Model Perplexity and ASR Word Error Rate for Modern End-to-End Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05612)
*Mohammad Zeineldeen,Albert Zeyer,Haoran Zhang,Robin Schmitt,Ralf Schlüter,Hermann Ney*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了现代端到端自动语音识别（ASR）系统中语言模型困惑度（PPL）与词错误率（WER）之间的关系。研究发现，外部语言模型对当前ASR系统的提升有限，且PPL与WER在对数空间中的线性关系已不再成立。此外，编码器上下文长度和内部语言建模（ILM）的影响显著，尤其当扣除解码器内部语言模型后，PPL-WER关系发生明显变化。大语言模型（LLM）的困惑度并不符合传统神经语言模型的趋势，表明需重新评估外部语言模型在现代ASR中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，语言模型困惑度（PPL）被用作自动语音识别（ASR）词错误率（WER）的代理指标，且二者在对数空间中呈近似线性关系。然而，现代端到端ASR系统具备内置语言建模能力，常不依赖外部语言模型，并可结合神经语言模型和大语言模型（LLMs）。因此，有必要重新评估PPL与WER的关系是否仍成立，以及外部语言模型的实际贡献。

Method: 通过实验分析不同编码器上下文长度、外部语言模型引入与否、内部语言建模（ILM）的影响，以及大语言模型（LLM）的困惑度表现，系统地考察现代端到端ASR系统中PPL与WER的关系。采用消融实验分离内部语言模型成分，以评估其对整体性能评价的影响。

Result: 1. 外部语言模型对现代端到端ASR系统的性能提升有限；2. PPL与WER在对数空间中的线性关系不再成立；3. 编码器上下文长度影响该关系的稳定性；4. 内部语言建模（ILM）是关键因素，扣除后PPL-WER关系显著改变；5. 大语言模型（LLM）的困惑度偏离传统趋势，无法直接用于预测ASR性能。

Conclusion: 在现代端到端ASR系统中，不能简单依赖语言模型困惑度（PPL）作为词错误率（WER）的代理指标。内部语言建模能力必须被考虑，外部语言模型的作用受限，且大语言模型的困惑度不适用于传统评估框架。未来评估应更关注系统内部语言建模机制与外部模型协同方式。

Abstract: Language model (LM) perplexity (PPL) has historically been used as a proxy for automatic speech recognition (ASR) word error rate (WER), with prior work reporting an approximately linear relation in log-log space. Modern end-to-end ASR systems challenge this assumption because they already contain internal language modeling capacity, are often evaluated without external language models, and can now be combined with neural LMs and large language models (LLMs) through different recognition strategies. This paper revisits the relation between PPL and WER for modern ASR systems. We study whether external LMs still improve current end-to-end ASR systems, whether the PPL-WER relation remains linear in log-log space, how encoder context length affects this relation, and how LLM perplexities fit into the trend observed for standard neural LMs. We further investigate internal language modeling (ILM) in attention-based encoder-decoder systems and show that ILM subtraction changes the observed PPL-WER relation, indicating that the decoder's internal LM must be considered when interpreting the effect of external LM quality.

To accurately capture the structural and contextual complexity of these forms, we define a fine-grained annotation schema comprising 26 types of form entities, along with a separate coarse form entity set consisting of 5 types. We evaluate the latest MLLMs from the ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude, Qwen, and Kimi series using zero-shot and chain-of-thought prompts under both low and high reasoning setups. Our results reveal limitations in current MLLMs' ability in comprehending Bangla forms, particularly in accurately localizing highly granular form entities. Our dataset and code is available at: https://huggingface.co/datasets/Mausul/bafco

### [108] [Population-Level Profiling of DSM-5 Depressive Symptoms Among Self-Reported ADHD and ASD Users on Twitter: An Exploratory Study Using Advanced NLP and Statistical Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05626)
*Muhammad Rizwan,David Nabergoj,Jure Demšar*

TL;DR: 本研究分析了社交媒体上自报患有ADHD和ASD的用户在推文中表达DSM-5抑郁症状的差异，发现两组在认知问题、睡眠障碍、食欲变化和疲劳方面更倾向ADHD，在自杀意念和快感缺失方面更倾向ASD。尽管分类性能中等但稳定，且症状共现结构基本一致，未发现显著的疾病特异性差异，结果具有可重复性但不具临床有效性，结论为探索性，不能推断个体层面的症候学差异。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Background: Depression frequently co-occurs with ADHD and autism spectrum disorder (ASD), but population-level differences in symptom expression between these groups remain underexplored. Objective: We examined whether social media users with ADHD and ASD differ in how they express DSM-5 depressive symptoms in their tweets, and whether differences persist across varying levels of depressive-content filtering. Methods: We analysed 1,282,437 tweets from 792 users (622 ADHD; 170 ASD) with self-reported diagnoses on Twitter. We applied L1-penalised logistic regression with cross-validation to distinguish ADHD from ASD users, complemented by Pearson correlations for symptom co-occurrence, and tested robustness across five filtering thresholds using bootstrapping. Results: MentalRoBERTa achieved macro-F1 of 0.901 on a held-out set, outperforming the original ReDSM5 benchmark. ADHD vs ASD classification yielded stable but modest performance (cross-validated ROC-AUC 0.645-0.653). Cognitive issues, sleep issues, appetite change, and fatigue leaned toward ADHD, while suicidal ideation and anhedonia leaned toward ASD. A largely shared symptom co-occurrence structure emerged between groups; no pair met our criterion for a robust disorder-specific difference. Conclusions: Population-level differences in depression-related language between ADHD and ASD social media users were consistently observed across thresholds, reflecting reproducibility rather than clinical validity. Findings are exploratory and do not establish differing phenomenology at the individual level.

### [109] [Do It Right! A Methodology for Successful NLP System Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05644)
*Olga V. Patterson,Brett South,T. Elizabeth Workman,Scott L DuVall*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于系统开发生命周期（SDLC）的逐步方法，用于依赖语言处理进行数据提取的自然语言处理（NLP）项目，强调算法知识之外的其他关键要素对NLP项目成功的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有大量教材和教程介绍了文本处理的具体算法和应用，但算法知识只是成功实施NLP项目的一个方面，实际项目中还需考虑流程管理、需求分析、系统设计等系统性因素。

Method: 基于现有文献，采用系统开发生命周期（SDLC）框架，将NLP项目分解为多个阶段，包括需求分析、系统设计、开发、测试与部署，以确保项目有条不紊地推进。

Result: 该方法有助于提高临床研究和决策支持中从电子病历中提取信息的NLP项目的可重复性、可靠性和整体成功率。

Conclusion: 成功的NLP项目不仅依赖于先进的算法，更需要遵循系统化的开发流程，而SDLC提供了一个有效且可操作的框架来指导整个项目生命周期。

Abstract: Natural language processing (NLP) is a common method for supplying data to clinical research and decision making by extracting information from electronic medical records. Numerous textbooks and tutorials describe specific algorithms and applications for text processing, yet algorithmic knowledge is only one ingredient of a successful NLP project. ### [110] [RPAM: A Principled Metric for Evaluating Associations in Language Models with High Predictive Validity in Downstream Outputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05679)
*Damian Hodel,Jevin West,Aylin Caliskan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为相对概率关联度量（RPAM）的上游评估指标，用于衡量生成式语言模型中的关联性。该方法在不同质量与用途的语言模型（Mistral-7B-Instruct、Mistral-7B、GPT-2）上验证，发现其与人类隐含/显性关联以及下游偏差测量结果有强相关性，优于现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法多依赖下游生成文本指标，但因生成内容差异大而需专用数据集，缺乏通用性；而上游指标虽具普适性，却未有效捕捉真实世界关联关系。因此需要一种既通用又准确的上游评估方法。

Method: 引入相对概率关联度量（RPAM），基于嵌入或续写概率等基础层面分析语言模型中的关联性，实现跨模型的一致性评估。

Result: 在多个模型和数据集上，RPAM与人类认知及下游偏差测量高度相关，显著优于已有指标表现。

Conclusion: RPAM是一种有效的上游关联评估指标，能够可靠地揭示生成式语言模型中的偏见，并具备良好的泛化能力，为偏见分析与缓解提供了新工具。

Abstract: Language models (LMs) exhibit problematic biases, such as stereotypes. Effectively analyzing and mitigating such biases requires accurate and generalizable evaluation methods of the underlying associations. Some existing approaches focus on downstream metrics that analyze associations in generated text. Since generated text content can vary drastically across LMs, such metrics often require specialized evaluation datasets, which limits the generalization of such downstream metrics. In contrast, upstream metrics examine LMs at the fundamental level of embeddings or continuation probabilities, enabling principled association analyses across LMs. Yet, to date, no upstream metric for generative LMs has uncovered a strong relationship with real-world associations, including those measured in generated text. To address this gap, we introduce the Relative Probability Association Metric (RPAM), an association evaluation metric for generative LMs. For three LMs of different quality of language generation and purpose (Mistral-7B-Instruct, Mistral-7B, and GPT-2) and well-studied evaluation datasets (WEAT-WS, Bellezza, WS-353, and SST2), we find a strong relationship between upstream RPAM measurements and corresponding implicit and explicit associations observed in humans, as well as biases measured downstream with LM-specific tasks, outperforming prior record values where applicable.

Abstract: We present our systems for SemEval-2026 Task 10 (PsyCoMark), addressing conspiracy marker extraction (Subtask 1) and document-level conspiracy detection (Subtask 2). For marker extraction, we formulate the task as multi-label span classification over enumerated candidate spans, using IoU >= 0.95 positive labeling, hard-negative sampling, and containment-based non-maximum suppression (NMS) with boundary-aware span representations. Document classification is modeled independently using a sequence classifier with label smoothing and a stratified train-validation split. Analysis shows that entity-like roles (Actor, Victim) are detected robustly, while abstract roles (Action, Effect, Evidence) remain sensitive to boundary criteria. On the official test set, our systems rank 7th in Subtask 1 (0.2251 macro F1) and 11th in Subtask 2 (0.7694 weighted F1).

### [112] [Where to cut, how deep: BPE and Unigram-LM on chemistry SMILES](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05691)
*Hunter Heidenreich*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究对比了化学语言模型中常用的BPE与另一种替代方案Unigram-LM在小词汇量下的表现，发现两者生成的子词词汇几乎不重叠（交集Jaccard指数最高仅0.161），且Unigram-LM对分子的分词更细粒度，分割出更多token。这种差异在不同数据集、边界策略和词汇规模下均持续存在，表明子词算法选择是关键建模决策而非默认选项。研究未训练任何语言模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前化学语言模型普遍采用来自自然语言处理的字节对编码（BPE）作为SMILES字符串的分词方法，但缺乏对其适用性的深入评估；尽管在自然语言中，Unigram-LM已被证明能生成结构不同的词汇，但在化学领域这一差异是否成立尚不清楚。因此，本文旨在系统比较BPE与Unigram-LM在化学语料中的表现，揭示其对模型输入结构的根本影响。

Method: 在固定165个词元的基础词汇上，对三种不同类型的化学语料（多样、类药物、天然产物）分别采用两种预分词边界策略，在小词汇量条件下进行受控对比实验，评估BPE与Unigram-LM生成的子词词汇的重叠程度、分词粒度差异及稳定性。

Result: 在全部22组匹配条件下，两种算法构建的子词词汇近乎不重叠（交叉重合率<0.161，加权后最高仅0.05）；Unigram-LM比BPE多出29-41%的分词结果；多数分子的切分位置一致但深度不同，表明BPE是Unigram-LM的粗化版本；该差异在不同语料、边界策略和词汇规模下均稳定存在，甚至在八倍规模下仍显著。

Conclusion: 子词分词算法的选择在化学语言模型中并非可忽略的默认设置，而是一个具有深远影响的建模决策，应根据具体任务仔细评估。

Abstract: Every chemical language model reading SMILES begins with a tokenizer, yet the field has inherited byte-pair encoding (BPE) from natural language with little scrutiny. In natural language, BPE's principal alternative, Unigram-LM, is known to build structurally different vocabularies. Whether that contrast survives in chemistry was open. We report a controlled comparison of BPE and Unigram-LM over a fixed 165-token chemistry base, at the small vocabulary sizes where token embeddings are learnable, across three corpus typologies (diverse, drug-like, natural-products) and both pre-tokenization boundary policies. The two do not converge. In all 22 matched conditions they build near-disjoint subword vocabularies: cross-algorithm Jaccard overlap on the learned pieces never exceeds 0.161, and at most 0.05 once weighted toward the high-frequency pieces a model updates most. Unigram-LM also segments held-out molecules into 29-41% more tokens; the arms largely agree on where to cut but not how deeply, so BPE's segmentation is a strict coarsening of Unigram-LM's on 80-99% of molecules. The separation holds across corpus, boundary, and vocabulary size, persisting even at eight times that scale. The subword algorithm is therefore a modeling decision, not a free default. The study trains no language models.

### [113] [SpanUQ: Span-Level Uncertainty Quantification for Large Language Model Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05721)
*Yimeng Zhang,Yingying Zhuang,Ziyi Wang,Yuxuan Lu,Pei Chen,Aman Gupta,Zhe Su,Ming Tan,Zhilin Zhang,Qun Liu,Manikandarajan Ramanathan,Rajashekar Maragoud,Edward Vul,Jing Huang,Dakuo Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的细粒度不确定性估计任务——段落级不确定性估计（SLUE），旨在定位语义连贯的文本片段中的不确定性。为此，作者设计了SPANUQ，一种轻量级探针模型，通过单次前向传播从大型语言模型的隐藏状态中提取不确定性知识。该方法采用DETR风格的跨度解码器，结合贝塔分布混合模型进行不确定性估计，并使用贝塔NLL回归与对比排序目标联合训练。构建了首个段落级不确定性基准SPANUQ-BENCH，包含20K提示、293K标注段落和连续软标签。实验表明，SPANUQ在五个LLM上均显著优于现有基线和采样方法，且速度提升10-20倍，同时实现了0.910的F1分数，较最佳启发式方法提升39.4%，具备精准错误定位能力，具有跨模型家族的良好泛化性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有不确定性估计方法存在粒度不匹配问题：词元级评分缺乏语义一致性，序列级评分无法精确定位错误。为实现更自然、可解释的不确定性评估，需要在语义连贯的文本段落层面进行建模。

Method: 提出SPAUUQ模型，基于DETR架构的跨度解码器，利用混合贝塔分布对不确定性进行建模，通过联合优化贝塔负对数似然损失与对比排序损失来训练，实现高效且准确的段落级不确定性估计。

Result: SPANUQ在五个主流大模型上均取得最优的段落级不确定性表现，显著超越所有采样方法和探针基线，推理速度提升10-20倍；其跨度检测F1达0.910，较最佳启发式方法提高39.4%，有效支持错误精确定位。

Conclusion: 本文提出的SPANUQ框架成功定义并解决了段落级不确定性估计任务，提供了兼具准确性、效率与可解释性的新范式，为可信生成和自修正系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: Uncertainty estimation is essential not only for the trustworthy deployment of large language models (LLMs) but also as a foundation for self-refinement in LLM generation. However, existing approaches operate at suboptimal granularities: token-level scores lack semantic coherence, while sequence-level scores fail to localize errors. We formalize Span-Level Uncertainty Estimation (SLUE), a new task that targets the natural granularity for uncertainty: semantically coherent text spans, each conveying a single assessable unit of meaning. To address this task, we introduce SPANUQ, a lightweight probe that distills the uncertainty knowledge from expensive multi-sample inference into a single forward pass over LLM hidden states. SPANUQ employs a DETR-style span decoder to simultaneously detect spans and estimate their uncertainty via a Mixture of Beta distribution, trained with a principled combination of Beta NLL regression and contrastive ranking objectives. We construct SPANUQ-BENCH, the first span-level uncertainty benchmark comprising 20K prompts, 293K annotated spans, and continuous soft labels derived from multi-sample claim verification. Experiments on five LLM backbones show that SPANUQ consistently achieves the best span-level uncertainty quality, outperforming the strongest probe baseline and all sampling-based methods while being 10-20x faster. Its DETR-based span detector attains 0.910 F1, surpassing the best heuristic by 39.4%, enabling precise error localization that sequence-level methods cannot provide. The framework generalizes across five LLMs spanning two model families.

### [114] [Nemotron-Labs-Diffusion: A Tri-Mode Language Model Unifying Autoregressive, Diffusion, and Self-Speculation Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05722)

TL;DR: Nemotron-Labs-Diffusion 是一个统一自回归（AR）、扩散模型和自推测解码的三模式语言模型，通过联合训练实现模式切换，在不同部署场景下保持高吞吐。研究发现：1）AR与扩散目标互补，前者提供语言先验，后者增强前瞻规划；2）在自推测模式中，扩散生成草稿、AR验证，优于多标记预测方法，提升接受率与设备效率；3）速度分析显示，最优采样器下扩散可比自推测多输出76.5%的令牌。该模型系列（3B/8B/14B）在准确率与速度上均超越现有开源模型，如8B版本相比Qwen3-8B快6倍，吞吐提升4倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为解决传统自回归模型在长文本生成中的效率瓶颈，以及扩散模型在推理速度上的不足，提出一种融合多种解码机制的统一架构，以实现高效、灵活且高性能的生成能力。

Abstract: We introduce Nemotron-Labs-Diffusion, a tri-mode language model (LM) that unifies AR, diffusion, and self-speculation decoding within a single architecture. Trained with a joint AR-diffusion objective, Nemotron-Labs-Diffusion can switch modes to sustain high throughput across deployment settings and concurrency levels. Our study shows that (1) AR and diffusion objectives are complementary: diffusion improves lookahead planning, while AR provides left-to-right linguistic priors. (2) In self-speculation mode, diffusion drafts while AR verifies, outperforming multi-token prediction (MTP) methods in both acceptance rate and real-device efficiency. (3) A speed-of-light analysis further demonstrates diffusion's long-term potential, with up to 76.5% more tokens per forward pass than self-speculation under an optimal sampler. Scaling to 3B, 8B, and 14B parameters, our Nemotron-Labs-Diffusion family, including base, instruct, and vision-language models, consistently outperforms state-of-the-art open-source AR and diffusion LMs in both accuracy and speed. For example, Nemotron-Labs-Diffusion-8B decodes 6x more tokens per forward than Qwen3-8B with comparable accuracy, translating to 4x higher throughput on SPEED-Bench with SGLang on a GB200 GPU.

### [115] [When Should LLMs Search? Counterfactual Supervision for Search Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05752)
*Minho Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种实例级别的搜索路由问题，旨在判断在特定任务中是否需要外部搜索以提升表现。通过比较无搜索与强制搜索的结果，构建基于任务成功的“最优”决策（不搜索、搜索、未解决），并以此作为监督信号训练搜索路由策略。采用监督微调和偏好优化方法，显著提升了路由性能（如Gemma E2B的宏F1从0.7082提升至0.8235），且不同模型学习到不同的改进方向：Gemma主要学会避免不必要的搜索，而Qwen则更有效地识别应搜索的场景。剩余未解决案例揭示了模型能力、检索预算、证据利用及策略行为等多重瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有搜索增强型语言模型在使用外部证据时存在不均衡问题，例如对本可回答的问题仍调用搜索，或在应澄清、修正或放弃时依赖噪声证据。因此，亟需一种智能路由机制，在合适时机决定是否启用搜索，以提升整体任务成功率。

Method: 构建一个基于任务成功与否的“最优”路由标签（即oracle），通过对比同一问题在无搜索与强制搜索下的输出结果来生成；将此oracle作为监督信号，采用监督微调和偏好优化训练搜索路由策略。

Result: 在oracle可适用的样本上，搜索路由策略的宏观F1得分显著提升：Gemma E2B从0.7082升至0.8235，Qwen3.5-4B从0.7053升至0.8365。进一步分析表明，模型分别解决了自身特有的路由缺陷，但仍有部分未解决案例反映出多方面挑战，包括模型容量、检索资源、证据利用效率和策略本身局限。

Conclusion: 通过引入基于任务成功反馈的搜索路由机制，可以有效引导语言模型在适当情境下使用外部搜索，减少无效调用与错误依赖。该方法在多个主流模型上均取得显著性能提升，并揭示出当前系统中存在的多样化瓶颈，为后续优化提供方向。

Abstract: Search-augmented language models can use external evidence to compensate for limitations in parametric knowledge, but search is not uniformly beneficial: models may call search for questions they can already answer, or rely on noisy evidence when correction, clarification, or abstention would be more appropriate. We formulate this as an instance-level search-routing problem: deciding whether search is needed to improve task success relative to a no-search execution. To derive supervision, we compare no-search and forced-search outcomes for the same question and construct an oracle over NO SEARCH, SEARCH, and UNSOLVED based on task-specific success. Using this oracle as both an evaluation criterion and a learning signal, we train search-routing policies with supervised fine-tuning and preference optimization, improving routing macro-F1 on oracle-eligible examples from 0.7082 to 0.8235 for Gemma E2B and from 0.7053 to 0.8365 for Qwen3.5-4B. Further analysis shows that the learned policies reduce model-specific routing failures: Gemma primarily learns no-search restraint, while Qwen further reduces missed search; residual UNSOLVED cases reveal heterogeneous bottlenecks involving model capacity, retrieval budget, evidence use, and policy behavior.

### [116] [Inject or Navigate? Token-Efficient Retrieval for LLM Analysis of Transactional Legal Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05764)
*Mahmoud Hany,Mourad ElSheraey,Mahmoud Said,Peter Naoum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究如何在法律文档问答系统中替代将整个语料库注入大模型上下文的基线方法。通过对比基于结构化分块的两种检索模式（NAVEMBED和NAVINDEX），发现二者在保持高准确率的同时显著降低输入令牌数量和成本。其中，NAVINDEX在18个问题上与全量注入持平，仅需1.61倍的总令牌开销、约56倍更小的推理上下文，并节省25%的成本。研究还提出一个闭式缓存交叉规则：当语料规模低于检索负载的十倍时，缓存注入更经济。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全量语料注入虽能最大化召回率，但导致上下文长度随文档量增长，引发长上下文性能下降且成本高昂。亟需更高效、可扩展的检索方案以应对实际应用中的效率与成本挑战。

Method: 采用结构感知分块技术，构建两种检索路径：基于嵌入向量的检索（NAVEMBED）和利用大模型导航紧凑结构索引（NAVINDEX）。通过参考锚定的成对评估器进行人工判断，量化不同方法在准确性、上下文大小和成本方面的表现。

Result: 在20个问题的基准测试中，语义检索结合重排序在16/18个文档相关问题上与全量注入持平（仅2个偏好注入），输入令牌减少17.3倍；使用GTE配置可达29.9倍减少但匹配率下降。NAVINDEX在全部18个问题上表现相当，总令牌开销仅为1.61倍，推理上下文缩小56倍，成本降低25%。

Conclusion: 结构化检索方法（特别是NAVINDEX）可在保证答案质量的前提下大幅降低大模型在法律文档问答中的计算成本与上下文负担，是全量注入的有效替代方案。同时，提出的缓存交叉规则为系统设计提供了明确的决策依据。

Abstract: Answering questions over a set of transactional legal documents is most simply done by injecting the whole corpus into the LLM's context window on every query. That baseline maximises retrieval recall, but its token footprint scales with the corpus rather than the question, and long-context degradation scales with it. We report what it took to replace full-corpus injection in a legal-document analysis system, comparing it against two structured retrieval modes over our proprietary structure-aware chunking: embedding retrieval (NAVEMBED) and LLM navigation over a compact structured index (NAVINDEX). On a 20-question benchmark with verified ground-truth answers, a position-bias-controlled, reference-anchored pairwise judge scored semantic retrieval with reranking tied with injection on 16 of 18 document-bound questions (injection preferred on 2) while attending to 17.3x fewer input tokens (a general-text-embedding (GTE) configuration reaches 29.9x at a lower tie rate); both modes were judged tied on the 2 out-of-scope controls. NAVINDEX was judged tied on all 18 at a 1.61x smaller total token footprint, a ~56x smaller answering context, and 25% lower dollar cost. We derive a closed-form caching-crossover rule: cached injection is cheaper in dollars only while the corpus stays below roughly ten times the retrieval payload. Scope and uncertainty are quantified in Section 8.

</details>


### [117] [CoPiT: Cognitive Pivot Translation for Digraphic Low-Resource Mongolian in the Traditional Script](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05849)
*Burte Bayarsaikhan,Serynn Kim,Buru Chang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出CoPiT，一种基于认知动机的枢纽翻译管道，用于解决蒙古语在传统文字和西里尔文字之间数据不平衡问题。通过将翻译任务经由资源更丰富的西里尔文字进行路由，有效缓解了传统文字的拼写歧义问题，提升了翻译准确性和稳定性。实验表明，CoPiT在多种模型和目标语言上均优于直接翻译，显著提升BLEU分数并带来1.5-1.6倍的COMET增益，使开源模型性能达到甚至超过GPT-4.1水平。此外，该方法还能生成合成双语数据，缓解真实低资源场景下的数据稀缺问题。研究还发布了包含蒙语双文字与英、韩、俄语的多语言平行数据集，所有资源已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蒙古语作为双文字语言，其传统文字数据极度匮乏且拼写模糊，导致直接翻译性能严重下降；而西里尔文字资源相对丰富，因此需要利用这种内部资源层级关系来提升翻译质量。

Method: 提出CoPiT，一个基于认知动机的枢纽翻译管道，通过将传统文字文本先映射到西里尔文字，再进行翻译，从而显式消除传统文字带来的歧义，实现更稳定准确的意义传递。同时利用该机制生成合成平行数据以缓解数据稀缺问题。

Result: CoPiT在多个骨干模型和目标语言上持续优于直接翻译，实现显著的绝对BLEU提升，并带来1.5-1.6倍的COMET增益；开源模型在同等评估条件下可媲美或超越GPT-4.1；同时支持从传统文字文本构建合成平行数据，有效应对低资源挑战。

Conclusion: CoPiT通过利用双文字语言中的资源层次结构，有效解决了蒙古语传统文字数据稀缺与拼写歧义问题，不仅提升了翻译性能，还为低资源语言的数据增强提供了新路径。研究成果已通过公开数据集和代码实现共享。

Abstract: Low-resource languages remain challenging for machine translation, and Mongolian is a representative case. As a digraphic language, Mongolian is written in both Cyrillic and Traditional scripts, which exhibit a severe imbalance in data availability. While the Cyrillic script is relatively well-resourced, the Traditional script remains extremely data-scarce and orthographically ambiguous, leading to substantial performance degradation in direct translation. We propose CoPiT, a cognitively motivated pivot-based translation pipeline that exploits this internal resource hierarchy by routing translation through the Cyrillic script. The pipeline explicitly resolves script-induced ambiguity in the Traditional script before translation, enabling more stable and accurate meaning transfer. Across multiple backbone models and target languages, CoPiT consistently outperforms direct translation, achieving substantial absolute BLEU improvements together with consistent 1.5-1.6x COMET gains. These gains allow strong open-source models to match or outperform GPT-4.1 under comparable evaluation settings. Beyond inference-time improvements, CoPiT enables the construction of synthetic parallel data directly from Traditional-script text, mitigating data scarcity in realistic low-resource scenarios. We release a new multi-script parallel dataset covering Mongolian in both scripts alongside English, Korean, and Russian. All datasets and code are publicly available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/anonymous_project-76C7.

### [118] [Mitigating Factual Hallucination in Large Reasoning Models via Mixed-Mode Advantage Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05861)
*Kaishen Wang,Tong Zheng,Xuehao Cui,Ruibo Chen,Tianyi Xiong,Heng Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为MARGO的强化学习框架，用于在事实性问答中抑制由显式思维引发的幻觉问题。研究表明，尽管显式思维通常能提升答案质量，但有时会破坏原本正确的直接回答，导致事实性偏差。为此，作者将显式思维建模为对模型直接回答倾向的残差，通过混合模式滚动（包含思考与非思考轨迹）来评估思维是否真正增加了事实价值。MARGO利用非思考路径作为参考，仅保留有益的思维行为，同时抑制幻觉倾向。实验表明，MARGO在多个事实性问答基准上显著提升了事实可靠性，且在数学推理任务中保持了良好的通用推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在事实性问答中，虽然显式思维有助于恢复知识和优化答案，但存在一种反直觉现象：显式思维可能推翻原本正确的非思考答案，导致事实性错误，即‘思维诱发幻觉’。这种失败模式限制了大型推理模型的实际应用效果，亟需机制来识别并抑制有害的思维行为。

Method: 将显式思维形式化为相对于模型直接回答倾向的思维残差；提出MARGO框架，采用混合模式滚动组（包含思考与非思考轨迹），以同模型的非思考路径作为优势估计的参考，从而判断显式思维是否带来额外的事实价值。通过强化学习策略优化，只保留有益思维，抑制幻觉倾向。

Result: 在多个事实性问答数据集上，MARGO显著优于现有强基线模型，在保持高准确率的同时大幅提升了事实可靠性；在数学推理任务上，其推理能力未下降，证明该方法有效平衡了事实性和通用推理能力。

Conclusion: MARGO通过引入非思考路径作为参考，实现对显式思维的精准评估，有效抑制了思维诱发的幻觉问题，同时保留有益推理行为。该方法为提升大型推理模型在真实场景中的可信度提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) improve language model capabilities by generating explicit thinking traces before final answers. In factuality-oriented question answering (QA), such thinking often improves overall performance by helping the model recover relevant knowledge and refine its answers. However, we find that this benefit is not uniform at the instance level: explicit thinking can also overturn correct non-thinking answers and lead to factual drift. We refer to this failure mode as \emph{thinking-induced hallucination}. To explain this phenomenon, we formulate explicit thinking in factuality QA as a thinking residual over the model's direct-answer tendency, which can either recover missing knowledge or introduce unsupported associations. Based on this formulation, we propose MARGO, \underline{\textit{M}}ixed-Mode \underline{\textit{A}}dvantage \underline{\textit{R}}egularization for \underline{\textit{G}}rounded \underline{\textit{O}}ptimization, a reinforcement learning framework that uses non-thinking rollouts as same-model references in advantage estimation. By constructing mixed-mode rollout groups with both thinking and non-thinking trajectories, MARGO evaluates whether explicit thinking adds factual value beyond direct answering, thereby suppressing hallucination-prone thinking while preserving beneficial thinking behaviors. Experiments across multiple factuality-oriented QA benchmarks demonstrate that MARGO improves factual reliability over strong baselines, while evaluations on mathematical benchmarks show that it preserves general reasoning ability.

### [119] [Is Domain Adaptation Always Helpful? A Frozen-Backbone Study of Cross-Domain Sentiment Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05937)
*Phat Tran,Artin Lahni,Pranav Kulkarni,Yaolun Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究评估了在冻结预训练语言模型（PLM）主干上进行显式领域适应的有效性，使用Qwen3-Embedding系列、RoBERTa-base和FinBERT作为主干，结合DANN、MMD和SCL方法训练轻量级MLP适配器，在消费者评论数据上进行训练，并在电影评论（SST-2）和金融新闻子集（Financial PhraseBank）上测试迁移性能。结果发现：在SST-2上，领域适应几乎无增益；而在金融子集上，小规模通用主干通过领域适应显著提升性能。值得注意的是，对抗性对齐（DANN）会损害领域专用主干（如FinBERT）的性能，而监督对比损失则能更好保留其领域结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前情感分析中广泛采用冻结预训练语言模型主干，但显式领域适应的实际效益尚不明确，尤其当主干模型具备不同程度的目标领域知识时。本文旨在探究领域适应在不同主干模型上的有效性差异，揭示其与主干是否已包含目标领域知识之间的关系。

Method: 采用一系列冻结嵌入主干（Qwen3-Embedding 0.6B/4B/8B、RoBERTa-base、FinBERT），在消费者评论数据上训练轻量级MLP适配器，使用三种领域适应方法：域对抗神经网络（DANN）、最大均值差异（MMD）和监督对比学习（SCL）。在电影评论（SST-2）和受限金融新闻数据集（Financial PhraseBank）上评估迁移性能，分析不同主干与方法组合的表现差异。

Result: 在SST-2任务上，无论主干规模如何，领域适应带来的性能提升可忽略；在金融新闻子集上，小规模通用主干通过领域适应显著恢复性能；对抗性对齐（DANN）导致领域专用主干（如FinBERT）性能下降，可能因破坏已有领域结构；而监督对比损失则有助于保持领域特定特征。

Conclusion: 显式领域适应的有效性高度依赖于冻结主干是否已具备目标领域知识。对于缺乏领域覆盖的小型通用模型，领域适应可带来显著收益；而对于已具备领域专长的模型，不当的适应方法反而会损害性能。因此，应根据主干模型的领域匹配程度选择合适的适应策略。

Abstract: Sentiment analysis with frozen pre-trained language model (PLM) backbones has become a common paradigm, yet the practical benefit of explicit domain adaptation remains unclear, particularly when backbones encode varying degrees of target-domain knowledge. We present a preliminary case study evaluating a controlled family of frozen embedding backbones (Qwen3-Embedding 0.6B, 4B, 8B), alongside RoBERTa-base and FinBERT. We train a lightweight MLP adapter on consumer reviews using Domain-Adversarial Neural Networks (DANN), Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD), and Supervised Contrastive Learning (SCL), and evaluate transfer to movie reviews (SST-2) and a heavily restricted subset of financial news (Financial PhraseBank). Within this constrained sample, we observe two distinct transfer patterns. On SST-2, domain adaptation provides negligible gain regardless of scale. On the financial subset, explicit domain adaptation appears to recover substantial performance for small general-purpose backbones. Notably, we find that adversarial alignment (DANN) is associated with degraded performance for domain-specialized backbones like FinBERT, consistent with erosion of pre-existing domain-specific structure, whereas supervised contrastive loss appears to preserve it. These preliminary findings suggest that the efficacy of explicit domain adaptation is highly contingent on whether the frozen backbone already possesses target-domain coverage.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 年龄和语速与FP率呈负相关；性别效应具有语言特异性且方向相反于以往研究；情感与FP率呈正相关；政治立场和权力地位对FP率存在议会特异性影响，反对派发言人的FP率低于执政者。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了填充停顿在多语言、真实语境下的复杂动态，强调语言差异和社会角色在言语行为中的关键作用，为跨语言口语研究提供了新的实证基础。

Abstract: Filled pauses (FPs) are a universal feature of spontaneous speech, yet most studies rely on small, single-language corpora, limiting the generalisability of their findings. We analyse ~4,000 hours of parliamentary speech across four related Slavic languages (Croatian, Czech, Polish, Serbian). FP occurrence is obtained via transformer-based automatic detection, while FP rate is modelled using Generalised Estimating Equations (GEE) with Mundlak correction to distinguish within- from between- speaker effects. We replicate a negative association of age and speech rate with FP rate, but find that gender effects are language-specific and directionally opposite to most prior literature. ### [121] [InfluMatch: Frontier-Quality KOL Search at 4B-Model Cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05968)
*Krittanon Kaewtawee,Petmongkon Pornpichitsuwan,Natchaya Temyingyong,Nutnicha Laplamoon,Wachiravit Modecrua,Krittin Pachtrachai,Touchapon Kraisingkorn*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出InfluMatch系统，通过三阶段级联（检索→重排→推理）实现低成本、高精度的泰国营销影响力人物匹配。使用小型开源模型，先用密集检索获取50个候选，再用4B点式重排器筛选10个，最后由4B推理模型基于泰语理由对每个标准评分。该设计显著降低计算成本：仅对前10名推理使令牌消耗减半，同时性能提升14分。在11个查询的测试中，整体系统达到94.1% P@5，优于仅检索基线，接近前沿模型Kimi-K2.6（91.8%），但输出令牌减少约35倍，单次50个候选查询仅需约20秒（单个A100）。唯一有效微调为成对训练的重排器，其最佳选择准确率达78.0% EM；而对推理模型进行逐项标签微调虽提升离线分数，却损害端到端排序表现，归因于绝对标注任务设计。最终采用未微调的基础推理模型作为最优部署方案，实现可部署、可解释的低成本影响力人物搜索系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有影响力人物匹配方法要么依赖关键词搜索，难以捕捉语义契合度；要么使用大型语言模型逐一评估所有候选人，虽准确但代价高昂且速度慢。亟需一种既高效又精准的低成本解决方案，尤其适用于自由格式、多维度的泰国市场营销需求。

Method: InfluMatch采用三阶段级联架构：第一阶段为密集检索，从大规模候选集中召回50个初步结果；第二阶段为4B参数量的点式重排器，基于单个'是'标记的对数概率对候选进行打分并保留前10名；第三阶段为4B参数量的推理模型，针对每条营销标准生成泰语解释，并依据评分标准进行打分。整个系统完全基于小型开源模型构建，优化成本与效率平衡。

Result: 在包含11个查询的测试集上，完整级联系统达到94.1% P@5，远超仅检索基线（近似随机），性能接近前沿模型Kimi-K2.6（91.8%）。相较之下，其输出令牌数减少约35倍，单次处理50个候选者仅耗时约20秒（单张A100）。实验发现，只有成对微调的重排器带来显著收益（最佳选择准确率78.0% EM）；而对推理模型进行逐项标签微调虽提升离线指标，却导致端到端排名性能下降，揭示了绝对标注任务设计的潜在缺陷。最终，未微调的基础推理模型表现最优，适合作为实际部署方案。

Conclusion: InfluMatch成功构建了一个低成本、高性能、可解释的影响力人物匹配系统，可在不依赖大型语言模型的前提下，实现接近前沿模型的精度，同时大幅降低计算资源消耗和延迟。其核心在于合理设计的三阶段级联流程与对微调策略的深刻理解，尤其强调未微调基础模型在推理阶段的优势。该系统具备良好的可部署性，适用于真实商业场景中的泰国市场营销需求。

Abstract: Matching influencers (KOLs) to free-form, multi-part Thai marketing criteria is today served either by keyword search over structured profiles, which misses semantic fit, or by prompting frontier LLMs over every candidate, which is accurate but slow and expensive. We present InfluMatch, a low-cost three-stage cascade -- retrieval $\rightarrow$ rerank $\rightarrow$ reason -- built entirely from small open-weight models: dense retrieval returns 50 candidates, a 4B pointwise reranker scores each by the log-probability of a single Yes token and keeps 10, and a 4B reasoner grades the shortlist per criterion on a rubric with a Thai rationale. The cascade is designed for cost: reasoning over a filtered top-10 halves token spend versus reasoning over all 50 while scoring 14 points higher. End-to-end against human relevance labels on an 11-query set with all 50 candidates labeled, the full cascade reaches 94.1% P@5, versus a retrieval-only baseline near random; it matches the frontier model Kimi-K2.6 (91.8%) while emitting ${\sim}35\times$ fewer output tokens and serving a 50-KOL query in ${\sim}20$ s on one A100. Notably, the only fine-tuning that pays off is pairwise: a SimPO-tuned reranker matches the frontier baseline's best-pick accuracy (78.0 EM), whereas fine-tuning the reasoner on pointwise per-criterion labels improves offline scores yet degrades end-to-end ranking -- an inversion we trace to the design of the absolute labeling task -- leaving the untuned base model as the strongest deployed reasoner. The result is a deployable, explainable KOL search system at a small fraction of frontier serving cost.

</details>


### [122] [MemDefrag: Latent Memory Defragmentation for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05969)
*Ruiyi Yan,Zhuoyuan Mao,Yiwen Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MemDefrag提出了一种无需训练、模型无关的框架，通过探测中间层注意力密度发现潜在的内存追踪信号，实现内存碎片整理（排序、重排、过滤）和基于信息量引导的比例遗忘机制，显著提升长时记忆性能，在知识保留和长上下文任务中优于MemoryLLM和M+。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于潜伏记忆的长期记忆范式在内存更新时因位置编码错位和缺乏区分目标与无关记忆片段的追踪机制而性能下降，亟需一种有效的追踪方法以改善记忆管理。

Method: 通过分析分层注意力密度，发现少数中间层对目标记忆片段具有最高注意力集中度，利用此内在追踪信号进行内存碎片整理，并引入基于信息量的成比例遗忘策略以应对容量超限问题。

Result: 实验表明，MemDefrag在50次内存更新后知识保留率高达43.0%，远超MemoryLLM（17.4%）和M+（17.6%），且在长上下文基准测试中表现优异，具备跨多种LLM及潜伏记忆变体的良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: MemDefrag成功揭示并利用了潜伏记忆中的内在追踪信号，实现了高效、无训练的内存管理，为大语言模型的长期记忆优化提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Latent memory, which stores past knowledge fragments as per-layer hidden states, has emerged as a promising paradigm (e.g., MemoryLLM and M+) for long-term memory in large language models (LLMs). However, the paradigm suffers from significant performance degradation during memory updates, due to positional encoding misalignment and the absence of any tracing mechanism to distinguish target memory fragments from irrelevant ones. To discover such a tracing mechanism, we probe the layer-wise attention density over stored memory fragments, and find that a small set of middle transformer layers consistently concentrates the highest density on the target fragment - exposing an inherent tracing signal. In light of this, we propose MemDefrag, a training-free and model-agnostic framework that (1) uses a middle-layer tracing signal to conduct memory defragmentation (rank, reorder, and filter memories), and (2) applies an informativeness-guided proportional forgetting mechanism once capacity is exceeded. Experiments show that MemDefrag substantially outperforms MemoryLLM and M+ on knowledge retention (e.g., 43.0% vs. 17.4%/17.6% after 50 memory updates) and long-context benchmarks, and generalizes well across various LLMs and latent-memory variants.

</details>


### [123] [PluraMath: Extending Mathematical Reasoning Evaluation Beyond High-Resource Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05992)
*Daryna Dementieva,Nikolay Babakov,Kathy Hämmerl,Ilseyar Alimova,Jindřich Libovický,Shu Okabe,Miras Baisbay,Lukas Edman,Abrorkhon Inomkhujaev,Antonia Karamolegkou,Mateusz Lango,Volkan Özer,Nikola Selic,Subhankar Swain,Tsedeniya Kinfe Temesgen,Galit Bary Weisberg,Alexander Fraser*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 细粒度分析显示，高资源语言与低资源语言在数学推理性能上存在持续差距；模型表现优劣主要与指令遵循能力相关；所有数据与工具完全开源，促进多语言基准的可及性与可持续发展。

Conclusion: PluraMath填补了多语言数学推理评估中对低资源语言覆盖的空白，揭示了当前模型在非主流语言上的局限性，并通过开源推动公平、包容的多语言模型研究生态。

Abstract: Mathematical reasoning has become a central task for evaluating and tuning reasoning Large Language Models (LLMs), yet existing benchmarks remain heavily biased toward high-resource languages, with English and Chinese dominating both pre-training corpora and evaluation suites. The recently released PolyMath (Wang et al., 2025) dataset represents a significant step forward, yet its coverage is still limited to 18 only high-resource languages. To address this gap, we introduce PluraMath, an extension of PolyMath to 18 additional {underrepresented languages spanning 6 language families -- ranging from mid-resource to extreme low-resource settings. We constructed the dataset through a human-curated pipeline, where native speakers thoroughly validated pre-computed translations. Using PluraMath, we then benchmark 27 reasoning LLMs across four model scales -- small, mid-size, large, and closed-source ensembles -- probing the multilingual mathematical reasoning capabilities of state-of-the-art models under diverse linguistic conditions. Our fine-grained analysis confirms a persistent gap in mathematical reasoning performance between high-resource and underrepresented languages, with stronger results largely associated with better instruction-following ability. We fully open-source our dataset, data acquisition pipeline, and evaluation framework, with the goal of lowering the barrier to multilingual benchmark development for underrepresented communities.

Abstract: Putnam's Social Capital Theory is a foundational framework for collective action and community prosperity. However, traditional empirical methods face practical limits on control and replication. Meanwhile, LLM-based social simulations are typically behavior-driven and lack theory-aligned environments for modeling Putnam's core propositions. To address these gaps, we introduce SocaSim, an LLM-based multi-agent simulation framework to study Putnam's Social Capital Theory from theoretical blueprint to simulated reality. Specifically, we build an environment integrating social network evolution, trust dynamics, and norm propagation, where agents engage in repeated collective-action experiments, and then apply the three dimensions to analyze adaptation challenges in smart elderly care. Our simulations reproduce Putnam's macro-level patterns and exhibit strong human-agent alignment at the group level. Unlike traditional methods, SocaSim traces micro-level causal pathways of social network, trust, and norms via round-by-round simulations and counterfactual interventions, enabling process-level interpretability. Taken together, these capabilities establish a research paradigm that leverages LLM agents to bridge social science and computer science.

### [125] [Measuring the practice of shared-decision making (OPTION12): An Investigation into Open-sourced Smaller LLMs (OS-sLLMs) for Better Privacy and Sustainability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06127)
*Tamara Wit,Lifeng Han,Carly Heipon,David Lindevelt,Anne Stiggelbout,Suzan Verberne*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究首次探索开源小型语言模型（OS-sLLMs）在使用Observer OPTION12框架进行共享决策制定（SDM）自动化评估中的应用，聚焦于隐私保护且可本地部署的模型与荷兰黑色素瘤咨询转录文本。通过专家标注的临床会话数据，评估了三种通用领域和两种医学领域OS-sLLMs，结果显示通用领域模型表现优于医学领域模型，后者存在严重幻觉和指令遵循失败问题。Gemma3:12b与人工标注达成最强一致性（皮尔逊相关系数r=0.51，斯皮尔曼等级相关系数ρ=0.59）。项目级和定性分析揭示了时间话语推理、对话角色归属和证据定位等方面的系统性挑战。研究还提出一种Judge-LLM共识框架以支持多模型间的分歧解决。尽管当前OS-sLLMs尚无法替代人类标注者，但其为隐私保护的人机协同SDM评估提供了有前景的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究依赖大型商业模型和较短的OPTION5量表，存在隐私泄露风险且难以适应真实临床场景。本研究旨在探索开源小型语言模型在本地部署环境下对共享决策制定进行自动化评估的可行性，尤其关注隐私保护与实际临床数据的应用，填补该领域的空白。

Method: 采用专家标注的荷兰黑色素瘤咨询转录文本，评估三种通用领域和两种医学领域开源小型语言模型（OS-sLLMs），使用Observer OPTION12框架进行自动化评估。通过皮尔逊和斯皮尔曼相关系数衡量模型与人工标注的一致性，并开展项目级及定性分析以识别模型缺陷。引入Judge-LLM共识框架处理多模型间分歧，提升评估可靠性。

Result: 通用领域模型整体表现优于医学领域模型，其中Gemma3:12b在一致性指标上表现最佳（皮尔逊r=0.51，斯皮尔曼ρ=0.59）。医学领域模型存在显著幻觉和指令遵循失败。系统性挑战包括时间话语推理不准确、对话角色误判以及证据缺乏有效支撑。Judge-LLM共识框架有助于缓解多模型分歧问题。

Conclusion: 当前开源小型语言模型尚不足以完全替代人类标注者，但在隐私保护前提下具备作为人机协同共享决策评估基础的潜力，未来可通过优化模型与共识机制进一步提升性能。

Abstract: We present LLM4SDM, the first study of open-source smaller language models (OS-sLLMs) for automated assessment of shared decision making (SDM) using the Observer OPTION12 framework. Unlike previous work that relies on large commercial models and the shorter OPTION5 instrument, our study focuses on privacy-preserving locally deployable models and Dutch melanoma consultation transcripts. Using expert-annotated clinical consultations, we evaluate three general-domain and two medical-domain OS-sLLMs during a development-phase pilot study. Results show that general-domain models outperform medical-domain models, which exhibit substantial hallucination and instruction-following failures. Gemma3:12b achieves the strongest agreement with human annotations (Pearson r=0.51, Spearman \r{ho}=0.59). Item-level and qualitative analyses reveal systematic challenges related to temporal discourse reasoning, conversational role attribution, and evidence grounding. We further introduce a Judge-LLM consensus framework designed to support disagreement resolution among multiple models. Our findings suggest that while current OS-sLLMs cannot replace human annotators, they offer a promising foundation for privacy-preserving human-in-the-loop SDM assessment.
