### [126] [CurateEvo: Data-Curation Evolving for Agentic Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06140)
*Dingzirui Wang,Xuanliang Zhang,Keyan Xu,Qingfu Zhu,Wanxiang Che*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CurateEvo 是一种基于失败驱动的动态演化框架，用于改进大语言模型代理在后训练阶段的数据筛选。它将数据筛选策略表示为可执行代码，并通过从保留开发集中的失败轨迹迭代重写该策略。每轮中，演化后的策略将固定原始语料库转化为监督微调数据、强化学习数据和推理时的记忆库。该过程首先通过诊断重复失败模式来增强有效性（如数据增强、过滤或精炼），然后通过成本感知目标剪枝冗余或低效训练回合以提升效率。在 ACEBench-Agent、BFCL-V4 和 τ^2-Bench 上的实验表明，无论在标注数据还是真实数据设置下，CurateEvo 均显著优于现有方法，平均得分分别提升 3.2 和 2.7 分。分析还显示其与多种后训练方案兼容，并大幅降低数据筛选开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型代理的后训练流程通常将数据筛选视为固定预处理步骤，主要关注数据增强，而忽视了对下游失败的过滤、精炼与适应，导致数据质量受限且效率低下。因此亟需一种能根据实际失败反馈动态优化数据筛选策略的方法。

Method: 提出 CurateEvo 框架，将数据筛选策略建模为可执行代码，利用保留开发集中的失败轨迹进行迭代演化。每轮中，策略动态生成监督微调数据、强化学习数据及推理记忆库；通过诊断常见失败模式实现数据增强、过滤或精炼以提升有效性，并在成本感知目标下剪枝冗余或低效训练回合以提高效率。

Result: 在 ACEBench-Agent、BFCL-V4 和 τ^2-Bench 上的实验结果表明，CurateEvo 在标注数据和真实数据设置下均显著优于现有方法，平均得分提升 3.2 和 2.7 分。同时，其具备良好的兼容性，能适配不同后训练流程，并显著减少数据筛选工作量。

Conclusion: CurateEvo 通过失败驱动的动态演化机制，实现了数据筛选策略的自适应优化，在提升长周期决策能力的同时降低人工干预与计算开销，是大语言模型代理后训练中高效、可扩展的数据筛选新范式。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents require post-training methods that can improve long-horizon decision making from environment feedback. However, existing agentic post-training pipelines often treat data curation as a fixed preprocessing step, focusing mainly on data augmentation while neglecting filtering, refinement, and adaptation to downstream failures. We propose CurateEvo, a failure-driven dynamic evolution framework for agentic post-training data curation. CurateEvo represents the curation strategy as executable code and iteratively rewrites it using failed trajectories from a held-out development set. At each epoch, the evolved strategy transforms a fixed raw corpus into supervised fine-tuning data, reinforcement learning data, and an inference-time memory bank. The evolution process first improves effectiveness by diagnosing recurring failure modes and augmenting, filtering, or refining data accordingly, and then improves efficiency by pruning redundant or low-utility training turns under a cost-aware objective. Experiments on ACEBench-Agent, BFCL-V4, and τ^2-Bench under both labeled and wild-data settings show that CurateEvo consistently outperforms prior curation methods, improving average scores by 3.2 and 2.7 points, respectively. Further analyses demonstrate that CurateEvo is compatible with different post-training recipes and substantially reduces curation overhead.

</details>


### [127] [Prompting Complexity: Shortest Prompts for Texts and Behaviors in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06145)
*Adrian Cosma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文定义了提示复杂度（prompting complexity）：在固定指令微调语言模型下，使确定性解码生成目标文本的最短合理提示是什么。该度量是资源有界柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度的模型相关类比，其中提示为程序，模型接口为解释器，提示中省略的信息由模型权重、训练分布、分词器、模板和解码规则提供。不同于经典柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度，该度量故意非通用；同一文本对不同模型可能成本差异巨大。研究限制程序为人类可读的合理文本而非任意标记串，以对齐提示工程。扩展至软提示复杂度以处理近似输出，形成模型相关的文本压缩形式及提示优化目标。还定义了提示距离与行为提示复杂度，用于比较最短生成提示及满足规范的输出。基于此，提出一项实证研究议程，探索在固定语言模型接口下，哪些文本和行为可通过短而合理的提示实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度无法直接应用于语言模型，因模型权重和训练数据提供了额外信息。需要一种模型相关的复杂度度量来理解提示工程中短提示的有效性，并指导提示优化。

Method: 提出提示复杂度的严格定义，将提示视为程序，模型作为解释器。采用可计算的枚举方法在有限上下文设置中求解。限制提示为人类可读文本以保持实际意义。扩展至软提示复杂度，引入损失性压缩概念。定义提示距离与行为提示复杂度，支持多维度分析。

Result: 成功构建了模型相关的提示复杂度框架，包括硬提示与软提示复杂度、提示距离、行为复杂度等。验证了其在特定模型下的可计算性与实用性，揭示了不同模型间复杂度的显著差异。

Conclusion: 提示复杂度为理解语言模型行为提供了新的理论工具，有助于指导高效提示设计与模型能力评估。未来研究应聚焦于跨模型比较、提示优化算法开发及复杂度与模型性能的关系探索。

Abstract: In this paper, we define the quantity of prompting complexity: for a fixed instruction-tuned language model, what is the shortest plausible prompt that makes deterministic decoding produce a target text? It is an LM-relative analogue of resource-bounded Kolmogorov complexity: the prompt is a program, the model interface is the interpreter, and information omitted from the prompt is supplied by the model's weights, training distribution, tokenizer, template, and decoding rule. Unlike classical Kolmogorov complexity, this measure is intentionally non-universal. In the finite-context setting it is computable by enumeration, but there is no model-independent invariance theorem; the same text may be cheap for one model and inaccessible or expensive for another. To keep the search space aligned with prompt engineering, we restrict programs to plausible human-readable texts rather than arbitrary token strings. We extend the exact definition to soft prompting complexity for approximate outputs, yielding a lossy notion of model-relative text compression and a formal target for prompt optimization. We also define prompting distance by comparing shortest generating prompts, and behavioral prompting complexity for reaching any output satisfying a specification. Based on these formulations, we define a research agenda for empirically studying which texts and behaviors are accessible from short plausible prompts under a fixed LM interface.

</details>


### [128] [LLM Agents for Deliberative Collaboration: A Study on Joint Decision Making Under Partial Observability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06157)
*Chenxu Wang,Yongkun Yang,Boyuan Du,Shiwei Lin,Huaping Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了在部分可观测联合决策任务中，大型语言模型（LLM）代理的辩论式协作。作者将辩论式协作形式化为具有部分和不对称观测的协作联合决策问题，并提出了一个可扩展的基准测试，涵盖多个任务设置和领域，要求代理通过辩论交流信息以达成共享奖励的联合决策。研究还构建了参考框架和评估协议，系统评估了多种代表性LLM。结果表明，复杂辩论式协作任务仍对当前最先进的语言模型构成挑战，即使借助外部数学工具，模型也可能在信息对齐或复杂推理过程中失败。但诊断分析也发现，辩论过程可能提供反思和纠错的机会，有时能提升性能，优于集中式基线。整体上，本工作为评估和改进基于LLM的辩论式协作代理奠定了基础，并揭示了当前多代理系统的优势、局限与特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类协作中自然存在沟通以对齐信息并达成共识的过程，而当前大型语言模型在复杂协作任务中表现不足，尤其在部分可观测和不对称信息环境下。因此需要建立一个系统化的评估框架，以理解并改进LLM在辩论式协作中的能力。

Method: 将辩论式协作形式化为部分可观测、不对称观测下的合作联合决策问题；设计可扩展的基准测试，覆盖多任务和多领域；构建参考框架与评估协议，系统评估多种代表性LLM在不同场景下的表现；进行诊断分析，探究辩论过程中的错误纠正潜力。

Result: 现有最先进的语言模型在复杂辩论式协作任务中仍面临挑战，常在信息对齐或复杂推理环节失败；但辩论过程具备反思与纠错能力，有时表现优于集中式基线，显示出其潜在优势。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了评估和改进基于LLM的辩论式协作代理的基础框架，揭示了当前多代理系统在协作能力上的优缺点，为未来研究提供了重要方向。

Abstract: Deliberation plays a crucial role in collaboration; when humans work together, they naturally engage in communication to align information and reach an agreement. In this paper, we investigate deliberative large language model (LLM) agents under partially observable joint decision-making tasks. We formalize deliberative collaboration as a cooperative joint decision problem with partial and asymmetric observations, and introduce a scalable benchmark that instantiates this problem across multiple task settings and domains in which agents must exchange information through deliberation to reach a joint decision with a shared reward. We then instantiate a reference scaffold and evaluation protocol for deliberative agents and conduct a systematic evaluation of a range of representative LLMs. The results reveal that complex deliberative collaboration tasks continue to challenge state-of-the-art language models. Even with the aid of external mathematical tools, language models may fail in either the deliberation process for aligning information or the complex reasoning process for making the decision. On the other hand, diagnostic analysis reveals that the deliberation process may also provide opportunities for reflection and error correction, sometimes improving performance over centralized baselines. Altogether, our work establishes a foundation for evaluating and improving LLM agents in deliberative collaboration and provides insights into the strengths, limitations, and properties of current LLM-based multi-agent systems.

### [129] [LongCrafter: Towards Diverse Long-Context Understanding via Evidence-Graph-Guided Instruction Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06160)
*Chenhao Yuan,Yinhao Xu,Shuwen Xu,Xizhi Yang,Jiaxiang Liu,Chenxi Zhou,Shaoping Huang,Haolin Ren,Pengfei Cao,Jun Zhao,Kang Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文SFT数据合成方法存在任务覆盖窄、指令难度不足、缺乏忠实度监督等问题，亟需更系统、可控制且可追溯的生成机制。

Method: 构建层次化任务分类体系（分局部/浅层与全局/深层），基于该分类生成对齐任务的长上下文，分解为显式证据图以建模段落间依赖，并生成严格基于证据片段的指令-响应对，确保推理的可解释性与忠实性。

Result: 在LongBench、LongBench v2和LooGLE上，使用LongCrafter数据微调的模型优于所有SFT基线及官方后训练模型，尤其在高难度任务上提升显著；数据更具多样性与难度分布均衡，模型能稳健定位证据，有效缓解‘中间丢失’现象。

Abstract: Synthesizing long-context supervised fine-tuning (SFT) data is a scalable way to enhance the long-context understanding of large language models (LLMs), yet existing approaches share three limitations: narrow task coverage, insufficient instruction difficulty, and a lack of faithfulness supervision. We propose \textbf{LongCrafter}, a structured synthesis framework that couples a hierarchical task taxonomy with an evidence-grounded pipeline. The taxonomy organizes long-context understanding into local/shallow and global/deep levels and yields 32 fine-grained task types that serve as a global generative prior. Guided by this taxonomy, LongCrafter constructs task-aligned long contexts, decomposes them into explicit evidence graphs that model cross-paragraph dependencies, and generates instruction--response pairs strictly grounded in the located evidence spans, ensuring both controllable difficulty and faithful, traceable reasoning. Models fine-tuned on LongCrafter data outperform all SFT baselines and even the official post-trained models on LongBench, LongBench~v2, and LooGLE across both Qwen2.5-7B and LLaMA-3.1-8B, with the largest gains on high-difficulty tasks. Further analysis shows that LongCrafter data is more diverse and better spread across difficulty levels, and that the trained models locate evidence robustly regardless of position, effectively mitigating the ``lost in the middle'' problem.

### [130] [Improving LLM-Generated Process Model Quality Through Reinforcement Learning: The Role of Reward Function Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06175)
*Alexander Rombach,Chantale Lauer,Nijat Mehdiyev*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了基于强化学习（RL）的流程模型生成中奖励函数的设计，通过48种配置在两个大语言模型（Llama-3.1 8B 和 Qwen-2.5 14B）上进行实验，使用包含38个度量的自动化评估框架评估语法、语用和语义质量。结果表明：1）RL显著提升语用与语法质量，同时保持语义一致性，输出变异性降低六倍以上；2）等权重奖励优于针对性加权，后者无法提升目标维度且可能导致模型陷入低质量模式；3）奖励设计与模型架构存在非平凡交互，如无效惩罚对一个模型至关重要而对另一个则无关，微调初始化对一个架构必要，对另一个反而有害。结论指出，奖励组合是优化结果的关键决定因素，其影响甚至可比应用RL本身还大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽能从自然语言生成BPMN流程模型，但监督微调受限于训练数据中的模式，难以突破性能瓶颈。强化学习可通过外部质量度量实现超越，然而当质量维度多元时，如何设计奖励函数尚不明确。因此亟需系统探索奖励函数设计对多维质量优化的影响。

Method: 采用组序列策略优化（Group Sequence Policy Optimization），在两个大语言模型（Llama-3.1 8B 和 Qwen-2.5 14B）上，基于由38个自动化指标构成的评估框架，测试48种不同的奖励函数配置，涵盖不同权重分配、惩罚机制及初始化方式，以分析其对流程模型生成质量的影响。

Result: RL显著提升流程模型的语法与语用质量，同时保持语义一致性，输出稳定性提升超过六倍；等权重奖励表现最优，针对性加权反而导致性能下降或模式坍缩；奖励设计与模型架构存在显著交互效应，如无效惩罚和微调初始化的作用因模型而异。

Conclusion: 奖励函数的设计是决定强化学习优化效果的核心因素，其影响程度堪比是否采用强化学习本身。该发现适用于任何需在多个自动化维度上评估质量的结构化生成任务。代码与实现已开源。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate BPMN process models from natural-language descriptions, yet supervised fine-tuning (SFT) limits their output quality to the patterns present in the training data. Reinforcement learning (RL) can optimize beyond this ceiling using external quality measures, but how the reward function should be designed when quality is multi-dimensional remains unexplored. We present a systematic investigation of reward function design for RL-based process model generation, training two LLM families (Llama~3.1 8B, Qwen~2.5 14B) under 48 configurations using Group Sequence Policy Optimization with rewards derived from an automated evaluation framework comprising 38 metrics across syntactic, pragmatic, and semantic quality. Three findings emerge. First, RL significantly improves pragmatic and syntactic quality while preserving semantic fidelity, reducing output variability by more than sixfold. Second, equal reward weighting consistently outperforms targeted weighting: emphasizing a specific dimension fails to improve it and can collapse the model into a low-quality mode. Third, design choices interact with model architecture in non-trivial ways: the invalidity penalty is essential for one model but irrelevant for the other, and SFT initialization is indispensable for one architecture but counterproductive for another. These results demonstrate that reward composition is a primary determinant of optimization outcomes, with effects as large as the decision to apply RL itself. The findings generalize to any structured generation task where quality is assessed along multiple automated dimensions. We release our implementation and experimental code at https://github.com/chlauer99/RL_for_process_modeling.

*Alicia Parrish,Rajat Shinde,Sanket Badhe,Xinyi Bai,Sree Bhargavi Balija,Hua-Rong Chu,Emilio Ferrara,Armstrong Foundjem,Rajat Ghosh,Aakash Gupta,Xuanli He,Ong Chen Hui,Minji Jung,Madhangi Karimanal,Faiza Khan Khattak,Boryoung Kim,Eugenia Kim,Liliya Lavitas,Seok Min Lim,Victor Lu,Jim Moirangthem,Dhivya Nagasubramanian,Deepak Pandita,Sita Rajagopal,Geetha Raju,Evgeniia Razumovskaia,Aravind Reddy,Federico Ricciuti,Nobin Sarwar,Sungpil Shin,Sunayana Sitaram,Snehal Thorat,Tharindu Cyril Weerasooriya,Jasmijn Bastings,Joachim Baumann,Kongtao Chen,Murali Emani,Mariya Hendriksen,Jiho Jin,Jun Seong Kim,Younghoon Ko,Alicja Kwasniewska,Minjae Lee,Tom Wei-cyuan Lin Kashyap Ramanandula Manjusha,Junho Myung,Junyeong Park,Roma Patel,Shyam Ratan,Sudarsun Santhiappan,Priyanka Suresh,Tuesday,Ksheeraj Sai Vepuri Laura Amortegui-Ordonez,Claire Dennis,Minsuk Kahng,Chris Knotz,Alice Oh,Balaraman Ravindran,Soojung Ryu William Bartholomew,Hiwot Tesfaye,Lora Aroyo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建 Pluralis v0.1 数据集，从亚太六国（孟加拉、印度、韩国、巴基斯坦、新加坡、台湾）真实文化情境中采集6,448个多模态提示；采用图文协同设计，使孤立内容无害但组合后触发文化或法律违规；提出 Judge-Pluralis 框架，利用基于实证文化分类的 LLM-as-a-Judge 集成模型进行评估。

Conclusion: Pluralis v0.1 不是最终解决方案，而是推动多语言多文化评估研究的起点。呼吁学术界基于此基础，发展更完善的AI文化对齐评估体系，以支持全球化部署中的负责任AI。

Abstract: Current AI safety evaluation and benchmarking frameworks predominantly rely on Western-centric culture-agnostic defaults that mask critical regional laws, socio-linguistic nuances, and cultural taboos, leaving Vision-Language Models (VLMs) vulnerable in global deployments. Crucially, it introduces a multimodal evaluation paradigm: user text (e.g., "Should I gift this?") and an image referring to "this" (e.g., a clock) - both innocuous in isolation, but synergistically triggering specific legal or cultural violations. Pluralis disentangles universal safety violations from localized cultural appropriateness, establishing the latter as a first-class evaluation axis. To operationalize this, we present Judge-Pluralis, an agreement-gated LLM-as-a-Judge ensemble trained on examples classified in an empirically derived cultural taxonomy. Observing VLM behavior on a subset of the Pluralis surfaces recurring, locale-specific failure modes such as image misidentifications with downstream harm, missed item-context-locale interactions, and inadequate refusals. These failure modes vary systematically across locales and languages, exposing blind spots that globally averaged metrics conceal. Ultimately, Pluralis is not presented as a solved evaluation framework for cultural alignment, but rather as a first step and catalyst for future innovation. We call upon the research community to utilize this foundation to advance the science of multilingual, multicultural evaluation to better support AI cultural alignment globally.

We introduce Spider 2.0-AIFunc, a benchmark of 465 verified instances across 125 real-world databases covering six types of AI functions on the Snowflake platform. Starting from an existing enterprise text-to-SQL benchmark, we construct Spider 2.0-AIFunc through an agent-based pipeline that rewrites source tasks into AI-native form, simultaneously transforming target queries and refining natural language instructions to make the intended AI-native solution explicit and reduce ambiguity. All instances pass a multi-round repeated execution protocol across temporally separated windows to confirm result stability before release. Agent frameworks designed for traditional text-to-SQL challenges, such as schema retrieval and relevant table selection, do not transfer effectively to AI-native SQL: a minimal agent setup consistently matches or outperforms more elaborate alternatives, suggesting that the strategies these frameworks employ are less critical in this setting. Data are available at https://github.com/Leolty/Spider2-AIFunc .

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨儿童词汇习得是否在语义和词类上存在不均衡现象，旨在理解早期语言学习的内在机制。

Overall, our findings suggest that vocabulary development can be understood through the non-trivial interplay between activation dynamics and some degree of constraints regulating the visiting of lexical categories in complex networks.

### [134] [From Sinhala to Dhivehi: Cross-Lingual Transfer Learning for Low-Resource Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06289)
*Lukmal Ilyas,Nevidu Jayatilleke*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了通过从语言上相关的斯里兰卡语（一种资源较丰富的岛国印度-雅利安语）进行跨语言迁移学习，是否能改善马尔代夫语（Dhivehi）的自动语音识别（ASR）。通过17个实验，比较了五种迁移学习范式：仅使用马尔代夫语的基线、顺序微调、多语言微调、持续预训练以及以土耳其语为无关语言的对照实验。表现最佳的系统是先在斯里兰卡语上进行持续预训练，再在马尔代夫语上微调，并结合KenLM解码，实现了12.89%的词错误率（WER）和2.70%的字符错误率（CER），相比仅使用马尔代夫语的基线分别降低了13.50% WER和3.02% CER。土耳其语对照实验表明，性能提升源于语言相关性，且适应策略与解码配置对迁移学习的成功同样关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马尔代夫语在自动语音识别（ASR）及其他自然语言处理任务中资源匮乏，因此需要探索有效的迁移学习方法来提升其性能。由于马尔代夫语与斯里兰卡语同属岛国印度-雅利安语系，具有语言相似性，因此研究其作为迁移源的潜力具有重要意义。

Method: 本研究设计并实施了17项受控实验，涵盖五种迁移学习范式：(1) 仅使用马尔代夫语的基线模型；(2) 顺序微调；(3) 多语言微调；(4) 持续预训练；(5) 使用土耳其语作为无关语言的对照实验。其中最优方案为在斯里兰卡语上进行持续预训练，随后在马尔代夫语上微调，并采用KenLM进行解码。所有实验均在相同数据集和评估标准下进行，以确保结果可比性。

Result: 最优系统在马尔代夫语上的词错误率（WER）为12.89%，字符错误率（CER）为2.70%，相较于仅使用马尔代夫语的基线模型，分别降低了13.50% WER和3.02% CER。土耳其语对照实验验证了性能提升主要源于语言相关性，而非通用迁移。此外，适应策略与解码配置对最终性能有显著影响。

Conclusion: 跨语言迁移学习从语言相关的斯里兰卡语可有效提升马尔代夫语的自动语音识别性能。持续预训练结合适当的解码策略是当前最有效的迁移范式。语言相关性是成功迁移的关键因素，同时适应策略和解码配置也必须精心设计以实现最佳效果。该研究为低资源语言的自然语言处理提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Dhivehi, the national language of the Maldives, is currently under-resourced for automatic speech recognition (ASR) and other NLP tasks. This study investigates whether cross-lingual transfer learning from Sinhala, a linguistically related, relatively well-resourced Insular Indo-Aryan language, can improve Dhivehi ASR. We conduct seventeen experiments across five transfer learning paradigms: Dhivehi-only baselines, sequential fine-tuning, multilingual fine-tuning, continual pre-training, and a control using Turkish as an unrelated language. The strongest system, continual pre-training on Sinhala followed by fine-tuning on Dhivehi with KenLM, achieves 12.89% WER and 2.70% CER, outperforming the Dhivehi-only baseline by 13.50% WER and 3.02% CER. However, the adaptation strategy and decoding configuration are equally critical for a successful transfer learning experiment. We conduct seventeen controlled experiments spanning five transfer learning paradigms: Dhivehi-only baselines, sequential fine-tuning, multilingual fine-tuning, continual pre-training, and a control experiment using Turkish as an unrelated language. The strongest system, continual pre-training on Sinhala followed by fine-tuning on Dhivehi with KenLM, achieves 12.89% WER and 2.70% CER, outperforming the Dhivehi-only baseline by 13.50% WER and 3.02% CER. The Turkish control experiment confirms that observed improvements stem from linguistic relatedness; adaptation strategy and decoding configuration are also critical.

### [135] [Estimating Uncertainty from Reasoning: A Large-Scale Study of Multi- and Crosslingual MCQA Performance in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06327)
*Andrea Alfarano,Andrea Bacciu,Saab Mansour,Amin Mantrach,Marcello Federico*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次在22种语言（涵盖高、中、低资源语言）上进行大规模不确定性估计（UE）方法评估，对比了9种开箱与闭箱UE方法，在不同模型规模和架构下表现。研究通过人工标注的问答数据集，避免使用LLM作为裁判或嵌入式评分，以减少评估噪声。主要发现：1）让模型用英语推理而问题保持在低资源语言时，可显著提升UE性能，说明低资源语言理解能力良好，瓶颈在于生成；2）英语推理能缩小低资源与高资源语言间的UE性能差距，表明生成语言比问题语言更重要；3）小模型应采用基于概率的开箱方法，大模型则更适合自述不确定性的闭箱方法。此外，还提供了选择阈值以实现选择性预测的校准建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有不确定性估计（UE）研究主要集中于英语，缺乏对多语言场景的系统评估，尤其在低资源语言中的表现尚不明确。为提升多语言LLM系统的可靠性，需了解不同语言、模型规模和方法下的UE表现，从而指导实际部署中的决策机制。

Method: 构建两个人工标注的Q&A数据集，覆盖22种语言，涵盖高、中、低资源语言；比较9种开箱与闭箱UE方法；在不同模型大小与架构下测试；要求模型进行长文本推理，避免使用LLM-as-a-judge和嵌入式评分，以降低评估偏差。

Result: 1）在低资源语言问题上，用英语推理显著提升UE性能；2）英语推理可弥合高低资源语言间UE性能差距；3）小模型中开箱概率方法更优，大模型中闭箱自述不确定性方法表现更好；4）提出针对选择性预测的阈值校准策略。

Conclusion: 不确定性估计在多语言环境中的有效性高度依赖于生成语言与模型规模。通过使用英语推理，可有效缓解低资源语言的不确定性估计难题；模型规模决定了最优的UE方法选择；合理设置阈值对于实现可靠的系统性拒答至关重要。

Abstract: Uncertainty estimation (UE) enables LLM-powered systems to recognize when to abstain, yet existing research has predominantly focused on English. We present the first large-scale evaluation of UE methods across 22 languages, spanning high-, mid-, and low-resource settings. Using two human-curated Q\&A datasets, we compare open and closed box UE methods (nine in total) across different model sizes and architectures while eliciting long-form reasoning, avoiding LLM-as-a-judge and embedding-based scoring, which can introduce evaluation noise. We report three main actionable findings. First, we find that prompting models to reason in English while keeping questions in low-resource languages substantially improves UE performance, suggesting that comprehension of low-resource languages is largely intact, and that the reliability bottleneck lies in generation rather than understanding. Second, prompting models to reason in English closes the UE performance gap between low and high-resource languages, demonstrating that generation language matters more than the question language. Third, the choice of UE method should depend on model scale: at smaller scales, open-box probability-based methods outperform alternatives; at larger scales, closed-box self-verbalized uncertainty becomes superior. Finally, we provide an analysis of threshold selection for selective prediction, offering guidance on calibrating abstention in multilingual settings.

</details>


### [136] [Automated Compliance Mapping in Cloud Security with Domain-Adapted Sentence Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06364)
*John Bianchi,Luca Petrillo,Fabio Martinelli,Marinella Petrocchi*

TL;DR: 该论文提出使用领域自适应的Sentence Transformer模型来自动化云安全控制与技术指标之间的映射，通过构建包含3,499个语义对的训练语料库，并利用反向翻译和大语言模型改写扩展至最多13,996个样本。在两个独立任务（控制到指标、跨标准控制关联）上评估了五种模型架构，所有微调模型均优于零样本基线。最佳模型在控制到指标任务中提升达23 nDCG@10，在跨标准任务中，multi-qa-mpnet-dot-v1模型在反向翻译数据下达到0.870 nDCG@10。结果表明，领域内训练数据是性能提升的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前云安全控制与技术指标之间的映射依赖人工，效率低且易出错。为提高自动化水平并减少人为偏差，亟需一种可泛化、高效的映射方法。

Method: 构建来自五个欧洲安全标准和技术指标的3,499个语义对作为初始训练集，通过反向翻译和大语言模型进行数据增强，生成最多13,996个样本；采用五种Sentence Transformer架构进行微调，并在两个任务上评估性能：控制到指标匹配和跨标准控制关联。

Conclusion: 领域内训练数据是提升模型性能的核心因素，表明通过高质量语义对构建领域适配的语料库，可有效实现云安全控制与技术指标的自动化映射。

Abstract: Mapping cloud security controls to technical metrics is currently a manual process. This paper proposes domain adaptation of Sentence Transformer models to automate it. We build a training corpus of 3,499 semantic pairs from five European security standards and a set of technical metrics, then expand it via back-translation and LLM-based paraphrasing to up to 13,996 samples across four scenarios. We fine-tune five architectures and evaluate their performance on two independent tasks: control-to-metric and cross-standard controls association. All fine-tuned models outperform their zero-shot baselines. On the control-to-metric task, the best model gains up to 23 nDCG@10 points, while on the cross-standard control task, \textit{multi-qa-mpnet-dot-v1} under back-translation reaches 0.870 nDCG@10. The results show that in-domain training data is a primary driver of performance for the considered case studies.

### [137] [From Voting to Agent Collaboration: Answer-Type-Aware LLM Pipelines for BioASQ 14b](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06452)
*Taeyun Roh,Eunha Lee,Wonjune Jang,Sohyun Chung,Junha Jung,Jaewoo Kang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种针对生物医学问答任务的题型特定大型语言模型框架，通过根据不同问题类型（是/否、事实性、列表类）采用不同的推理策略，提升答案鲁棒性和证据可追溯性。对于是/否问题，采用片段打乱和自我反思以增强决策稳定性；对于事实性问题，结合全片段输入与思维链式上下文学习以精准识别生物医学实体；对于列表类问题，采用多智能体架构协同完成证据提取、候选生成、答案验证和最终聚合。在BioASQ 13b上的初步实验筛选出有效策略，并在正式的BioASQ 14b任务中表现优异，尤其在第四批的事实性子任务中获得第一名。结果表明，题型特定推理、集成预测与基于代理的验证相结合能有效提升生物医学问答可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物医学问答不仅需要从科学文献中准确提取信息，还需可靠整合多文档证据。现有方法通常采用统一提示策略，难以适应不同问题类型的推理和评估需求，导致答案不稳定或证据不充分。因此，亟需一种能够根据问题类型动态调整推理机制的框架，以提升答案的准确性与可解释性。

Method: 提出一种题型特定的大型语言模型框架，针对是/否、事实性、列表类问题分别设计不同的推理流程：（1）是/否问题使用片段打乱与自我反思，减少对证据顺序的敏感性；（2）事实性问题采用全片段输入与基于思维链的上下文学习，增强实体识别能力；（3）列表类问题引入多智能体架构，分阶段协作完成证据提取、候选生成、验证与聚合。通过在BioASQ 13b上进行预实验优化策略，再在官方的BioASQ 14b Task B中验证效果。

Result: 在BioASQ 14b Task B的官方评估中，该框架在多个批次中表现出色，尤其在第四批的事实性子任务中取得第一名。实验验证了题型特定推理、集成预测与多智能体验证的有效性，显著提升了答案的稳健性与证据可追溯性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，根据问题类型定制推理策略，结合集成预测与代理协作验证，是实现高可靠性生物医学问答的关键路径。该框架为复杂医学知识问答提供了可扩展、可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: Biomedical question answering requires not only accurate extraction of information from scientific literature but also reliable integration of evidence across multiple documents. This study presents a question-type-specific large language model (LLM) framework for BioASQ 14b Task B, designed to improve answer robustness and evidence grounding in biomedical question answering. Rather than applying a single prompting strategy to all questions, the framework selects different inference procedures for yes/no, factoid, and list questions according to their distinct reasoning and evaluation requirements. For yes/no questions, snippet shuffling and self-reflection are used to reduce sensitivity to evidence ordering and improve decision stability. For factoid questions, full-snippet input is combined with chain-of-thought-based in-context learning to support accurate biomedical entity identification. For list questions, a multi-agent architecture is employed, in which evidence extraction, candidate generation, answer verification, and final aggregation are handled collaboratively. Preliminary experiments on BioASQ 13b were used to identify effective inference strategies for each question type, and the resulting framework was subsequently evaluated in the official BioASQ 14b Task B challenge. In the official evaluation, our framework showed competitive performance across multiple batches and achieved first place in the factoid subtask of Batch 4. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of combining question-type-specific inference, ensemble prediction, and agent-based verification for reliable biomedical question answering.

Method: 基于政府公开数据构建DataGovBench基准，设计Table QA（复杂可分解问题求解）和Table Insight（专家级发现生成）两类任务，通过对比多种先进LLM及其代理框架的表现进行评估。

Abstract: Current benchmarks for evaluating Large Language Models (LLMs) in data analysis often fail to reflect real-world settings. They typically focus on fact retrieval from small tables and overlook the challenges of large multi-tabular datasets, external knowledge integration, and exploratory insight discovery. We introduce DataGovBench, a benchmark derived from governmental open data designed to evaluate LLMs in practical scenarios. The benchmark includes two tasks: Table QA that requires solving complex decomposable questions and producing textual answers or visualizations, and Table Insight that evaluates the ability of models to generate expert-level findings through exploratory data analysis. Comprehensive experiments with state-of-the-art LLMs, both with and without agentic frameworks, reveal significant performance gaps across both tasks. These results suggest that current LLM-based systems remain far from satisfying the demands of real-world data analytics. DataGovBench provides a challenging benchmark for advancing research on LLMs capable of both answering analytical queries and discovering insights from data. Code and sample data are available at https://github.com/SoHasegawa/datagovbench.

### [139] [Pitwall: Faithful Natural-Language Race-Strategy Briefings from a Calibrated Real-Time Monte Carlo Engine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06495)
*Juan S. Santillana*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Pitwall 是一个实时生成 F1 战略简报的生产系统，通过将每个句子分解为可验证的事实性断言（如位置、差距、轮胎、速度、超车、赛事控制），并基于概率赛车状态进行验证，确保生成内容的忠实性。系统采用蒙特卡洛模拟引擎（N=2000/圈）校准于 2018–2024 年 126 场比赛，并在 2025–2026 年完全独立数据上验证，表现优异（胜者进入前三名 90.3%，Brier 得分 0.0745）。训练数据仅保留所有断言均被状态支持的 81.9% 的样本，其余使用可信模板替代，防止模型接触无依据的目标。系统揭示了性能权衡：校准最优不等于决策最优；丰富目标虽提升表达生动性，但在状态稀疏时导致幻觉，该问题被四基复制实验归因于指令遵循而非模型规模，且可通过稀疏上下文审计解决。系统已在奥地利和英国两场真实大奖赛中成功运行，银石站的预测概率轨迹在结果未知前即锁定最终赢家，提前十圈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实时体育解说需要在严格时间限制下生成准确、有依据的自然语言内容，但现有模型常产生脱离实际状态的幻觉。传统方法将忠实性视为目标而非架构属性，难以保障生成内容与动态变化的真实赛事状态一致。因此，亟需一种能将事实性作为系统核心设计原则的解决方案，以实现高可靠性的实时生成。

Method: Pitwall 系统将每条生成语句拆解为若干类型化的事实断言（如位置、差距、轮胎状况等），并通过一个基于向量化的蒙特卡洛赛车延续引擎（2000次/圈模拟）对这些断言进行验证。该引擎基于2018–2024年126场比赛数据训练，并在2025–2026年未见数据上验证。生成前，所有训练目标必须经由同一验证器筛选：仅当所有断言均有状态支持时才被保留，否则回退至可信模板。生成模型从未接触过无依据的目标，从而杜绝幻觉。此外，系统通过稀疏上下文审计机制识别并抑制因状态信息不足引发的错误。

Result: 系统在两次真实大奖赛（奥地利、英国，2026）中成功部署，端到端完成从实时数据到多语言简报的生成。在银石赛道，其生成的概率轨迹在比赛结果揭晓前已锁定最终获胜者，提前十圈。整体验证表现优异：在155次回溯测试中，胜者进入前三名的比例达90.3%，持有数据上的Brier得分为0.0745。同时，实验发现：过度依赖丰富目标会提升语言生动性，但在状态稀疏时引发严重幻觉；而通过四基复制实验确认，此问题源于基础模型对指令的遵循能力不足，而非参数规模。稀疏上下文审计可有效缓解该问题。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，将忠实性作为系统架构的核心属性是实现高可靠性实时生成的关键。通过将生成内容分解为可验证断言，并结合强概率建模与严格筛选机制，Pitwall 实现了在动态、高压力场景下的精准、可信输出。系统不仅在性能上表现出色，更揭示了生成质量中多个维度之间的内在权衡，强调了在设计生成系统时需对不同目标分别设限与监控。此范式可推广至其他需强接地的实时自然语言生成任务。

Abstract: Live sports commentary is grounded generation under a deadline: statements concern real, named athletes, the grounding state changes every few seconds, and no reference text exists at generation time. We present Pitwall, a production system that generates natural-language Formula 1 strategy briefings in English, Spanish, and Portuguese, treating faithfulness as an architectural property rather than an aspiration: every published sentence is decomposed into typed factual claims (positions, gaps, tyres, pace, overtakes, race control) and each claim is verified against the probabilistic race state that prompted it. The same verifier gates the fine-tuning data: of 3,045 model-written targets, only the 81.9% whose every claim is state-supported are retained, the rest falling back to a provably faithful template, so the generator never sees an ungrounded target. Verification is meaningful because of the grounding substrate: a vectorized Monte Carlo engine (N=2,000 per-lap race continuations) calibrated on 126 races (2018-2024) and validated on fully held-out 2025-2026 seasons (winner-in-top-3 90.3% over 155 backtests; held-out Brier 0.0745). A recurring finding spans both halves of the system: virtues trade off and must be gated separately. In simulation, calibration-optimal is not decision-optimal; in generation, fine-tuning on richer targets buys vividness that collapses into hallucination when the grounding state is sparse -- a failure a four-base replication traces to base-model instruction adherence, not scale, and that sparse-context auditing removes from the production model. End-to-end operation -- live timing to verified trilingual briefings -- was confirmed at two consecutive live Grands Prix (Austria and Britain, 2026); at Silverstone a timestamped probability trace, committed to disk before the outcome was known, locked onto the eventual winner ten laps before the flag.

</details>


### [140] [DynaKRAG: A Unified Framework for Learnable Evidence Control in Multi-Hop Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06507)
*Yaqi Wu,Xiaolei Guo,Chenyu Zhou,Jiaqi Huang,Xianfa Zhang,Junxu Zhang,Zhuo Yu,Zhubo Shi,Jianghao Lin,Dongdong Ge*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DynaKRAG提出一种基于状态条件的动态控制框架，用于多跳检索增强生成（RAG），通过学习共享策略选择有效的证据操作。它在每一步根据有效性层构建可执行动作集，并由学习控制器选择下一步操作，从而实现证据状态的演化与操作的自适应调整。实验表明，该方法在HotpotQA、2Wiki和MuSiQue上分别取得0.5998、0.5340和0.3061的F1分数，优于现有基线；移除控制器或缺乏充分性反馈会显著降低性能，证明了状态驱动的协调机制的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多采用特定管道或预定义拓扑结构组织多跳检索中的操作（如迭代检索、查询重写、证据批判、充分性判断），缺乏统一的状态感知策略来动态选择最优操作。因此，亟需一种能够基于当前证据状态智能决策的通用控制机制，以提升多跳推理的效率与准确性。

Method: DynaKRAG将多跳证据获取建模为状态条件下的控制过程：每一步通过有效性层生成当前可执行的动作集合，再由一个学习的控制器从中选择下一个操作；操作执行后更新证据状态，可能激活新的操作，形成动态演进。整个过程依赖于对证据状态的持续评估与反馈机制，特别是充分性判断。

Result: 在HotpotQA、2Wiki、MuSiQue三个基准上，DynaKRAG使用Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct模型分别获得0.5998、0.5340、0.3061的F1分数，均超越最强可控基线。若用均匀有效策略替代学习控制器，F1下降3.96–5.78点；若去除充分性反馈，则所有数据集性能均下降。此外，控制性检索实验显示，额外检索并非总是有益，说明智能调度的重要性。

Conclusion: DynaKRAG通过引入状态感知的动态控制机制，实现了对多跳证据获取中检索、诊断与缺口导向采集的协同优化，显著提升了复杂问答任务的表现，验证了基于证据状态进行智能决策的有效性。

Abstract: Multi-hop retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) acquires evidence sequentially, with each new document potentially revealing missing facts, bridge entities, query defects, or sufficient support for answering. Existing methods provide useful operations such as iterative retrieval, query reformulation, evidence critique, and sufficiency judging, but typically organize them within method-specific pipelines or predefined control topologies. This leaves underexplored how to learn a shared state-conditioned policy that chooses among currently valid evidence operations. We introduce DynaKRAG, which formulates multi-hop evidence acquisition as state-conditioned control over atomic evidence operations. At each step, a validity layer constructs the executable action set, and a learned controller selects the next operation. The resulting transition updates the evidence state and may enable new operations at subsequent steps. With Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct, DynaKRAG achieves F1 scores of 0.5998 on HotpotQA, 0.5340 on 2Wiki, and 0.3061 on MuSiQue, outperforming the strongest controlled baseline on all three benchmarks. Replacing the learned controller with a uniform-valid policy reduces F1 by 3.96--5.78 points, while removing sufficiency feedback hurts all three datasets. Controlled retrieval-cap experiments further show that additional retrieval is not uniformly beneficial. Together, these results demonstrate the benefit of coordinating retrieval, diagnosis, and gap-directed acquisition under an evolving evidence state.

</details>


### [141] [RSF-GLLM: Bridging the Semantic Gap in Multi-Hop Knowledge Graph QA via Recurrent Soft-Flow and Decoupled LLM Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06527)
*Sambaran Bandyopadhyay,Ananth Muppidi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RSF-GLLM提出一种解耦可微图推理与答案生成的框架，通过GRU引导的查询更新器和动态门控机制实现对语义不相似桥接节点的遍历，并引入流稀疏正则化保证从软概率到离散推理路径的收敛。该方法在WebQSP和CWQ数据集上表现优异，兼具高效推理与良好性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统检索-阅读流水线因不可微性导致检索器无法有效弥合中间节点与查询间缺乏词汇重叠的语义鸿沟，限制了多跳问答的准确性与效率。

Method: 提出RSF-GLLM框架，采用递归软流（RSF）模块，利用GRU引导的查询更新器传播连续相关性分数，结合动态门控机制通过结构线索遍历语义差异大的桥接节点，并引入流稀疏正则化确保推理路径从软概率收敛至离散路径；最终将提取的路径文本化并用于微调大语言模型，确保生成结果基于事实拓扑。

Result: 在WebQSP和CWQ数据集上的实验表明，RSF-GLLM在性能上具有竞争力，且推理效率显著优于依赖大语言模型的计算密集型方法。

Conclusion: RSF-GLLM通过解耦可微图推理与答案生成，有效解决了多跳知识图谱问答中的语义鸿沟问题，实现了高性能与高效率的平衡。

Abstract: Multi-hop Question Answering over Knowledge Graphs faces a critical challenge: traditional retrieve-then-read pipelines break differentiability, preventing the retriever from learning to bridge the semantic gap where intermediate nodes lack lexical overlap with the query. To address this, we propose RSF-GLLM, a framework decoupling differentiable graph reasoning from answer generation. Our Recurrent Soft-Flow (RSF) module employs a GRU-guided query updater to propagate continuous relevance scores, utilizing a dynamic gating mechanism to traverse semantically dissimilar bridge nodes via structural cues. We introduce flow sparsity regularization to theoretically guarantee convergence from soft probabilities to discrete reasoning paths. These paths are extracted and textualized to fine-tune a Large Language Model (LLM), ensuring generation is grounded in factual topology. Experiments on WebQSP and CWQ demonstrate that RSF-GLLM achieves competitive performance with superior inference efficiency compared to LLM based computationally expensive approaches.

</details>

Finally, we conduct an exploratory analysis mapping consumer loan delinquency across the derived affluence classes. By relying entirely on publicly available geospatial data, the proposed framework provides a scalable, interpretable, and cost-effective approach for granular urban affluence mapping across In-dian cities.

### [143] [Hierarchical Acoustic-Semantic Modeling: Modality Separation and Semantic Coherence for Full-Duplex SLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06540)
*Zhenyu Liu,Yunxin Li,Xuanyu Zhang,Qixun Teng,Shenyuan Jiang,Haolan Chen,Minjun Zhao,Fanbo Meng,Yu Xu,Yancheng He,Baotian Hu,Haizhou Li,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了全双工语音语言模型中模态干扰的根本原因——声学与语义建模在深层参数空间共享时产生的梯度冲突，并提出Lychee-FD框架，通过分层参数分离策略在深层解耦模态，同时通过专用语义对齐通道保持跨模态一致性。实验表明，该方法显著提升语音智能（Spoken QA提升7.4%）和交互流畅性（FullDuplexBench 1.5提升28.5%），且不牺牲推理效率。这是首个同时揭示模态干扰根源并提出有效解决方案的工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全双工语音语言模型受限于严重的模态干扰，导致知识退化和语义失真，使系统表现不自然、不智能，亟需从根本上解决模态间的冲突问题。

Method: 提出分层参数分离策略，将声学与语义模态在深层解耦，同时引入专用语义对齐通道以维持跨模态一致性，构建端到端的全双工框架Lychee-FD。

Result: 在多个全双工基准测试中，模型在语音智能（+7.4% on Spoken QA）和交互流畅性（+28.5% on FullDuplexBench 1.5）方面均取得显著提升，且推理效率未受影响。

Conclusion: 本工作首次揭示了全双工语音语言模型中模态干扰的根源，并提出了有效的分层解耦与对齐机制，实现了无缝、高性能、原生智能的全双工语音语言模型，推动了该领域的重大进展。

Abstract: Developing seamless, high-performance, native intelligent full-duplex Spoken Language Models (SLMs) remains a critical challenge and long-standing goal for the speech and NLP community. Despite notable progress, recent endeavors are fundamentally constrained by severe modality interference, which causes substantial knowledge degradation and compromises semantic integrity -- ultimately making full-duplex SLMs feel unnatural and unintelligent. In this paper, through an exhaustive fine-grained analysis of model optimization dynamics, we uncover the root cause of such performance degradation, revealing that modality interference arises from inherent gradient conflicts between acoustic and semantic modeling when the two modalities are forced to share a deep parameter space. Guided by this key insight, we introduce Lychee-FD, a native end-to-end full-duplex framework designed to mitigate modality interference. Importantly, we propose a hierarchical parameter separation strategy that decouples conflicting modalities in deep layers while preserving cross-modality coherence via a dedicated semantic alignment channel. Extensive experiments on multiple full-duplex benchmarks demonstrate that our method significantly advances the state of the art, yielding substantial improvements in both speech intelligence (+7.4% on Spoken QA) and full-duplex interaction fluidity (+28.5% on FullDuplexBench 1.5) without compromising inference efficiency. To the best of our knowledge, this work is the first to achieve two key advances: 1) uncovering and elucidating the root cause of modality interference in full-duplex SLMs, and 2) designing an elegant hierarchical model together with a practical solution for seamless, high-performance, native intelligent full-duplex SLMs.

### [144] [On the feasibility of dependency parsing of non-human sequences without a gold standard. Is evaluation possible in other species?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06542)
*Ramon Ferrer-i-Cancho,Catherine Hobaiter,Thore Bergman,Morgan Gustison*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文利用网络科学的最新进展，证明在非人类灵长类动物的发声或手势序列中，由于序列长度分布的快速衰减，解析器所获取的正确边的比例必然很高，因此无需真实标准即可进行评估。而人类语言序列不具备这一特性，故在人类语言中无真实标准的评估是难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上认为，无监督依赖解析在缺乏真实标注的情况下无法评估，尤其在非人类灵长类动物中因缺乏真实标准而被认为不可行。本文旨在挑战这一观点，探索在无真实标准条件下对非人类灵长类动物序列进行依赖解析评估的可能性。

Method: 基于网络科学的方法，分析非人类灵长类动物发声或手势序列的长度分布特性，结合其快速衰减的特征，推导出解析器必须高比例地恢复正确边的理论依据。

Result: 研究发现，非人类灵长类动物的序列具有快速衰减的长度分布，使得无真实标准下的评估成为可能，且解析器必须具备较高的准确率；而人类语言序列不具有该性质，导致无真实标准评估极为困难。

Conclusion: 尽管缺乏真实标注，但通过网络科学方法，可以在非人类灵长类动物中实现对无监督依赖解析的有效评估，这表明该方法在非人类物种中具有可行性，而在人类语言中仍面临巨大挑战。

Abstract: Dependency parsing consists of finding a tree representation for a sequence. Unsupervised dependency parsing aims to develop parsing methods without a gold standard during model training. In human languages, an unsupervised parser can be evaluated because some gold standard is usually available or can be created. For other species, a gold standard is unknown. Thus one may conclude that it is impossible to determine the accuracy of an unsupervised parser and, consequently, dependency parsing is unfeasible in other species. However, here we apply recent advances in network science to demonstrate that the proportion of correct edges retrieved by a parser must be high for the sequences of vocalizations or gestures that non-human primates produce due to the fast decay of the sequence length distribution. In contrast, human language sequences lack that property. Therefore, evaluation without a gold standard is feasible in non-human primates but a hard problem in humans.

</details>


### [145] [Diffusion Language Model Parallel Decoding via Product-of-Experts Bridge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.08048)
*Juntong Shi,Brian L. Trippe,Jure Leskovec,Stefano Ermon,Minkai Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PoE-Bridge introduces an intermediate distribution via Product-of-Experts (PoE) of diffusion and autoregressive models to bridge the gap between them, enabling faster and more accurate text generation. It uses parallel drafting with DLM, rejection sampling for refinement, and importance sampling for final correction, achieving 5× speedup and over 95% of AR model performance on hard tasks.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Diffusion language models (DLMs) offer fast parallel decoding but suffer from lower generation quality due to lack of token dependencies. Existing methods using importance sampling between DLM and AR models are computationally expensive due to large distribution gaps.

Method: PoE-Bridge constructs an intermediate PoE distribution combining DLM proposal and AR target. It first drafts multiple continuations in parallel using DLM, applies rejection sampling to align candidates with PoE, then uses importance sampling to correct toward the AR target. Additional techniques include mixed-temperature sampling for diversity and elastic rejection windows to reduce verification waste.

Result: PoE-Bridge achieves 5× speedup over standard DLM decoding and recovers at least 95% of the autoregressive model's performance, significantly improving accuracy on challenging tasks like mathematical reasoning and coding.

Conclusion: By introducing a well-designed intermediate distribution through PoE, PoE-Bridge effectively narrows the gap between diffusion and autoregressive models, enabling high-speed, high-quality text generation that surpasses previous approaches.

Abstract: Diffusion language models (DLMs) offer substantial speed advantages through parallel decoding, but the lack of token dependencies limits generation quality compared to autoregressive (AR) models. Recent progress attempts to bridge the gap via importance sampling, with DLM being the proposal and AR being the target. However, due to the huge gap between their distributions, the sampling requires a large number of particles and is thus expensive to compute. In this paper, we introduce PoE-Bridge, a novel decoding framework that drastically improves generation speed and accuracy by introducing an intermediate distribution to bridge the gap. The distribution is constructed as a Product-of-Experts (PoE) of the DLM proposal and the AR target. With the intermediate distribution, we first use the DLM to draft multiple continuations in parallel, then apply rejection sampling to verify the drafted tokens and move the resulting candidates toward the PoE. We then use importance sampling to further correct the PoE-aligned candidates toward the AR target. We further propose several improved techniques, including mixed-temperature sampling for enhanced diversity and elastic rejection windows for reducing wasted verification. Empirically, PoE-Bridge achieves significantly improved accuracy with $5\times$ speedup over the standard DLM decoding approach, and recovers at least 95% of the target AR model's performance, efficiently advancing most of the quality gap on challenging mathematical reasoning and coding tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/juntongshi48/poe-bridge.

</details>

### [146] [Prompt-to-Paper: Agentic AI System for Bioinformatics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05456)
*Ramsha Kamran,Maheera Amjad,Zartasha Mustansar,Arsalan Shaukat,Salma Sherbaz,Muhammad U. S. Khan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Prompt-to-Paper 是一个用于生成可发表级别科学论文的多智能体框架，通过检索增强生成、真实实验执行和多维度质量评估，解决了现有AI论文生成系统中缺乏可验证性、实验真实性及标准化评估的问题。系统在五个生物信息学案例中成功生成了无错误引用的提交格式PDF，平均质量提升17.96分（满分100），人类评审得分为7.0/10，每篇论文成本约0.31美元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型生成的学术论文存在三大缺陷：论断缺乏可验证文献支持、实验结果多为虚构、缺少标准化的质量评估体系，阻碍了其在真实科研中的应用。

Method: 提出多智能体框架Prompt-to-Paper，包含三个核心模块：(1) 基于章节感知相关性评分与雪球式引文扩展的确定性检索增强生成；(2) 自主代码代理执行真实计算生物学实验以生成真实数据；(3) 八维自动化质量评分器，结合参考统计与幻觉惩罚机制，并引入质量驱动的迭代优化循环。

Result: 在五个生物信息学案例中，系统生成的论文均无超出范围的引用，提交格式PDF完整；平均质量提升17.96分（最高+26.04）；人类评审平均得分7.0/10；每篇论文生成成本约为0.31美元。

Conclusion: Prompt-to-Paper 有效提升了AI生成论文的可验证性、实验真实性和整体质量，具备向真实科研出版流程集成的潜力，且具有高性价比。

Abstract: While recent advances in large language models have enabled end-to-end automated manuscript generation, existing systems suffer from three critical deficiencies: (i) generated claims are not deterministically grounded in verifiable literature, (ii) experimental results are frequently fabricated rather than executed, and (iii) there exists no standardized, multi-dimensional framework to assess whether AI-generated manuscripts meet the quality and rigor required for real-world publication. We present Prompt-to-Paper, a multi-agent framework that directly addresses this evaluation gap through three integrated innovations. First, a deterministic retrieval-augmented generation pipeline with section-aware relevance scoring and snowball citation expansion grounds every claim in a verifiable corpus of 60--100 papers. Second, an autonomous coding agent executes real computational biology experiments replacing synthetic outputs with genuine numerical results. Third, an eight-dimensional automated quality scorer, benchmarked with approximate reference statistics from published papers and augmented with explicit hallucination penalties, provides standardized, reproducible quality assessments. The quality-driven improvement loop uses a context-rich reviser that routes each iteration to one of three researcher actions and fires a deep research cycle every ten iterations to re-run experiments and re-manuscript from stronger outputs. We validate the system on five bioinformatics case studies; all five cases compiled submission-formatted PDFs with zero out-of-range citations. The improvement loop raises manuscript quality by an average of +17.96 points on a 0--100 scale (maximum +26.04. As partial external checks, a human reviewer scored the five manuscripts at an average of 7.0 out of 10. Complete manuscripts are produced at approximately 0.31 USD per paper.

</details>


### [147] [From Graphs to Gradients: Physics-Inspired Structural Attribution for Cyber-Physical IoT Systems and Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05563)
*Spyridon Evangelatos,Christos Diou,Georgios Th. Papadopoulos,Evangelos Markakis,Panagiotis Sarigiannidis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种受统计力学启发的新框架，通过无向能量模型来表示混合型网络物理物联网系统中的变量依赖关系，无需构建有向因果图即可实现依赖感知的归因分析。该方法能有效评估组件对系统行为的影响，并支持对扰动效应的推理，在工业物联网测试平台上验证了其在归因准确性、鲁棒性和可扩展性方面优于现有基于图的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统解释方法仅关注输入输出间的相关性，而因果解释需回答干预性问题以提供更稳健的洞察；但在大规模、具有反馈环和部分可观测性的复杂系统中，恢复显式有向因果结构不切实际。因此需要一种替代方案来实现可靠且可解释的分析。

Method: 提出一种基于能量的无向模型，利用统计力学思想建模系统中变量之间的依赖关系，通过分析能量景观的变化来量化各组件的影响，从而实现依赖感知的归因，无需显式构建有向因果图。

Result: 在包含连续与离散变量的工业物联网测试平台上进行仿真验证，结果表明该方法在归因准确率、鲁棒性及可扩展性上均优于当前最先进的图基方法，虽不能完全还原生成动态，但能提供对人类可理解且适用于预测与诊断任务的解释。

Conclusion: 所提框架为高维混合型网络物理与社会技术系统提供了原则性、结构化的解释能力，尤其适用于对可靠性要求高的场景，如工业物联网安全，具备广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Interpretable explanation methods in Artificial Intelligence aim to uncover the underlying causes and their effects, enabling a deeper understanding of why a system behaves in a certain way under different inputs. Unlike traditional explainability methods, which mainly highlight correlations between input and output variables, causal explanation focuses on interventional questions. By doing so, it provides more robust insights, helping users understand automated decisions, especially in high-risk domains. Recovering an explicit directed causal structure, however, is often impractical in large-scale, hybrid cyber-physical systems with feedback loops and partial observability. This paper introduces a novel framework inspired by statistical mechanics that instead models variable dependencies through an undirected, energy-based representation of cyber-physical IoT systems. Our approach enables rigorous dependency-aware attribution by analysing how variations in the energy landscape reflect the influence of individual components, without recovering a directed causal graph. It also supports reasoning about perturbation effects across hybrid interactions, providing reliable explanations of abnormal behaviours. We empirically examined our framework through simulations on an industrial IoT testbed with hybrid continuous and discrete variables, demonstrating higher attribution accuracy, improved robustness and better scalability than state-of-the-art graph-based approaches. While the attributions are not intended to fully recover the system's generative dynamics, they provide valuable, dependency-aware explanations supporting both human interpretation and downstream predictive and diagnostic tasks. Although demonstrated in industrial IoT security, our framework also applies to other high-dimensional cyber-physical and socio-technical systems requiring principled, structural explanations.

</details>


### [148] [CSTutorBench: Benchmarking Small Language Models as Tutors for Block-Based Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05571)
*H. Chad Lane,Bryson Kageler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出CSTutorBench，一个用于评估语言模型在VEX VR（基于积木的机器人环境）中作为计算机科学导师表现的基准测试。该基准包含17个情景化问题，采用基于教育辅导与反馈研究的评分标准，并通过人机协同的LLM评判流程进行评估。初步实验发现，尽管大模型在词汇和语气等表层表现良好，但在避免答案泄露、结合学生调试历史等深层教学行为上表现不佳。模型家族和指令微调方法比参数量更能预测教学质量，且基于教育提示工程的优化显著提升了10/11个模型的表现。研究强调了为特定教育场景设计、以教学法为基础的基准对小型语言模型选择的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型语言模型虽被探索用于教育辅导，但存在隐私、成本及依赖专有模型的问题。小型语言模型（SLMs）是潜在替代方案，但其在特定教育领域（如积木式编程）的应用缺乏有效评估工具，尤其当训练数据中缺少此类内容时。因此亟需一个面向具体教育场景、具有教学法基础的评估框架，以指导SLMs的合理选择与部署。

Method: 提出CSTutorBench基准，包含17个基于真实教学情境的问题，采用基于教育研究的评分标准；通过人机协同的LLM作为评判者流程实现自动化评估；选取11个不同规模（4B-120B参数）的语言模型进行测试，并分析模型家族、微调方式与性能的关系；进一步通过教育提示工程优化提示，评估改进效果。

Result: 模型在词汇、语气等表面指标表现良好，但在避免答案泄露、利用学生调试历史等深层教学行为上表现不足。模型家族与指令微调策略比参数量更能预测教学质量。经提示优化后，10个模型表现提升。结果表明，上下文相关的、以教学法为核心的基准对SLM在教育中的应用至关重要。

Conclusion: 开发面向特定教育场景、基于教学法的评估基准（如CSTutorBench）对于小语言模型在教育领域的有效选型与部署具有关键意义。提示工程可显著改善模型教学表现，未来应重视教学逻辑与上下文适配性设计。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly explored as AI tutors, yet deploying them in K-12 settings raises concerns around privacy, cost, and reliance on proprietary models. Small language models (SLMs) offer a promising alternative, but selecting the right model for a specific educational context remains difficult, particularly when the target domain, such as block-based programming, is largely absent from model training data. We introduce CSTutorBench, a benchmark for evaluating language models as CS tutors in VEX VR, a block-based robotics environment. The benchmark comprises 17 scenario-based questions scored against a pedagogical rubric grounded in established tutoring and feedback research, with a human-in-the-loop LLM-as-judge pipeline for evaluation. Preliminary findings across 11 models (4B-120B parameters) reveal that models perform well on surface-level criteria such as vocabulary and tone but struggle with deeper pedagogical behaviors, particularly avoiding answer leakage and engaging with student debugging histories. In our sample, model family and instruction-tuning approach appear to be better predictors of tutoring quality than parameter count alone, though the small number of models limits the strength of this conclusion. A targeted prompt revision grounded in recent educational prompt engineering research improved scores for 10 of 11 models. These results underscore the value of context-specific, pedagogically grounded benchmarks for SLM selection in educational deployment.

</details>


### [149] [Foundation Models for Automatic CAD Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05573)
*J de Curtò,Victoria Guillén,I. de Zarzà*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出LLMForge框架，通过多轮迭代优化实现从自然语言到参数化3D CAD设计的自动生成。采用统一评估流程与包含97个工程设计问题的基准测试集，对比七种基础模型在两种批判机制（IterTracer与IterVision）下的表现。结果表明，紧凑型指令微调模型可媲美大型系统；基于VLM的视觉语义批评在提升网格完整性方面更优，但在旋转对称结构上暴露语义与视觉评分差异。研究探讨了基准设计、失败模式及工业应用意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型和视觉语言模型已具备从自然语言生成参数化3D设计的能力，但缺乏统一评估体系与系统性分析，难以支撑工业级自动化机械设计。亟需构建可量化、可复现的评估框架以揭示模型能力边界与局限。

Method: 提出LLMForge多模态文本到CAD框架，集成JSON-schema验证、解析特征评分、网格合成与多轮迭代优化；设计两种批判机制：IterTracer使用基于Phong着色的光线追踪渲染与解析视觉指标（轮廓交并比、孔洞可见性、边缘间距、长宽比符合度）进行轻量反馈；IterVision引入Qwen2.5-VL-72B作为语义批判器，通过链式思维视觉推理评估空间一致性和设计意图。

Result: 在四种典型几何类型（带孔板、多特征盒体、法兰圆柱、L型支架）的基准测试中，高排名模型在IterTracer下形成紧密聚类（平均得分[0.885, 0.890]），网格成功率达98.97%；在IterVision下，最优模型实现100%密封网格生成，但旋转对称结构出现视觉与语义评分分歧，暴露系统性难题。

Conclusion: 紧凑型指令微调模型在参数化CAD生成中具备与大型模型相当的能力；基于VLM的语义批判能显著提升设计质量，尤其在复杂结构中发现隐性缺陷。研究为未来工业级自动化机械设计提供技术路径与评估标准。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision-Language Models (VLMs) enable the automatic generation of parametric 3D designs from natural-language specifications. This chapter presents an empirical study of foundation models for automatic Computer-Aided Design (CAD) generation of mechanical parts, using a unified evaluation pipeline and a curated benchmark of 97 engineering design problems. We introduce LLMForge, a multi-model text-to-CAD framework integrating JSON-schema validation, analytic feature scoring, mesh synthesis, and multi-round iterative refinement, studied under two critique regimes. IterTracer uses a Phong-shaded ray-trace renderer with analytic visual metrics (silhouette IoU, hole visibility, edge clearance, aspect-ratio conformance) for lightweight geometry-aware feedback across rounds. IterVision replaces the analytic scorer with a VLM semantic critic (Qwen2.5-VL-72B) that evaluates rendered views via chain-of-thought visual reasoning, assessing spatial coherence and design intent. On a benchmark spanning four canonical geometry families (plates with holes and bolt circles, multi-feature boxes, flanged cylinders, and L-brackets), we evaluate seven foundation models: DeepSeek-V3.2, Qwen3-235B-A22B, Llama-3.3-70B, Gemma-3-27B, GLM-4.5, MiniMax-M2.1, and INTELLECT. Under IterTracer, the four highest-ranked models form a tight cluster (overall mean in [0.885, 0.890]) with 98.97% mesh success, showing that compact instruction-tuned models can match substantially larger systems. VLM-based critique in IterVision yields 100% watertight mesh generation on the leading model while surfacing systematic difficulty on rotationally symmetric geometries such as cylinders, where visual and semantic scoring diverge most. We discuss benchmark design, failure modes, CAD-oriented prompting, and implications for industrial workflows and scalable automated mechanical design.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建基于叙事学的类型化时序状态图，并采用查询条件化的混合检索策略；通过固定阅读器和可复现数据集评估系统性能。

Abstract: Long-form fiction writers need memory that answers multi-hop questions about evolving story state: who knows a secret and when they learned it, whether an event preceded the narration that revealed it, whether a setup paid off, and how a relationship shifted. General-purpose retrieval and agent-memory systems represent entities and facts but not the narratological structure these questions turn on, so they surface the wrong evidence or none at all. We introduce the Narrative World Model (NWM), a writer-memory system that pairs a narratology-grounded typed temporal-state graph with query-conditioned hybrid retrieval. To measure memory rather than the answerer, we read every system through a single held-constant Opus 4.8 reader over only that system's chapter-safe evidence, on a reproducible public corpus and a validated multi-hop benchmark, and we compare against the strongest existing temporal-knowledge-graph agent-memory framework, Graphiti/Zep (Rasmussen et al., 2025). NWM substantially and significantly outperforms this baseline on multi-hop narratological QA across both corpora, and far exceeds GraphRAG and flat retrieval. The advantage is representational rather than an artifact of extraction: it survives rebuilding the baseline with NWM's own extractor, and traces to its narratology-grounded structure and query-conditioned retrieval, not to graph size or extractor quality.

### [151] [FirstResearch: Auditable Question Formation for LLM Scientific Discovery Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05682)
*Yufeng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FirstResearch提出一种基于第一性原理的研究问题生成框架，通过结构化的研究问题证书记录定义、假设、机制模型、矛盾点、可证伪假设、最小决定性实验和失败更新规则，提升LLM生成科学问题的可审计性。在10个研究主题上，该框架优于多个基线方法，在双盲评估中表现更优，且证书为核心关键组件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科学领域中的LLM系统虽能辅助研究构思、文献综述、实验设计和报告撰写，但其提出的首个研究问题往往难以审计，因缺乏对机制、可证伪性及假设的透明展示，限制了科学可信度。因此需要一种使研究问题可审查的方法。

Method: 提出名为FirstResearch的框架，核心为结构化研究问题证书，包含：原始定义、假设、机制模型、矛盾或张力、可证伪假设、最小决定性测试、失败更新规则。所有内容以形式化方式记录，确保研究问题的可追溯与可检验性。

Result: 在10个课题中，FirstResearch在DeepSeek盲评和Gemini独立评审中均显著优于多个基线（如AI co-scientist、Agent Laboratory、AI Scientist-v2），平均得分分别为4.86/5和4.38/5；移除证书后性能大幅下降，证明证书是核心贡献。

Conclusion: 显式推导约束是提升LLM生成科学问题可审计性的有效路径，尽管当前评估依赖于LLM评委而非人类专家，但结果支持其在特定范围内的科学发现潜力。代码与数据已公开。

Abstract: LLM systems for scientific discovery increasingly assist with ideation, literature synthesis, experiment planning, and report generation, but the first research question they propose can remain difficult to audit: it may sound plausible without exposing the mechanism, falsifier, or assumption that a scientist should inspect. We introduce FirstResearch, a first-principles research-question formation framework for scientific LLM agents whose core artifact is a structured Research Question Certificate. The certificate records primitive definitions, assumptions, a mechanism model, a tension or contradiction, a falsifiable hypothesis, a minimal decisive test, and a failure update rule, making the proposed question inspectable before downstream execution. On ten LLM-agent research topics, FirstResearch outperforms controlled prompt-level baselines inspired by AI co-scientist, Agent Laboratory, and AI Scientist-v2 under a primary DeepSeek-blind-judge protocol. A Gemini-2.5-Flash independent-judge rescore of the same 40 baseline packages preserves the system-level ranking, with FirstResearch scoring 4.86/5 versus 4.38/5 for the strongest baseline and Pearson agreement of 0.865 on average score. A one-repeat ablation checkpoint further suggests that the certificate-centered core is the strongest component: certificate-only scoring reaches 4.90/5 under DeepSeek and 4.88/5 under Gemini, while removing certificates drops below 1/5 under both judges. These results are preliminary and use LLM judges rather than human domain experts, but they support a narrow scientific-discovery claim: explicit derivation constraints are a promising mechanism for making LLM-generated scientific questions more auditable. Code, prompts, saved outputs, and reproduction scripts are available at https://github.com/louiswang524/FirstResearch.

### [152] [Memory in the Loop: In-Process Retrieval as ExtendedWorking Memory for Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05690)
*Yusuf Khan,Carlo Lipizzi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究语言智能体在推理循环中将记忆操作（读写）内置于每一步的可行性，突破传统仅每轮查询一次记忆的限制。核心挑战是延迟：网络存储响应慢（数十至数百毫秒），导致端到端延迟飙升。作者提出，延迟本质源于存储位置而非访问模式；当使用进程内存储（~100μs响应）时，每步开销可忽略，使记忆成为‘扩展工作记忆’。实验表明，在固定每轮延迟预算下，延迟越高，冗余动作越多（110ms时达7.2/12，而进程内为0.0/12，p=0.0079）。四款GPT-5级模型验证了该机制：在有限窗口内，记忆召回从0/5提升至3.6–4.8/5，且所有写入均成功（244/244），未失败源于代理读取策略。进一步测量发现，嵌入计算是主要瓶颈（200–400ms），结合本地小嵌入器后，整体延迟降至~40μs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统语言智能体的记忆系统位于推理循环之外，仅每轮查询一次，限制了动态记忆交互。尽管已有工作通过调度或限制检索频率缓解延迟问题，但未从根本上质疑其根源。本文旨在重新审视延迟的本质：是否真正由‘循环内访问’引起？若存储足够快，是否可实现真正的持续记忆交互？

Method: 设计并实现一个内置于推理循环中的进程内记忆系统，对比不同存储延迟下的行为表现。通过控制每轮记忆延迟预算，测试在不同响应速度（100μs vs 110ms）下，智能体产生的冗余动作数量，并评估记忆召回率。同时引入本地嵌入器以降低网络延迟影响，实现端到端低延迟运行。

Result: 在进程内存储（~100μs）条件下，智能体冗余动作显著减少（0.0/12），记忆召回率从0/5提升至3.6–4.8/5；所有写入均成功，无存储失效；嵌入计算为最大延迟来源，结合本地嵌入器后整体延迟降至~40μs。结果证明，快速存储可使记忆成为持续可用的扩展工作记忆。

Conclusion: 记忆的延迟并非来自‘循环内访问’模式本身，而是存储部署位置造成的。当存储响应快至微秒级，记忆可被无缝集成进每一步推理，形成真正意义上的扩展工作记忆。这不仅提升了记忆利用效率，也重新定义了智能体与外部记忆的关系——从工具式调用转向内在化协同。

Abstract: Language agents run a loop - observe, reason, act - but the memory they reason over sits outside it: a store queried at most once per turn. We study the regime where memory moves inside the loop, read and written on every step. The obstacle has always been latency: networked stores answer in tens to hundreds of milliseconds, and in-loop retrieval can inflate end-to-end latency by up to 83x when retrieval is expensive. Prior work manages that cost rather than questioning it: serving-layer scheduling hides it, "memory-first" designs ration retrieval to once per turn. We argue latency is a property of where the store lives, not the in-loop pattern: an in-process store answers in ~100us, three orders of magnitude below the network regime, and at that speed the per-step tax collapses. By the extended-mind thesis's parity principle, a store fast enough to be constantly and directly available becomes extended working memory, not a tool the agent merely consults. The premise is causal: holding a fixed per-turn memory-latency budget and varying only the store's answer speed, redundant actions rise monotonically with latency - 0.0 of 12 at in-process speed, 7.2 of 12 at a 110ms cloud round trip (gpt-5-nano, gpt-5-mini; exact permutation p=0.0079). We demonstrate the regime end-to-end: across four GPT-5-class models under a bounded window, recall improves from 0/5 to 3.6-4.8/5 with in-loop memory, store ops at p50 80-165us - though an instructed restate-every-reply baseline also solves it perfectly, at a token cost that grows with the working set. The store never lost a fact in any run (244 of 244 writes kept); every miss traces to the agent's read policy, not the store. Our measurements also relocate the bottleneck: the dominant per-step cost is embedding (~200-400ms over the network); pairing the in-process store with a small local embedder returns the complete operation to a measured ~40us.

</details>


### [153] [Akashic: A Low-Overhead LLM Inference Service with MemAttention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05708)
*Yang Liu,Zhaokai Luo,Huayi Jin,Ruozhou He,Chenchen Hong,Zhiyong Wang,Yifei Liu,Yunfei Gu,Chentao Wu,Junhao Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Akashic 是一种基于 MemAttention 的低开销记忆系统，通过将上下文划分为有界块并建模块间语义关系，有效保留跨块证据，避免重复写入完整历史。结合软硬件协同设计的内存放置策略，减少检索碎片化和 I/O 开销。在四个工作负载和三种模型规模下，相比现有基线，任务准确率提升最高达 10.2 点，吞吐量提升最高 1.21 倍，可持续请求率提升最高 1.88 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统 LLM 代理系统在多轮交互中持续积累上下文，导致历史过长，引发预填充开销大、超出上下文长度限制、关键信息被无关内容淹没等问题，影响服务效率与输出质量。需要一种高效、可扩展的记忆机制来管理长期上下文。

Method: 提出 Akashic 系统，核心为 MemAttention，将上下文组织为有界块，并建模块间的语义关联；采用硬件-软件协同设计的内存放置策略，将可能同时被检索的块物理邻近存放，降低检索碎片化与 I/O 延迟。

Result: 在四种代表性工作负载和三种模型规模下，Akashic 相比强基线，任务准确率最高提升 10.2 点，吞吐量最高提升 1.21 倍，可持续请求率最高提升 1.88 倍。

Conclusion: Akashic 有效解决了长期上下文管理中的效率与质量瓶颈，通过智能分块、语义建模与内存优化，在保持高准确率的同时显著提升系统吞吐与可扩展性，是面向大规模 LLM 代理系统的实用记忆架构。

Abstract: Recent LLM-based agent systems continuously accumulate context across multi-turn interactions, tool invocations, and cross-session workflows. Replaying the full history for every request quickly becomes impractical: long contexts increase prefill cost, may exceed context limits, and often bury task-relevant evidence in irrelevant content, degrading both serving efficiency and output quality. We propose Akashic, a low-overhead memory system built around MemAttention, which organizes context into bounded chunks and models semantic relationships across chunks, preserving cross-chunk evidence without repeatedly rewriting the full history. Akashic further applies hardware-software co-designed memory placement to co-locate likely co-retrieved chunks, reducing retrieval fragmentation and I/O overhead. Across four representative workloads and three model sizes, Akashic improves task accuracy by up to 10.2 points, throughput by up to 1.21x, and sustainable request rate by up to 1.88x over strong prior memory baselines.

</details>


### [154] [ArtisanCAD: An Industrial-Level CAD Agent with Expert-Grounded Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05750)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CAD-IR作为可执行的程序化表示，用于编码参数、操作顺序、工具绑定、依赖关系和验证规则；通过专家操作记录进行知识蒸馏，构建可复用的参数化技能；利用检索与修订机制生成初始CAD-IR，经由CATIA-MCP后端执行并结合多视角视觉反馈进行迭代优化，最终生成生产级B-Rep模型。

Result: 在Text2CAD基准上，使用CAD-IR将中间级别提示的平均Chamfer Distance从14.83降低至9.88，显著提升生成精度；在四个复杂汽车部件上成功将专家CATIA操作记录转化为可复用技能，实现了新变体请求下的可编辑CATIA原生B-Rep模型生成。

Conclusion: \algname通过引入专家引导的知识蒸馏与可执行的CAD-IR表示，有效弥合了自然语言描述与可执行工业建模之间的鸿沟，具备生成高质量、可编辑、生产级CAD模型的能力，为工业级智能设计提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Computer-aided design (CAD) for industrial components requires long-horizon procedural modeling, robust feature dependencies, editable parametric geometry, and production-grade B-Rep execution. Existing text-to-CAD methods have made promising progress in generating CAD programs from natural-language descriptions, but they still struggle when user prompts are ambiguous, underspecified, or only describe high-level design intent. They also rarely exploit expert procedural knowledge naturally available in industrial workflows, such as CATIA operation recordings, macro logs, drawing notes, and engineering descriptions. We present \algname, a skill-guided industrial CAD agent with expert-grounded knowledge distillation. The core of \algname is CAD intermediate representation (CAD-IR), an executable procedural representation that encodes parameters, ordered operations, MCP tool bindings, dependencies, generated entities, and verification rules. CAD-IR plays two key roles: it first serves as the carrier for distilling expert CAD procedures into reusable parameterized skills; then it provides a procedural scaffold that turns vague or intermediate-level prompts into complete executable CAD operations. \algname retrieves expert-derived skills, instantiates and revises CAD-IR, executes the resulting procedure through a dedicated CATIA-MCP backend, and uses multi-view visual feedback for iterative refinement, and finally generates production-ready B-Rep models. On the Text2CAD benchmark, CAD-IR improves generation from intermediate prompts by reducing mean Chamfer Distance from $14.83$ to $9.88$, showing its ability to bridge ambiguous textual intent and executable CAD construction. On four complex automotive components, CAD-IR enables expert CATIA recordings to be distilled into reusable skills, allowing \algname to generate editable CATIA-native B-Rep models for new variant requests.

Across the literature, we find that failures compound nonlinearly with task length, that strong performance on individual sub-tasks does not reliably translate into end-to-end success, and that additional scaffolding does not consistently improve reliability. At the same time, substantial progress has been demonstrated in single-turn tool use, short-horizon web navigation, and narrowly scoped coding tasks.

### [158] [Controlling Tool Use with Heading-Specific Activation Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05790)
*Yuqi Chen,Vincent Siu,Yang Liu,Dawn Song,Chenguang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究工具增强型大语言模型在推理时对工具调用的决策机制，发现可通过从头部锚点位置提取的引导向量实现对工具使用行为的双向因果控制。该方法在五个开源模型和三个领域中有效抑制了不必要的工具调用，尤其在仅需参数化推理的领域效果最佳。然而几何分析显示，工具调用步骤与抑制向量之间呈现弥散、双峰对齐而非线性一致，且不同工具类型具有高度分离的内部表征，特征重叠低。这表明工具的非参数特性可能解释了这种几何不规则性，并区别于参数化概念的引导向量。尽管如此，这种几何不规则性与实际因果有效性之间的关系仍待探究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究工具调用决策是否存在可提取和操纵的稳定内部表征，以解决大语言模型在无须调用工具时仍频繁调用的问题。

Method: 从头部锚点位置提取引导向量，并通过其对工具调用行为进行干预，结合几何分析验证其在多模型、多领域中的因果控制能力。

Result: 引导向量能有效抑制不必要的工具调用，尤其在参数化推理即可完成的任务中；但工具调用行为与抑制向量的对齐呈现非线性、弥散、双峰分布，且不同工具类型的内部表征差异大，特征重叠低。

Conclusion: 工具调用的内部表征具有非参数特性，导致其几何结构不规则，这可能解释了为何引导向量虽具因果效力却不符合线性编码预期。该现象揭示了工具使用机制与参数化认知的根本差异，相关机制仍有待深入研究。

Abstract: Tool-augmented large language models extend their capabilities beyond parametric knowledge through external tools, but tend to invoke them unnecessarily. We investigate whether tool-use decisions have any stable internal representation that can be extracted and manipulated, a question that is non-trivial given that tools exist entirely in context at inference time and have no direct encoding in model weights. We show that steering vectors extracted from heading-anchors positions exert bidirectional causal control over tool-invocation behavior across five open-source models and three domains, suppressing unnecessary tool use most effectively in domains where parametric reasoning suffices. However, geometric analysis reveals that this causal effectiveness does not correspond to clean linear structure: tool-invocation steps exhibit diffuse, bimodal alignment with the suppression vector rather than the consistent negative alignment a linear encoding account would predict, and different tool types recruit largely distinct internal signatures with low cross-tool feature overlap. We hypothesize these geometric properties are indicative of the non-parametric nature of tools, and distinguish tool-use steering vectors from those extracted for parametrically grounded concepts. The relationship between this geometric irregularity and the observed causal effectiveness remains an open question.

NapMem organizes user history into a linked multi-granularity memory pyramid, where raw conversations, typed memory records, topic tracks, and user profiles are connected through provenance relations, and exposes these levels through memory tools. The agent is trained to select memory according to the query and intermediate evidence, allowing it to inspect different memory granularities before answering. Experiments on PersonaMem-v2, LongMemEval, and LoCoMo show that a NapMem agent trained with memory-tool reinforcement learning is competitive across diverse memory-intensive tasks, while evaluations on non-memory tasks suggest that the learned policy largely preserves general reasoning and tool-use abilities. ### [160] [TurnOPD: Making On-Policy Distillation Turn-Aware for Efficient Long-Horizon Agent Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05804)
*Yuhang Zhou,Kai Zheng,Haoling Li,Dengyun Peng,Can Xu,Jingjing Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出TurnOPD，一种针对长时序智能体的高效在线策略蒸馏方法，通过两阶段预算控制（自适应回放深度与渐进式归一化损失）解决传统OPD在长任务中的效率与训练不平衡问题，显著提升验证准确率并优化训练时间-精度权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线策略蒸馏（OPD）在长时序智能体任务中存在两个核心问题：全周期回放浪费计算资源于低效尾部动作，且轨迹级KL损失集中于浅层token，导致深层决策训练不足。

Method: 提出TurnOPD，包含两个预算控制器：1）基于探针的自适应回放深度预算，根据回合统计动态确定回放长度；2）渐进式归一化损失预算，逐步将KL权重从词元级转向回合均衡监督。

Result: 在ALFWorld、WebShop和多跳搜索任务上，使用专用教师模型的实验表明，TurnOPD在相同训练时长下达到更高验证准确率，并突破了传统OPD的精度-时间边界。

Conclusion: TurnOPD通过精细化的回合级预算机制，有效提升了长时序语言智能体训练的效率与质量，为在线蒸馏在复杂任务中的应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student policy by matching a stronger teacher on the student's own trajectories, offering a promising framework for language agent training. However, its application to long-horizon agentic tasks remains insufficiently explored. We identify two key inefficiencies in vanilla agent OPD: (1) full-horizon rollouts often waste wall-clock resources on tail turns that provide weak and noisy KL supervision, and (2) trajectory-level KL objectives concentrate most of the loss on shallow tokens, leaving deeper decision turns under-trained once initial behaviors are aligned. To address these challenges, we propose TurnOPD, a turn-level budgeting strategy for efficient on-policy distillation of long-horizon agents. TurnOPD consists of two budget controllers: adaptive rollout-depth budgeting, which uses probe-based turn statistics to determine rollout length, and progressive turn-normalized loss budgeting, which gradually shifts KL weighting from token-level to turn-balanced supervision. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Multi-Hop Search with task-specialized teacher models show that TurnOPD achieves superior validation accuracy under equal wall-clock training budgets and advances the accuracy--time frontier beyond vanilla OPD.

### [161] [Onnes: A Physics-Grounded Multi-Agent LLM Simulator for Cryogenic Fault Diagnosis in Quantum Computing Infrastructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05805)
*Praneeth Narisetty,Uday Kumar Reddy Kattamanchi,Shiva Nagendra Babu Kore*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Onnes，一个基于物理的数字孪生模拟器，用于稀释制冷机故障诊断。该系统结合真实制冷机数据、从BlueFors日志中学习的噪声与相关性指纹，以及六个基于物理的故障类别，通过零样本LLM代理面板与监督式机器学习分类器进行对比测试。在1000轮评估中，零样本代理在检测上表现相当，但在分类上落后，主要错误集中于易混淆故障。通过精心设计的对比少样本示范和自洽投票机制，分类准确率从0.685提升至0.990，接近监督模型（0.985），仅需六条标注示例且无需参数更新。消融实验表明性能提升几乎完全归因于示范。系统作为持续监控工具，在九次故障注入实验中实现100%召回率，且通过置信度门控有效抑制前兆误报。此外，仅使用真实蓝福斯遥测数据训练的检测器在真实硬件上实现了6.4%误报率和100%召回率，验证了其有效性。所有结果均来自公开运行日志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前稀释制冷机的故障诊断依赖阈值报警，仅提示异常发生而无法定位具体问题。为提升诊断精度与可解释性，亟需一种能融合物理规律与真实数据的智能诊断方法。

Method: 构建基于物理的数字孪生模拟器Onnes，整合真实制冷机运行数据、学习到的噪声与相关性指纹，定义六类物理驱动故障；采用零样本多代理LLM系统与监督学习分类器对比，并引入少样本示范与自洽投票机制优化分类性能；系统作为实时监控器部署于真实硬件环境。

Result: 零样本代理经少样本示范与自洽投票后，分类准确率达0.990，媲美监督分类器（0.985）；在真实硬件上实现6.4%误报率与100%召回率；系统可在单个轮询周期内捕捉所有故障发展，置信度门控有效降低误报。

Conclusion: Onnes数字孪生系统结合物理建模与数据驱动，显著提升了稀释制冷机故障诊断的准确性与可靠性。少样本示范与自洽推理机制使零样本代理达到接近监督模型的性能，具备实际部署潜力，为量子计算基础设施的智能化运维提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Dilution refrigerators are the enabling infrastructure of superconducting quantum computers, yet their fault diagnosis is still dominated by threshold alarms that report that something is wrong, not what. We present Onnes, a physics-grounded digital-twin simulator of a dilution refrigerator (a forward physics model with a learned real-fridge noise fingerprint) that drives a live multi-agent LLM operations layer, and use it for a controlled head-to-head between a zero-shot LLM agent panel and a supervised ML classifier on cryogenic fault diagnosis. The twin couples a real dilution-cooling floor, a noise-and-correlation fingerprint learned from real BlueFors logs, and six physics-grounded fault classes, three engineered to overlap on temperature but separate on flow and pressure. Across a 1000-turn evaluation the zero-shot panel shows no significant difference from the classifier on detection but trails on classification, its errors concentrating on the confusable faults. Curated contrastive few-shot demonstrations and self-consistency voting then raise classification accuracy from 0.685 to 0.990, matching the supervised classifier (0.985) with no parameter updates and six labeled demonstrations; an ablation attributes the gain almost entirely to the demonstrations. Run as a continuous monitor across a nine-run fault-by-seed sweep, the agent catches every developing fault within one poll interval, and a confidence gate suppresses pre-onset false alarms whose rate is backend-dependent. As a first sim-to-real check, a detector trained purely on real BlueFors telemetry posts a real-hardware false-alarm rate of 6.4% and 100% recall on physics faults injected onto real held-out windows. All numbers are drawn verbatim from released run logs.

</details>


### [162] [StateFuse: Deterministic Conflict-Preserving Memory for Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05844)
*Sergey Volkov,Yang Li,Ye Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: StateFuse 是一种基于标准 OpSet/CRDT 合并的冲突感知复制内存协议，通过不可变历史、显式冲突对象、精确语义修正标识（claim_id / claim_ref）、确定性谓词合约和投影时解析机制，保留冲突可见性而不修改已复制状态。在 MemoryAgentBench 测试中，各方法准确率相当，但保留冲突的方法能持续暴露矛盾，支持更安全的放弃与修正；消融实验表明，在缺乏精确前序标识时，语义修正句柄至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有内存层在处理多分支、重试和副本中的冲突观察时，常采用难以检查或修正的覆盖规则，导致冲突被掩盖。需要一种能显式保留并可审计冲突的内存机制，以提升系统安全性与可追溯性。

Method: StateFuse 基于标准 OpSet/CRDT 合并，引入代理感知语义层：包含不可变历史、显式冲突对象、精确的修正标识（claim_id / claim_ref）、确定性谓词合约，以及在投影阶段进行的非重写式冲突解析。

Result: 在 282 道含冲突的 MemoryAgentBench 测试中，各方法准确率相近，但保留冲突的方法持续暴露矛盾，而折叠式方法隐藏了冲突。在统一验证的代理循环中，保持模糊性有助于更安全的放弃与修正。消融实验显示，当无法获取精确前序标识时，语义修正句柄具有关键作用。

Conclusion: StateFuse 最适合作为公开记忆契约，用于暴露矛盾、支持安全放弃与可审计修正，而非普遍提升准确率。

Abstract: Agent systems accumulate conflicting observations across branches, retries, and replicas, yet many practical memory layers still collapse disagreement behind overwrite rules that are difficult to inspect or correct. We present StateFuse, a conflict-aware replicated memory contract built on standard OpSet/CRDT merge. StateFuse does not introduce a new join algebra; it defines an agent-facing semantics layer with immutable history, explicit conflict objects, exact and semantic correction handles (claim_id / claim_ref), deterministic predicate contracts, and projection-time resolution that cannot rewrite replicated state.
  We evaluate StateFuse against flat multi-value, raw-log, provenance-style, and collapsed baselines under matched resolver and verification policies. On a 282-question official conflict-bearing MemoryAgentBench slice, the compared methods tie on answer accuracy, but conflict-preserving surfaces keep contradictions visible while collapsed surfaces do not. In a controlled agent loop with uniform verification, preserving ambiguity enables safer abstention and correction than early collapse. A correction-handle ablation further shows that semantic handles matter when exact prior identifiers are unavailable.
  The resulting claim is narrow: StateFuse is best supported as a safer public memory contract for contradiction surfacing, abstention, and auditable correction, not as a universal accuracy gain.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动抑郁检测在音频-视觉数据中面临特征分布重叠和决策边界不稳健的挑战，亟需更有效的多模态融合方法以提升检测精度。

Method: 提出基于时序编码器与互变压器的细粒度多模态框架，引入二元优势加权排序损失，通过计算成对预测差异矩阵并动态加权困难样本，同时最小化类内方差，使特征向类中心聚集。

Result: 在D-vlog和LMVD数据集上的实验表明，该模型能有效重构潜在序结构，优先关注困难样本，显著提升抑郁检测性能，达到当前最佳水平。

Conclusion: 所提方法通过优化潜在空间分布，有效解决了多模态抑郁检测中的特征重叠与边界模糊问题，具备更强的泛化能力与判别性能，为自动抑郁检测提供了新思路。

Abstract: Automatic depression detection using audio-visual data faces significant challenges, particularly in disentangling overlapping feature distributions and establishing robust decision boundaries. To address this, we propose a fine-grained multimodal framework featuring a temporal encoder and a mutual transformer to facilitate deep cross-modal fusion. Our core contribution is the Binary Advantage-weighting Ranking Loss, which optimizes the latent space distribution through two complementary mechanisms: Advantage-weighted Separation, which mines hard pairs by computing a pairwise prediction difference matrix and dynamically weighting them based on their difficulty; and Advantage-weighted Compactness, which minimizes intra-class variance to force features to cluster around their respective class centers. Extensive experiments on D-vlog and LMVD demonstrate that our model reconstructs the latent ordinal structure by prioritizing hard pairs, thereby achieving state-of-the-art performance.

### [164] [PCBWorld: A Benchmark Environment for Engine-Grounded PCB Design Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05915)

  <summary>Details</summary>
